1)  
Let Us Become Those Who Know It Is a Gift  
Genesis 1:24-31  
<Prayer> We cannot help but worry whether our being can truly be offered before the Father, and as we look into ourselves, we cannot help but bow our heads with a shameful heart, wondering if we are in a state to receive the gifts granted by the Father.  
Until now, we have known that the Father has never forsaken anyone who can measure their own path, and that the Father does not abandon any individual or nation that struggles to live with repentance even in a place of sorrow.  
Father, although our hearts and bodies may be far from You, we know that You desire to dwell in our hearts. We understand that the Father's heart longs for the day when He can directly govern our bodies, and that He has been a historical Father, a timely Father, and a Father who cannot abandon us in the future, having a creative connection with us.  
We find ourselves in such a position, and we must face the Father who must deal with us in that way. This connection cannot be severed by anything, and we know that even in sorrow, pain, or anger, the Father has embraced these and has walked the historical path with them. We earnestly hope and desire that the Father will once again show us mercy at this time.  
Who among us dares to stand before the Father? Who can say they can stand before the Father? On October 25, 1959, at the former headquarters church.  
Let Us Become Those Who Know It Is a Gift  
Who can be confident? The more we know, the more we feel the piercing sorrow of Heaven. We cannot dare to lift our faces, nor can we know where to place our bodies in the presence of the awe-inspiring image of the Father and His heart, and we are grateful that we have been allowed to recognize such truths.  
We have come to know through teaching and learning. Who has allowed us to know this? It was not because we were capable, nor was it because we were equipped to do so. We have come to understand that the countless ancestors who admired goodness throughout history have connected us with Heaven without our knowledge.  
Let us be allowed to know that we are not just ourselves today, and let us be people who respect that connection, enjoy it, and not become those who betray it. Let us be those who immerse ourselves in that connection, sing of it in our hearts, and glorify the Father before Him.  
Father, what position is our heart in? What is our body waiting for, and by what are we moving, and where do we wish to be? Let us think about this ourselves. In the quietness, let us feel in our hearts that the Father is urging us to recognize the value of life even at this moment, and let us understand that the Father can only look upon humanity with sorrow due to the tragic events of people who struggle only to hold onto their own lives.  
Father, who governs our hearts and the world of our minds, please come personally and govern us all fundamentally at this time. Let us be those who rejoice in goodness and become people who can harmonize with the Father in heart and body, and we earnestly hope and desire that You grant us new words.  
Now, I wish to express the Father's words, but what should I say? Although many words have already been spoken, when we come to understand that we have a mission to find the value of those words through our hearts and bodies at this moment, we find ourselves utterly lacking. However, we know that we are those who must be revived, and even if the same words are spoken, we must receive the admonition once again. We, who must receive the words of life to not be cut off from the Father, have bowed down before Him with shameless and insufficient hearts, so please allow our desire to convey and our desire to receive to become one.  
Where is the capable person, and where is the incapable person? We know that through heart, we are one, so allow us to resonate with the heart of Heaven, to feel it, and to respond to it. Thus, may only the glory of the Father appear before the life of us all, and may the gift of the Father's life deeply permeate our hearts. Move our hearts and minds so that this time may be one that opens up the eternal path of life and allows a new resolve and determination to explode from within our hearts to resolve the sorrow of restoration.  
At this time, we believe that the lonely members scattered throughout South Korea are earnestly praying for the nation, so may the Father be their friend and become the subject of grace before them. Please govern them personally, and if tears are to be shed, let them be shed on behalf of the Father, and if there are sorrowful matters, let them first think of the Father's sorrow, and if there is labor to be done, let them labor on behalf of the Father to establish a new foundation of blood and flesh before this nation, and may this time be one of blessings where we can encounter the gifts of Heaven.  
At this time, please grant the authority of life to all beings who bow their heads, and may the countless sons and daughters in Heaven unite with us to cooperate in establishing a victorious foundation of glory. I earnestly request this as I offer all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen.  
<Words> The title I wish to think about today is  
Let Us Become Those Who Know It Is a Gift.  
10  
Let Us Become Those Who Know It Is a Gift.  
Humans Cannot Escape the Realm of Connection  
You regard yourselves as very important. You live with yourself at the center, always wishing that the entire world revolves around you. It is undeniable that we desire to be in the foremost position. If we are that precious, we are beyond measure precious. Therefore, Jesus expressed that he knew the precious value of human beings and that he could not exchange himself for the world. God also said that when we possess infinite value, He would make our individual selves into His temple.  
What is the purpose of our struggles and faith in our life journey today? We cannot deny that our existence is driven by the purpose of connecting our individual selves to the value of the whole. When we look at ourselves, we see Heaven above and the earth below. To the left and right, we have the world we live in, our families, and our tribes, and in front and behind, we have our ancestors and descendants. When we look at these dimensions, we must feel that we cannot escape from the realm of connection. Yet, we must feel this once again at this time.  
Whether we look up or down, forward or backward, or to the left or right, everything is connected to us. Moreover, this connection is not temporary; it is a lifelong journey of connection that carries life. In fact, it is a connection that has existed since the beginning of history and must continue through our present selves to our descendants for thousands of generations.  
When I break, the connection with Heaven centered on me will break, the connection with the earth will break, and all connections with the world, tribe, and family will break. This is why people say that humans are a microcosm representing Heaven and earth.  
My heart wishes to embrace Heaven. My body desires to occupy the earth. I also want to move by the heart of the sovereign, the representative, which cannot be blocked by anything in Heaven and earth. When we deeply analyze ourselves with such connections, we will realize that we are infinitely valuable beings, infinitely great beings.  
So why were we born? We were not born without purpose. Even a spoonful of rice you eat without thinking in the morning is not consumed without purpose. The way I live my day and act is also driven by a significant purpose when viewed from such a serious perspective.  
Even when looking at my individual self, there is Heaven above, the earth below, and all matters of the world. Can we say that all of these operate without any purpose or ideology? We must recognize that all these movements are a negotiation concerning our human existence. You are in a position to be representative offerings that can negotiate in front of Heaven and earth. If you fulfill your responsibilities as offerings, Heaven and earth will open the way to enter the realm of goodness, but if you fail to fulfill those responsibilities, you will inevitably stand in the position of a traitor before Heaven and earth.  
Those who felt this heart and acted responsibly are undoubtedly historical figures.  
Humans Sent as Gifts from Heaven  
You have been sent to this earth. You were born through the blood of your parents. You must understand that you, as an individual, are a most noble gift sent to this earth to be established as a victorious figure supported by Heaven and earth. Whether you represent a tribe, a nation, or any other aspect from a universal perspective, you must realize that you are the one sent as a gift from Heaven.  
Nothing that starts from my body, my mind, my thoughts, or my heart belongs to me. When you delve into your individual self, you will find your ancestors connected, and when you delve into this connection, you will uncover the entire history of humanity up to today. When you realize that you are in a position that is being led by this connection, you must not take yourself lightly.  
While I may seem like my own, I am not entirely mine. Before this nation, I am a gift sent for the nation; before my family, I am a gift sent for the family; in the context of a couple, I am a gift sent for the partner; and in relation to Heaven and earth, the entire world, I am a gift sent for each of them.  
You must understand this.  
Look at yourself as an individual. People say that the heart symbolizes Heaven and the body symbolizes the earth. Then, what will Heaven and earth, this universe, revolve around? It is ideology. That ideology is the perspective of living. This perspective of living must not be centered on myself; it must be centered on Heaven and earth. In other words, it must be a life centered on Heaven and earth.  
You must understand that my original individual self was created to represent Heaven and earth. I walk meaninglessly and move meaninglessly, but the entire Heaven and earth has been mobilized to create me.  
We have three parents. The first is this earth, which gives birth to and nurtures our bodies. Therefore, the nation, the world, all point toward the earth. Next, there are the parents who gave birth to my physical body. Lastly, there are the parents of my heart, my heart's parents. You must understand that humans should not forget these three parents. My body symbolizes the earth, and my heart symbolizes Heaven; thus, how should these two be? They must eternally unite and embrace each other. The heart is the subject, and the body is the object; Heaven is the subject, and the earth is the object. Therefore, Heaven and earth must embrace and harmonize with each other according to the principle of creation.  
If there is a Creator who created Heaven and earth, why did He create all things? It was not to leave them alone and merely observe. He created the universe to establish a world where all things can interact eternally, to give and receive, and to harmonize eternally. We must understand this.  
Then, we need to think about where the one form that the body and heart, shaped by Heaven and earth, can eternally embrace and enjoy is. No matter how smart or powerful someone may boast to be, if their body and heart are in conflict, they cannot be considered someone who has respected the divine gift endowed by the principle of creation.  
That is why Jesus said, "The Father is in me, and I am in the Father, and I am in you, and you are in me." What can be the center of this? Can it be centered on the body? No. Can it be centered on ideology? No. It must be centered on the world of our hearts and emotions.  
Jesus also said, "The kingdom of Heaven is within your heart." Our heart's world sings of infinite connections, and our emotions are filled with infinite sweetness and...
We are now able to boast of our fulfillment. For this reason, we are precious gifts sent on behalf of heaven and earth today. Have you ever thought of yourself as a precious gift? Have you considered the gift that you are? 

Any religion, ideology, or doctrine is fine, but we must understand what the purpose is. Have you thought about the value of yourself, sent as a gift on behalf of heaven and earth? Have you considered that you were sent to become a form that heaven delights in and that earth welcomes, and that you are struggling to become such a form? 

Our hearts command us to follow our true nature, while our bodies command us to struggle against this world. The heart and body, moving in these two conflicting directions, must unite at the historical final stage, but if there is nothing that can bring about this unity, then religion, creator, or any ideal becomes useless. In this light, we, who have been sent as gifts upon this earth, must recognize that we are gifts. 

If words are precious, then they are infinitely precious. Therefore, those who disregard this gifted self cannot stand before the laws of heaven. Humans are meant to harmonize with heaven and earth. Human ethics are meant to harmonize with heavenly ethics. The subject must harmonize with the object, or the subject must harmonize with the object. Since the object is in the position of the subject, it has a direction towards the subject. For this reason, we try to live centered around our conscience, even if we do not know why. There is not a single person who tries to live outside the commands of their conscience. 

Heavenly ethics and human ethics are not separate. When my heart and body harmonize and move, heavenly ethics and human ethics can harmonize and achieve unity. But why are there human ethics and heavenly ethics? It is because humans do not follow heavenly ethics. Thus, the reality of the lives of fallen humanity is that they struggle to live according to heavenly ethics once again. 

The purpose for which we were sent as gifts upon this earth 
You have been sent as a gift upon this earth by chance. So what is the purpose of sending you as an individual gift upon this earth? What is the purpose of establishing individuals? What do you want to achieve by establishing individuals? It is to embrace a partner and form a couple. Then what is the purpose of forming couples? It is to embrace children. That is the family. What is the purpose of establishing families? It is to embrace tribes. What is the purpose of establishing tribes? It is to embrace clans, nations, and further, to embrace the world. What is the purpose of establishing nations? It is to embrace the world. What is the purpose of establishing the world? Here lies the history of today. 

Humans have been sent as gifts upon this earth, and that gift must not stop at the individual. Although the body is one, the world of the heart and the world of feelings desire to embrace and sing of the infinite universe. If there is a creator, how will they govern us? They govern through the world of feelings and the world of ideals. There, they call out to us, come, come, come. This is a call that comes through conscience. Conscience is an action of a power that cannot be understood. 

Individuals must regard individuals as precious. A person who can value individuals must also be able to value families. We must not stop at valuing families. The primitive era was an era of family units. However, the era of family units has passed. We must move beyond it. Why? Because we humans have the responsibility to complete the position of being a universal gift by embracing the universe and to sing of the value of the relationships that have been gifted to us. For this reason, history progresses. The time of loving only within one's own circle and loving only one's own family has passed, and we must move beyond families to clans, beyond clans to tribes, and beyond tribes to nations. It does not stop at nations. Next, we must establish a nation, but it cannot stop at just that nation. We must move beyond nations to the world. Now what remains? The purpose for which we were sent upon this earth is undoubtedly to hope that our hearts and bodies can embrace the world and harmonize with it. 

In the Bible, it is said that heaven created Adam and Eve and blessed them. Adam had Eve, and Eve had Adam. They were a precious gift from heaven, becoming one while being two. Thus, heaven blessed them to become one and govern all creation. Eve symbolizes the body and the earth, while Adam symbolizes the heart and heaven, encompassing the whole. So how should these two become? They must become one, one. This is the principle of heaven and earth. 

The body is two but is one, a unity. What were they commanded to do as one? They were commanded to govern the universe. What is the purpose of this governance? It is to establish a relationship with all things. Since the creator is not the creator of individuals but of the entire universe, He granted humanity the authority to govern all things to establish a relationship with the entire universe. 

For this reason, human history flows toward a standard where humanity can govern the entire world. Just as the heart and body harmonize, this world is turning toward a world where it can harmonize with the heart and body. 

What should we embrace? 
We can say that the time is now at its end. This is being said unanimously. A time has come when it is difficult to solve the issues of the world with any global denomination or ideology. The claims presented to humanity up until today cannot encompass our world of hearts or provide rest for our world of feelings. Philosophy, religion, and science have all entered a stage where they must surrender. 

What is the issue we must understand here? It is what this world must embrace. What must it embrace? It must embrace the infinite beyond the world of hearts and beyond heaven. We must feel that embracing something greater than what this world holds and singing of its value is more precious than anything on this earth. Only then can we govern this world. 

Individuals were established to embrace families, families were established to embrace societies, societies were established to embrace nations, and nations were established to embrace the world. In the past, there were many doctrines and claims, but they became global doctrines for the world. If someone steps forward with a doctrine, they can extend that doctrine to the world by establishing a foundation that can embrace the world. In doing so, the notions of clans will all break apart. The notions of nations will also break apart. This is because the ideology of creation does not allow for that. 

Today is the era of globalism. It is a time when two camps confront each other and divide the world. This must not end in conflict. Unless a standard is set to determine which symbolizes the heart and which symbolizes the body, this world will fall into chaos and cannot escape the path of self-destruction. So, from the perspective of the principles of creation, what should we, who stand at the end of the century, do? If the ideology of creation is such, and if there is an absolute God who can embrace this universe, then humanity can also embrace God. Thus, the human heart is striving to reach the level where it can embrace God. 

That is why it is said that God is within you. How grateful is that? But would God enter into your physical body? The world of the heart is infinite. The world of feelings is also infinite. Because the heart possesses such a nature, God can move centered around that heart and can also be with it. Isn’t that true of your heart? If it were not so, then even if someone were to gain the ability to govern this world freely, there would be no way to fulfill the standards that the heart desires. There is nothing on this earth that can allow the heart to sing and find rest outside of the infinite world and heavenly ethics. If there is a subject that can perform such actions and evoke such feelings, this desire cannot be fulfilled until a relationship is established with that subject. 

We must be humble before heaven. It is heaven that has brought the fallen descendants, who are unworthy and deserving of curses, this far. The author of the Bible we read today, John, has already said that humanity is dead. It is written, "You have a name that you are alive, but you are dead." (Revelation 3:1) 

Though it seems alive, humanity is suffering and groaning under the power of death. This humanity has been brought out, regardless of the means. Through numerous doctrines, it has been brought out. Doctrines that love nations more than individuals have moved nations, and doctrines that love the world more than nations have moved the world. Now what remains is not just the world, but a doctrine that can love both heaven and earth; such a doctrine will be able to conquer heaven and earth. God has brought forth this pitiful humanity through countless struggles and has created such a world today. 

Today, this earth has become a global form, but is there truly a world that resembles God's heart? The form of the body, that is, the external aspect, is all in place, but if this body symbolizes the earth, the question is whether there is a foundation that can connect with God's heart at the end. 

The governance of history 
Today, we do not realize that all phenomena appearing globally in this era are gifts of the historical process moved by heavenly ethics. Because of this, if one has opposed these processes with their own subjectivity during numerous revolutionary processes, they are considered traitors to heavenly ethics. This era is attempting to transition into a new era. When heaven tries to lead this era into a new world of hearts, if many people of the world rebel, they too cannot escape condemnation. The Jewish religion did so before Jesus, and the Israelite nation did so before Jesus. 

Now, as the era of globalism passes and a new era of heavenly ideals approaches, if we do not welcome it with both hands and if the whole does not submit before the center of that era, everything will break apart. This is what is called the great judgment. When the Israelite nation, even in their misery, forgot their historical notions and everything, bowed their heads before Moses, and held onto Moses, who was with heaven, they could cross the blocked Red Sea without difficulty and could overcome the adversities and painful environments beneath Pharaoh. However, once they separated from Moses, the 600,000 people collapsed in the wilderness. Why was that? 

What governs history? It is not the ideologies or doctrines that lead the people of that time. It is the heart that leads toward a higher place. Where is that higher place? It is God's heart. Therefore, history is ultimately paving the way to connect with God's heart. What governs history is not any sovereignty, organization, or institution of that time, but a high ideal that can lead that organization. When a nation is imbued with that ideal and united around it, it thrives; when it is not, it perishes. 

God has a will to establish such an ideal, and centered around that ideal, He has pushed the world into a global form, leading it to the end. So what kind of form should emerge in this world? If the divine content that can become the heart of history does not appear before humanity, then all talk of God's love and so on becomes a lie. This is also why religion has been established in world history. Something new must emerge. 

Grandfather Noah longed for a day when he could receive heavenly blessings while looking forward to something new in the era of family. When God blessed Abraham, He set a condition of hope, saying that his descendants would prosper like the stars of heaven and the sands by the sea. When the Israelite nation came out from the oppression of Pharaoh, He promised to give them the blessings of Canaan. So what did He make them long for when He sent Jesus to this earth? He made them anticipate the Messiah, the embodiment of hope. However, after Jesus could not fulfill that will and departed, for 2,000 years, what did He make them hope for? He made them hope for a new day, the end. Therefore, a nation that loses this standard of hope will be crushed. 

Our bodies are a gift endowed by heaven, but due to the fall, they have not yet become a body that can be gifted. Furthermore, we have not completely found the homeland of our hearts. We have not found the eternal homeland where we can enjoy life with heaven and earth. We have not found the homeland of life where we can live centered around feelings and enjoy life with heaven. 

Human history is said to be a history of recreation, and we have learned that it moves to complete a single person. Therefore, it has led us to place the external aspect of the body on the world stage. The issue here is the homeland of the heart, the homeland of the heart. No matter how much this world externally possesses the form of heaven, if it does not have the homeland of the heart, humanity will be unhappy. No matter how highly developed 20th-century civilization boasts of its contributions to humanity, if it does not provide a resting place for the heart where humans can find peace and forget everything, this history will eventually break apart at some point. 

It is said that humanity has fallen. If the fall is death, then humanity has fallen, and thus the world has died. Because the world is in a position of death, humanity is suffering from the pain that results from it. In other words, it means that humanity is undergoing suffering to resurrect from death. This is the pain of resurrection. 

The greatest desire of humanity and the greatest gift 
When God created humanity, He did not create the heart first but created the body first. Therefore, we must first establish the external world in order to resurrect. You all know from the principles that there are forms of good and forms of evil in this external world, which are today’s two camps. They are clashing and engaging in the ultimate battle. In any case, this must move centered around one; to do so, what must be present? There must be an ideology that can be enjoyed with the external body. If that is absent, the history of humanity will be miserable. 

Humanity has yet to find the homeland of the body. When we see that our bodies are placed in a world of fear, we can understand that we have not found the homeland of the body. No matter how dangerous or difficult the situation may be, a child does not feel fear when they are in their parent's embrace. Likewise, if the homeland of our bodies is found, we should feel joy in our reality, both in heart and body, but on this earth, as time goes on, we are increasingly being captured by fear. 

Heaven did not create everything in the world to destroy humanity. In other words, He did not create everything like a gift filled with poison. 

The fallen human fate is that they must inevitably go through the process of resurrection. We have a historical burden of sin, and we can only conclude that we have reached a final stage where we must settle this burden of sin and transition to a new world. 

So what should we do? Our bodies must be reborn and find rest. We must pass through this hill. Today, the world is at this hill where...
I am in labor. I am experiencing the pain of childbirth. It is to be embraced in the arms of my parents, to find a resting place for my body, to seek the welfare of my body.

The body symbolizes the earth. Therefore, if one wishes to go toward a place where the body can rest and live, one must endure the pain of being reborn. As time passes, one becomes increasingly engulfed by anxiety and fear. However, beyond that peak, there is joy. Isn’t that so? Pregnant women experience increasing pain as the time for childbirth approaches, but once they overcome that pain, there is joy that accompanies it; thus, such a critical moment must exist.

Heaven, which loves humanity, created humans and blessed them, saying, "Your body shall dominate the earth, and your heart shall dominate the heavens." Everyone, have you learned the principles of creation? Our bodies must dominate the earth, and our hearts must dominate the heavens.

What is the greatest desire among human desires? Is it this piece of land? No. The earth can be dominated by this body, but with the heart, one wishes to dominate the spirit world and even make God one’s own. Only then can you find comfort. Until the day you make the best things your own, you must not be at ease. Otherwise, all the words of the Bible are in vain. They are in vain.

What is the purpose for which God created all things? It was to give humanity the most wonderful gifts. What greater gift is there than this body, molded from clay? What greater gift is there than the life breathed into this body, which can attain eternal life?

For 6,000 years, God has gone through a history of bloody struggles to establish a foundation where His heart can dwell. Until now, He has held onto humanity, enduring sacrifice after sacrifice and suffering after suffering, calling and choosing those who have been established as the responsible ones of heaven’s providence, the religious people.

Eventually, a time will come when a new era will arise, a time when childbirth can happen, a time when the world of the body can find rest. At that time, the teachings that lay the foundation for a new heart will be given as words. This is what God is doing. Today, Satan is intruding because a world of rest is coming upon the earth.

Everyone, there will come a time when the value of the gift will be judged. Let us become those who know that the historical body that heaven wishes to establish is a universal gift.

There will come a time when we will be judged by absolute standards, and that time will be the day of judgment. That time will be the day of judgment.

God said that the body should dominate all things, so this body must be able to stand proudly before all things. All things should see this body and say, "Yes, this is my master," and worship it. Therefore, human history has flowed out to fulfill the purpose of the Creator’s blessing.

In the past, when humanity did not know the world, the world seemed infinitely far away, but as civilization has developed, today the world has entered into a single living sphere. Therefore, we must live with a global perspective. On that foundation, our hearts and bodies must transcend the connections of globalism and connect with the cosmos. Heaven has come forth, hoping for a day when that can happen. To make that connection, the one who comes as a representative of humanity is the Messiah. We must not be foolish. The providence is being carried out with orderly laws and contents.

Today, we are individuals within a nation and individuals within a family. However, we must not forget that our nation is a being with cosmic responsibility, and that nation is the greatest gift sent before heaven and earth. You must learn to value your own body. My body is a precious body that heaven and earth have sought for 6,000 years, a precious historical gift. Those who can bow their heads in recognition of this will undoubtedly become the sons and daughters of heaven. They will surely go to heaven.

To complete my one body, God has left bloody traces in history. The path of tears, the path of bloodshed, the path of suffering, the path of injustice have all been walked to establish me as a gift. I must recognize that I have been established as this one body. And I must examine whether I have become one who has betrayed that grace and see what position my appearance, which is a heavenly gift meant to move for the ideals of the cosmos, is in. If that body is lacking and insufficient, I must learn to bow my head. Such people, those who possess such a heart, will undoubtedly become the sons and daughters of God. Such people will surely go to heaven.

Feeling this, when dealing with one’s family, whether with a spouse or children, standing in this position and recognizing oneself as a gift sent for that ideal, and when facing all things, recognizing oneself as one sent to fulfill the purpose of the great universe, if one has only that concept without conscience, one cannot become a cosmic human. Therefore, I must recognize that my body is a historical and cosmic gift. Having such a body, one has acted according to one’s own will, trampling upon heaven above, earth below, and everything surrounding. Would such beings be sent to heaven? They would be thrown into hell immediately, wouldn’t they?

Now we understand, even if we did not know at first. This body is the highest essence created by God over six days, made with the utmost energy, skill, and heart. It is God who dreamed of the world through this and sought to govern the world through it. Humanity has lost this precious gift, this body. Jesus came to restore this body, saying, "What will it profit a man if he gains the whole world and loses his own soul?" (Mark 8:36). Those who abuse the gift of themselves and betray the gift of themselves will perish. If an individual does this, the individual will perish; if a family does this, the family will perish; if a nation does this, the nation will perish; and if the world does this, the world will perish.

In today’s chaotic age, which is the historical end, the confused trends are sweeping around us, but is there not a noble figure that can sing the value of my body, which has been given as a gift before the heavenly providence?

If heaven has awaited one person for 6,000 years, then my body is a gift given by the Father, and when I say, "I will offer this body as a gift," can I not hear the response, "Yes"? This is the highest goal of Christianity seeking the ideal of the bride today.

The Holy Spirit came to the earth because Jesus went away. Jesus is the bridegroom, and the Holy Spirit is the spirit of the bride, so He works on the earth. What has the spirit of the bride been doing for 2,000 years? It is to make the body a gift. The Holy Spirit altar, that is, the 2,000 years of Christian history, is to build an altar where the gift can be completed. Therefore, the bridegroom cannot come until this is concluded.

Then, who will the bridegroom be? He will come as the master of constructing the welfare of the heart and the welfare of the spirit. He is the Lord who comes with the welfare of the heart, a resting place for the heart, and the cosmic perspective. Only then will He become the historical Lord. Only then will He become the historical God, and only then can we become the historical victorious sons and daughters. What good is it to remain in the same state as before?

The ancestors of faith established traditions, and heaven longs to hold onto all of humanity, which is entering into the realm of death, but cannot do so; therefore, it has labored to hold onto one person. After 1,600 years of the fall, the one established was Grandfather Noah. Yet these wretched humans do not know whether heaven exists or not. However, heaven has formed a heart connection with such humans, making it a hope, and has been working to subdue their bodies. We must absolutely obey that will. What kind of obedience must we have? We must know that those who start as individuals representing the historical ideals will receive historical suffering, and we must be grateful for that. Those who wish to escape the judgment of the end must endure the suffering that can transcend judgment at this very moment.

Heaven governs with a historical content, so when our ancestors appear with a heavenly mission, although their forms are small and the time of suffering is short, they have internalized the content of global suffering, putting all conditions in place and working through history. Therefore, if you unravel Noah’s family, all 66 books of the Bible will unravel.

If you unravel Adam’s family, the entire history of the world will unravel. Why? Because although they are individuals, they have symbolically contained global content and have borne all historical responsibilities. The same goes for Abraham and the Jewish people.

In the end, we must surely find the homeland of the heart. The time will undoubtedly come when we can receive the gifts permitted by heaven. You must clearly understand that for 6,000 years, we have come from individuals to families, clans, nations, and now to the world. This is not a passing remark from the person speaking here today; it is a fact.

So what should we do? We must respect the traditions established by the ancestors of faith. We must respect the heavenly lineage. The time has come.

The spirit of loyalty that Grandfather Noah had for 120 years for heaven, the spirit of Abraham wandering in the wilderness after leaving Ur of the Chaldeans, the spirit of Jacob entering Egypt after abandoning the land of Canaan, the spirit of the Israelite nation marching toward the land of Canaan after leaving the enemy’s land of Egypt, and the spirit of Jesus, who came to this earth to gather the Israelite nation and run toward a new welfare of Canaan, a new Eden—where have these spirits gone? You must inherit this spirit through tradition.

When Grandfather Noah was persecuted and wronged by those around him, what did he hope for in his heart? He hoped for the day when God would bless him. The more he was divided, the more he looked forward to the promised day of judgment from God, enduring and enduring again. The same was true for Abraham and Moses.

Moses, who grew up in the palace as the son of a princess, personally had no reason to envy anything in his happy environment, but in his heart, he thought, "This is not where I belong, nor is this where I should live! This is not the welfare that I should enjoy. This is not the place where the Israelite nation, blessed by heaven, should live." He closed his eyes for 40 years, thinking of the land occupied by the seven nations of Canaan, praying secretly, "Father, please fulfill the promise that our chosen Israelite nation will govern the land of Canaan." You must know that this burning heart was present among the more than 600,000 people suffering in Egypt, which is why the Israelite nation chose Moses as their leader.

You know Jesus as the Lamb, but that is not His original form. The Jesus I know is not that Jesus. He had infinite cosmic standards, but He had to become like a lamb because it was not yet the time to exercise His authority. It was indeed a time of chaos, a time when Satan was active. Therefore, He had to become a pitiable figure like a beggar. Today, we are learning about that Jesus.

If Jesus had been able to exercise the authority at that time by fulfilling the hope that had been awaited for 4,000 years from His ancestors, today this world would have already become a good world. However, Jesus left with a heart full of sorrow, never having exercised that authority even once. What was the gift that heaven gave to Jesus? It was to confront the enemies and make them bow their heads and surrender. It was nothing else. If heaven had given Jesus a gift, it was to eradicate the enemies opposing the construction of a new garden, a new land of Canaan. What greater gift could there be? That was the greatest gift heaven could give to Jesus, yet He left without being able to bear that gift.

Heaven gives gifts to connect with our hearts. There is still no welfare of the heart in heaven and earth, so it is anxious. Everywhere one goes, there is an anxious state where the heart is invaded. Isn’t that so? The external world is anxious, and this world must be resolved so that we can find inner peace. Therefore, even if fear enters through this body, if one can sing of heaven with the heart, one will remain until the end.

For 6,000 years, our ancestors have received gifts. What is the purpose of the gift? It is to bear the greatest fruit as a gift that can be offered to the altar of heaven and earth, a gift that heaven and earth can sing about. Seeing the fruit of that gift, even all of creation that has groaned should be able to sing with joy, and even heaven, which has been filled with resentment, should be able to welcome it. You yourselves must become that way. Only then are you the sons and daughters of God. Heaven? The heaven I know is different.

Heaven is externally engaged in a battle with Satan and humanity, while internally, God is working in the providence of the heart, intertwining the hearts of people and God. Do you understand? Externally, the fallen archangel is intruding upon the bodies of humans, while internally, God is intruding upon the hearts of humans. Thus, He is controlling the external world by governing the heart. So, what must we do to bring about the end that heaven desires? Before an environment can appear where the standard of the heart can be established on earth, such an end cannot come. What I mean is that before the Lord comes to this earth, bringing a group where the heart can find rest, that end cannot happen.

Today, our hearts and bodies are being invaded by God and Satan. However, if both the body and heart lean toward God at the same time, God’s battle will end. Satan cannot claim dominion. It will be finished. Furthermore, if the body completely captures the heart centered around the body, that battle will also end. God will not seek to save that person. We are at the intersection of these two battles. If you understand this, you must recognize that there is a Satan who is using this body as a stage for activity.

In this way, our bodies are running toward Satan while our hearts are running toward heaven. Now, a victor must appear who can strike and subdue this external world with the authority of the heart and further subdue Satan. The one who has come with the authority of victory is Jesus. But will you always live believing in Jesus? Until when will you live only serving the Lord? While believing in Jesus, you must also do the work that Jesus did.

Heaven has suffered sorrow, pain, and injustice along with our ancestors throughout the course of history. After 4,000 years, in the second end time, which is the historical end time—if Noah’s time was the first end time, then Jesus’ time is the second end time—who came with the heart and mind of heaven? It was Jesus. He is the human representative sent by God as a gift over 4,000 years, who came with the highest authority to represent heaven and earth. Since we have driven away such a Jesus, He must come again. That is why you say, "Lord! Come!" 

Now is the time to seek the welfare of the heart beyond the welfare of the body.
Welfare of the Mind. No matter how much internal fear surges and the waves of death sweep in, those who can bravely overcome it, those who possess the welfare of the heart, are the citizens of heaven. Even if the waves of death sweep in, the past martyrs who overcame it with a smile are the heavenly people.

Jesus, who hung on the cross and bled in front of countless traitors, even while facing a pitiful and tragic death, prayed for his enemies with courage. This was a manifestation of manly spirit. Although his body was likely to be killed, he established the welfare of the heart. The welfare of the heart cannot be violated, which is why Jesus' body could be resurrected. Where there is a complete plus (+), a complete minus (-) arises. At that time, the authority of resurrection can be invoked. Everyone, it is good to long for the returning Lord. However, more than that, one must become a complete minus in their own body. When there is a complete minus, a complete plus will come.

Those who could not serve the Lord as a bridegroom during their lifetime and could not live as a bride will not enter heaven. This applies to personal heaven and familial heaven alike. Therefore, Jesus had to manifest as a personal Jesus, a familial Jesus, a tribal Jesus, a societal Jesus, a national Jesus, and a global Jesus during his lifetime. You may think that Jesus became a global Jesus all at once, but that is not the case. If that were possible, he would not have died. He could not become a personal Jesus, a familial Jesus, a national Jesus, or a Jesus as the Son of God from Israel. He could not fulfill everything. So, how could he not die?

Today, we believers must know how to embrace the personality of Jesus, who lived for the nation for 30 years, possessing a national personality. Furthermore, you must establish a victorious foundation to embrace the bridegroom Jesus with a national personality. Only then can the Lord, who will come as a global personality, embrace you.

The establishment of a nation is to embrace the world, and the establishment of the world is to embrace heaven and earth. There is no greater crime than casting away the one who was to establish the standard of rest for our bodies and minds as an ideal entity 2,000 years ago. What can we compare this sorrow to? How unfortunate is this?

Jesus established the resting place for our bodies and minds, and furthermore, the ideology of the bride and bridegroom, saying, "I love you." After the resting place for the body and mind was established, he intended to give the love that could embrace heaven and earth, but that plan was shattered. Thus, we are struggling to return.

Where has Judaism, which was established for Jesus after his death, gone? Where has the nation of Israel gone? Where have the old priests and Pharisees gone? They are the arch-enemies of Jesus. The foundation prepared for Jesus over 4,000 years was shattered. Was there a church where Jesus could step in? Was there a person upon whom Jesus could rely? No, there was not.

God sent personal gifts, national gifts, and gifts from nations or denominations for 4,000 years. However, Israel became miserable because it could not embrace Jesus, the heavenly gift who could dominate the whole. The chosen people, who awaited the day of glory and blessing, have suffered and wandered, and this has been the history of Israel up to today. This is the price of the sin of killing Jesus.

Still, because they were blessed, they have come forth before the world, even while being trampled and wronged. A nation that should have come forth in glory has become a people who think their suffering history is a gift. 

Even when we analyze history, we cannot deny this fact, yet do you believe that Jesus came to die? That is not the case.

We must prepare our bodies and repent of the historical crimes. Abraham and Moses committed wrongs, but they could all be forgiven if they repented. They were messengers. But what about the nation that killed its beloved son? Think about it. When you consider your love for your children and God's love for Jesus, which do you think is greater?

When Jesus died, the heavens and the earth were dark for three hours. Wouldn't that be so? All the efforts God made over 4,000 years were shattered in an instant, and at the moment when his beloved son was ensnared by Satan and crucified, do you think God said, "Oh, the history of salvation is being completed, oh, victory has been achieved"? No. God must have felt unbearable sorrow. Knowing this heart of heaven, Jesus died. We must understand this.

The wrongs committed by our ancestors in the past can be forgiven. But what about the sin of our ancestors who nailed the Messiah to the cross and made him bleed? What must we do? The historical sin of killing Jesus, who was to become the body of heaven and the victorious temple, who said, "I am in you, and you are in me, and I am in the Father, and the Father is in me," must be repented. We must repent and believe in Jesus.

Today, 2,000 years after history has passed, we are again struggling, longing for the gifts of the heart and mind. How can we receive those gifts? This is the challenge for the world ahead. So what must we do? We must know what God has done in the past. We must understand why it has come to this. We must also know what God is doing in this age. Furthermore, we must know what God intends to do in the future. In other words, we must know the times. We must be able to discern whether it is night or day, morning or evening.

Look. From a historical perspective, we are now in the autumn season. The 20th century is the civilization era of the autumn season. The ancient civilization era was the summer season, the tropical civilization era, and today is the autumn season, the temperate civilization era. After the autumn civilization era passes, the winter season, the polar civilization era, will come, and after that, the spring civilization era will arrive. This is the new age.

Since humanity fell, we have not been able to welcome the spring civilization era. The heart has not rejoiced, the body has not rejoiced, and we have not been able to enjoy a world where everything that moves in heaven and earth can bring joy to heaven. To welcome that world, you must know the historical God. You must know the historical God, the God of the times, and the God of the future. Then God will give us a gift to determine the value of the whole.

Now we must establish a center that can achieve the welfare of the heart and a center that can achieve the welfare of the mind, finding a standard where the heart, mind, and body can connect. After the body and mind become one, we must embrace the world. Therefore, in this age, the ideology of Godism must emerge, greater than that of globalism. We must establish a God-centered ideology. Only then can humanity live on this earth, and if we do not establish a firm standard through which our bodies and minds can connect with the heart of heaven, we cannot live happily.

Thus, we must live in our living sphere centered on that ideology, where our hearts and bodies can rest and enjoy, while also experiencing the historical heart of God, the heart of God of the times, and the heart of God of the future. Only then can we stand before the world as the final gift of the universe. 

So what is the ultimate purpose of this gift? It is not to dominate the earth. It is to embrace the infinite world based on this world and ultimately to embrace God. This is the ultimate purpose. To embrace God, to make God ours. We must understand that under this purpose, God has been working to restore humanity.

God wants to give everything of the heart world and the heart realm to humanity, and eventually, even God Himself. This is the great gift that heaven will give to humanity, and the remaining gifts that will be given to us from now on. We cannot receive that gift until we know the historical, the God of the times, and the God of the future. God is saying that He will give Himself to humanity. He gave His son, and later, God Himself will come to live with humanity.

"You are me, and I am you," and "I am your Father, and you are my son and daughter." He wants to live in that position. You must understand that being able to live with God at the center of love in the welfare of the heart is the greatest gift that humanity can receive. Heaven has been working tirelessly to achieve that purpose.

From an individual perspective, the body is a gift representing the earth, the heart is a gift representing heaven, and the ideology is a gift that can embrace the entire universe. Even this alone is overwhelming, but later, God Himself will also give you as a gift, and I hope you will become a qualified person who can stand before this grateful meaning.

<Prayer> Father, we have heard Your words. We did not know that we ourselves are such a tremendous gift, and we did not realize that the reason for regulating our lives hour by hour and commanding our hearts was to give such a gift for the sake of the precious whole value.

Even when we stand in a position of injustice, allow us to be able to receive the gifts that the heart brings before the body. Also, allow us to be those who can cherish the ideology that attracts the heart.

When God's heart wants to give Himself as a gift through my ideology, my heart, and my body, may we be sons and daughters who can step forward without shame. 

Please allow us to realize that we are living our lives through this three-dimensional connection. We understand that we are in a struggle to separate good from evil in all aspects of our lives and to establish the reality of good. Now, in the new cosmic age that remains after history has passed, may we receive the Father as a gift, and may we become those who are not lacking in receiving the love of the Father, the ideology of the Father, and the heart of the Father.

May we be heavenly sons and daughters who know how to cherish the gifts, and may the Father bless us and take pride in us. May we become sons and daughters who are not lacking in taking on the responsibilities and legacy of the whole world, and I earnestly pray this in the name of the Lord. Amen.

2)
The Ultimate Issue is the Father and Me
We must become people who can treat the earth and all people with the heart of a parent. If Adam and Eve had been grateful before God with that heart, just as God treated them, God would have added something new to them. However, because they fell, God had to stop that. That is why God has been pouring His heart and effort into restoring humanity for 6,000 years until today. 

The root of tragedy is considered to be due to Satan rather than the children, and the unjust and sorrowful conditions are attributed to Satan, while only the joyful conditions are used to deal with the children. 

God fulfills what the intangible heart desires in a tangible way. We must fulfill God's hope even if it means dying and dying again. If we cannot do that, we cannot remove God's sorrow. 

You do not know how much effort God has put into raising you to this standard, which you cannot hear or see. Therefore, we must realize that we were called and born for the sake of the Father.

The reason our ancestors were close to the archangel but not close to the Father was the cause of the fall. 

Restoration is not for any nation or humanity, but for the Father. We must keep this in mind. Therefore, in any difficult situation, we must work for the nation or the state while being grateful. Then, even if we cannot become sons of God, we can become loyal subjects of the state.

No matter what difficulties, frustrations, or injustices we face, it is natural to recall the work of the Father. We must be able to say, "Thank you." God will bless those who can do this. In the face of providential will, there is infinite pain, infinite sorrow, and infinite crosses. God is looking for those who do not know where to place themselves due to their own shortcomings. 

Let us not become those who lament for ourselves in the future. We must not evade the banner of Satan or become weary and fall before it.

The ultimate issue is the Father and me. If we understand how the Father’s restoration work is carried out, we have no excuses. Only with this heart can we find true sons and daughters. The issue is to know the heart of the Father and to participate in the restoration work. 

Even if I have to leave everything behind, I will do any work, including evangelism. Now, please entrust me with the cross of the Father. We must have the heart of love for our parents to overcome this final hurdle. We must know that the Father is the entirety of hope and value and uphold Him. Furthermore, we must be able to feel honored to be the sons of the Father. 

The love of God that raised Jesus from death comes from the relationship between the Father and the Son. Therefore, we must have the heart that says, "The Father has worked for 6,000 years, suffering and being wounded. How can my efforts, wounds, and sorrows compare to that of the Father?" If we have this heart, Satan cannot pull us away.

If we think of God, who grieved over losing His children, we must be able to weep for the pitiful humanity and grasp the God who has endured historical sorrow. Even though I am just one out of 2.7 billion people, I must have the heart that participates in God's will. Now, we must not only receive the love of our parents but also become their representatives.

Even while I am asleep, the Father is working somewhere. When you see someone in a difficult situation, do not treat them from your own perspective; rather, know that they have a wife or husband, parents and children, or siblings who love them dearly, and treat them from that perspective. 

If parents have a cross, there is no cross greater than the emotional cross. When you see a villager in a difficult situation while passing by, or when the nation faces a dire situation, live with the heart that says, "Do not worry on behalf of the Father. Am I not here?" If you live with that heart, they will be friends, brothers, and sons and daughters of heaven. 

Parents always carry the emotional cross and walk the path of the sacrificial cross. No one has worked harder than God, not Noah, not Moses, not even Jesus.
God is the one who has worked harder than any individual, any nation, or any teacher. In this age, God is the one who stands in the position of a sacrifice. Since the Father is like that, I must also walk the path of sacrifice. The only way for us to stand before the Father is through that. Therefore, regardless of which country or institution we face, this is the Father's, and thus it is mine. Those who work there are doing the Father's work, which means they are doing my work. We must think this way. When we see a farmer working in the field, we should be able to comfort them, even if it means giving them some money from our pockets, and we should be able to bless them, thinking that my sons and daughters are working there. Only then can we become the sons and daughters of the Father.

Even when looking at a blade of grass, we should be able to shed tears, realizing that it has grown for the Father. The people of the Third Israel must move with such a heart and think that wherever they go, it is my land and my work. In the future, what the teacher aims for is to create many individuals who can take on the role of the owner in place of the Father, possessing the heart of a parent.

What I wish for the young men and women of this land is this: above all, they must become those who possess the Father. If my heart is like this, I must be able to think about what the Father's heart must be like. The Father who looks up high and wide, the teacher also looks at you in that way.

Therefore, you must become those who endure the position of the cross and sacrifice. Those who evangelize, study, and work with such a heart cannot fail. Volunteer to be the sacrifice at the very bottom. A sacrifice prays when there are difficulties. That position is not a comfortable one.

When you stand in the position of a sacrifice, you will hear many comments about whether it is good or bad, but you must become the sacrifice of that region wherever you go. A sacrifice cannot protest even when it is killed. However, a bowed-down sacrifice appears with the authority of life. God has walked this way, and the teacher and the members of the Unification Church have walked this way.

We have our own path and the path of sacrifice. While walking my own path, I cannot evangelize. However, if I walk the path of sacrifice for more than three years, up to six years, no one can resist before it. Approach everything from the standpoint of being the son of a wealthy family, the son of God. With such a heart, when you cross the peak of blessings, God will entrust everything to you.

What shall we live for?
Matthew 6:16-34
<Prayer> Father, we who admire You have gathered here, hoping to see You and to discuss with You, despite our shortcomings, so please do not forsake us. 

Father! Please be harmonious with our hearts and connect with our bodies. May the flow of Your earnest heart not remain solely Yours, but may the flow of the life of Your existence deeply permeate our hearts at this time. 

As we gaze upon the image of the Father who commands thousands and millions of saints, may we be able to embrace the infinite love of the Father and be immersed in longing for You. May this hour allow us to thank You for being in the warm nest of nature and to call upon You with our bowed heads and hearts. 

Father! We know that before You, who calls us and cares for us on the path of struggle, You are the Father who is deep within our hearts, in a quiet place, where we cannot help but feel and think of You. We know that the bond that allows us to call You our Father must be established in our lives. 

Have we ever had a secret discussion with the Father on any given day? On November 1, 1959, at the former headquarters church, was there a time when we bowed our heads in worship before the Father, intoxicated by His gentle voice and glory? We know that such moments are essential on the path of faith. We also know that the Father has worked hard until today to grant us such moments, so please allow this time to be one where our bodies and hearts can joyfully welcome the Father of nature, the Father of our true nature, and the Father of our essence. 

You are not a Father who sets conditions and approaches us; You are the Father who flows with the movement of our hearts and acts according to the movement of our hearts. We recognize that being in harmony and moving with our original feelings and emotions is the hope and ideal we must have while living on this earth. 

We know that You are the Father who manages everything invisibly and strives to manifest results, the Father who seems absent but truly exists, the Father who governs our hearts despite seeming unrelated to us, and the Father who governs the infinite world. 

We long for the original state that can harmonize, be still, and move within that jurisdiction. Therefore, Father, please do not forsake us. If there is anyone whose heart is closed, please open that door, and if there are those who are caught in the shadow of death, suffering mentally or physically, please have compassion on them as well. We have gathered here to seek and respect our connections, so please guide this hour to not be in vain. 

For whom, for what, have we moved our steps to come to this place today? Father, do not forsake us, and if there is no true heart longing for the existing Father, let us realize how shameful it is to stand before You, the Father of heaven and the Father of existence. 

Even today, as we think of the Father and look upon Him, we must be able to immerse ourselves in the grace of the Father, and this time is absolutely necessary for Your sons and daughters gathered here to be caught in the grace of the Father. Therefore, Father, manifest Your work of compassion, fulfill us with the authority of power, and sincerely hope and desire that You will resolve our hearts that carry the sorrow of restoration left by You. 

Let us be able to laugh at the authority of death and confidently assert what authority we have to boast about it, and let us be able to tell everyone to look upon the glory of heaven and to take pride in heaven, becoming victorious sons and daughters who can sing of the glory of the Father. 

Knowing that there is heaven and earth, we understand that humanity must exist alongside them, and even if the waves of death and the waves of fear sweep in, we know that heaven and earth will remain forever. Please guide us to be sons and daughters who can participate in the world of joy beyond this world of fear, and let us be pioneers in pioneering the world of ideals. 

Even if our hearts are different today, and our circumstances and internal customs or subjective views and concepts are different, we know that the desire to harmonize with the original world of heart is the same, and that both good and evil people can harmonize with that. Therefore, we earnestly hope and desire that You will lead us to be able to do so at this time. 

We wish for this time to be one where we can lay everything before the Father and, with a selfless heart, find our original heart to serve the Father and be able to reshape ourselves through the Word. 

Please do not let the hearts of the one who conveys and the one who receives become two. Knowing that the dark conditions of evil are lurking for gaps, may our hearts and bodies harmonize with the Father's heart and movement, allowing us to be caught in the heart of peace, the heart of love, and the heart of noble ideals. We earnestly ask that this hour may be one where we can raise new resolutions and new lives, and we pray all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen. 

<Word> The title I wish to speak about today is "What Shall We Live For?" 

Everything that exists has a purpose. This is true for the earth and the heavens. There is a heaven and an earth, and we humans, who represent that heaven and earth, exist. Although we may not realize it, heaven must have a great purpose, and the earth must also have a great purpose. Even though the positions and standings of heaven and earth may differ, their purposes must be the same. Why is that? Because heaven is the subject, and earth is the object; heaven is the Creator, and earth is the creation that has been created. Thus, as long as this earth is a creation that has come into being by the Absolute Being, we cannot deny that heaven and earth are in the same fate within the purpose of the Absolute Being.

If heaven and earth are like that, what about humans, who have appeared in place of heaven and earth? If humans cannot deny heaven and cannot deny earth, then neither can heaven nor earth deny humans. From this perspective, it is certain that heaven and earth are looking toward some great purpose together with humanity.

That is why we say that our hearts symbolize heaven and our bodies symbolize the earth. The body seeks the things of the earth, while the heart seeks the things of heaven. The self is not just the heart or just the body. The self can only be called the self when the heart and body are united. What does this self symbolize? It can be said to symbolize God.

Even if you consider yourselves to be inadequate, incomplete, or in an unfinished stage, the individual that is formed by the union of heart and body must remain within a certain purpose realm, and that is to be with God. With heaven as the subject, I become its object, and as an existing entity that symbolizes the existing God, I must coexist with Him. Only then can I embrace and move heaven and earth. Achieving that time and place is the highest purpose of humanity. It must absolutely be so. Therefore, heaven and earth are playing a game of elevating humanity.

What has God been working for until now? It is not for heaven. It is not for the earth. It is for humanity. He has worked solely to save fallen humanity, that is, to save you yourselves. 

You may live without knowing this reason, but even in your existence, the myriad spirits of heaven are mobilized, the earth is mobilized, and even God is mobilized to work for you. Do you know this fact? 

Even if I am an extremely insignificant being, in the journey of life that represents this universe, the myriad spirits of heaven move for me, the earth moves for me, and God works for me. In the face of this undeniable fact, we, the common people, must bow our heads in awe. We must be able to do so. A person who lives with such a heart is a conscientious person. We must recognize that the steps taken by those who have walked the historical path, holding onto God, are the footsteps of religious individuals.

All things, including God and the created world, must recognize that everything is mobilized to make my individual self a person who can achieve a purpose and win. However, fallen humanity does not recognize this. 

What shall I live for?
So now, for whom shall I live, and for what shall I live? This is the question. When considering this, I must reflect on what I am currently living for. What have you lived for until now? Have you lived for the earth? Have you lived for heaven? I can find no one today who can confidently say that they have lived fully to fulfill the Creator's will on this earth.

What is the reason for this? Whether viewed religiously or otherwise, it is because humanity has fallen. Because of the fall, humanity has left the original ideal garden where it could live well and has left the environment where it could live for the whole. The heart desires to live that way, but the body cannot achieve it; this is the condition of fallen humanity living on this earth.

In this position, we are living. Originally, humanity should live in the world of high ideals, but having fallen from that position, the dignified humanity is struggling in an utterly miserable place. 

However, you will feel a desire to live better. There is no one who can deny the desire to live better, to feel greater, wider, higher, and more infinite value. 

This desire to live better exists, but there is no practical content or life ideals that can move toward that purpose. Even though you live, can you confidently say, "Heaven, earth, God, cooperate with me"? Many of you cannot do that. 

I cannot be a being who knows the content of the original life of creation, nor can I stand confidently before the myriad spirits of heaven, the creatures of the earth, and the Creator God. However, the myriad spirits of heaven are working for you even at this moment, the earth is also working for you, and God is working for you. Yet, humanity has walked a historical path of wandering, longing for that world, without even knowing whether there is heaven, earth, or God.

Moreover, the young men and women gathered here must take this opportunity to reconsider what they live for. If God were to ask you, "What have you lived for?" what would you answer? Among you, would anyone confidently say, "I lived for my family"? "I lived for my loved ones"? "I lived for my country"? "I lived for my faith"? "I lived for my studies"? 

However, taking a step further, if you ask for whom those things exist, you cannot say they exist for yourself. For whom does that country exist? You must understand that it does not exist solely for itself. Why? Because it is a nation, a people, and a world that is within the purpose realm of the great universe. Therefore, it is certain that everything that exists does not exist solely for itself.

Is my purpose view correct?
Originally, these things are meant to exist based on the original heart, yet today, human concepts are centered around themselves. The idea of concluding everything in a self-centered family, nation, and world is fundamentally flawed. Even if one says they live for their family, living for the family is not the entirety of purpose. Living is good. Living for others is also good. However, one must recognize that the environment in which they are living for is not the ultimate thing that can receive that purpose.

That is why it is a natural phenomenon to long for something higher beyond the place we are living in. The heavenly principle encourages you in this way, urging you to go toward a higher place. Today, at this time, I hope you will all reflect on what you live for.
is being urged. It is good to love one's children with all the intelligence one possesses. But where does a person originate from? The limbs and body of my own being did not originate solely from myself. If we dig deeply, we find that they came from ancestors throughout history, and if we dig even deeper, we find that they originated from some master who is the source of those ancestors' spirits.

For this reason, the emotions we feel today are historical emotions. The hopes we desire today are also historical hopes. Although we may discuss various ideologies today, those ideologies are not new to this era. Our ancestors may not have known or spoken about them, but their hearts have longed for a world beyond the ideals of today.

Now is the time for the ideals of that emotional world, which we have hoped for alongside history, to emerge. Therefore, when we focus our energies on something, we must gather ourselves and think once more. What I prioritize for myself cannot be a true purpose. We must automatically consider the fact that it is not something worthy of which we can invest our entire being and sacrifice our lives.

You must think again about the steps you take without much thought. For whom am I going? For whom am I moving? And where will what I prioritize show its value? Just because my being feels satisfaction and joy from that movement, does it mean I can conclude my mission to boast before the universe? No, it does not. We must think again. It is time to reconsider.

Even if I devote my heart and all my efforts to something to the extent that I cannot gather my spirit, my being is not the initiator of that movement. When you say you love someone and act for someone, does it seem that the true subject creating that heart is yourself? That subjective heart may seem to be within me, but it passes through me, and though it may seem absent from me, it comes through me. Thus, it is a phenomenon occurring in an environment that can be connected through you. Therefore, you will feel in your living environment that you cannot be the subject or the position to conclude any content.

The place where the body, mind, and heart can reside
Humans have a body and a mind. They have a body received from their parents and are supplied with the materials that constitute the body from the earth. However, the mind is problematic here. God wants to establish that body and mind on the expectation of an unchanging heart. This is the purpose for which God created humans and the purpose for which He governs fallen humanity. No matter how good and comfortable the heart may be, that heart cannot rest in the house of the heart, and neither can the body. When you consider your reality, you cannot deny this fact.

There must be a place where the human body can reside, a place where the mind can reside, and a place where the heart can reside. Humans are struggling in the process of seeking such places.

I do not know how it happened, but I have embarked on the journey of life and find myself in a position where I cannot turn back. In this situation, I realize that longing for something and living for someone cannot be the true purpose of life. As long as we live like this, we must recognize that we will have to go through a sorrowful process in living out the remaining life.

We must know this and reflect once more on how we have lived until now. In this world, there are many people living like travelers carrying burdens, struggling through life without knowing where to go or what direction to take. You, who are present here, must also think about yourselves once again. In such a position, no matter how much you say you live for someone, that purpose has nothing to do with the purpose of the heavenly principle.

History is a continuous revolution. There have been times when individuals were respected, families were respected, clans were respected, nations were respected, and the world was respected. Thus, history progresses through a process of revolution toward the world of purpose.

Countless ideologies have emerged until now, and many tribes have asserted ideologies centered on their own tribes or clans, but they have all passed. Now, what remains in the world are two major ideologies. The purpose is one, but having two ideologies indicates that we are getting closer to one, and that is why today is called the end.

The flow of history is moving toward an environment that can pave the way for the world of purpose. So, when the time of purpose comes, what should we do? We must collide. We must either break or unite. The place where broken beings are gathered and dealt with is hell, and the place where unbroken beings are gathered is heaven. The division between heaven and earth, heaven and hell is based on the perspective of purpose.

The problem of the flow of history and the perspective of purpose
Today, even when we look at the flow of history or the trends of the times, we have arrived at a breathless era. In this age, for whom shall we live, and for what shall we live? The time of living for the family has passed. Look at the advanced countries. Everything is divided. It is individualism. Where are the parents, and where are the children? Everything that can be trusted is breaking apart.

We are living shaken by these world trends. In this living environment, for whom am I living? Living for the family is good. However, the world trend does not allow for comfort and happiness within the family. The same applies to the nation and the world. Since history flows toward the world of purpose, the world itself cannot solve everything, and each cannot live for itself. This fact is clearly proven by history. Therefore, people of this era long for something new, a purpose or a great purpose in which they can participate.

From this perspective, how have you lived? If you only know your own children and your own possessions within the confines of your family, can you participate in the day when the great universe's purpose is achieved? What you have lived for is for your own comfort, your own environment, and your own family, not for the great purpose. That is why you are falling behind. When someone asks you, "For whom have you lived?" and you cannot provide evidence of what you have lived for, you should feel indignant and wronged.

Setting aside the past, if we ask at this very moment for whom and for what you are living, is there anyone who can boast that they live centered on what is best in the world? However, even if you say you live like that, can you incorporate the world of conscience flowing toward the great purpose into your life and live a peaceful life? No, you cannot. Therefore, you cannot reach the infinite world.

The movement of the heart that desires to live joyfully is heading toward that purpose, even if you forget time and moments. But do you have the capacity to embrace not only yourself but also your family, your tribe, the world, and heaven and earth? Today, there are various ideologies, but is there an ideology that can embrace God within its sphere? Is there an ideology that can embrace the heavenly principle? There is not.

How much capacity does your heart have to endure?
You have a heart, but what does that heart seek to embrace? It seeks to embrace the world, to embrace heaven and earth, and ultimately to embrace God. That is the purpose of the heart. That is why Jesus said, "The kingdom of heaven is within your heart." Furthermore, He said, "I am in you, and you are in me, and the Father is in you, and you are in the Father."

Today, how much can you involve your neighbors in the ideals you possess or the living environment in which you exist? How much can you include your nation, and how much can you encompass the world? Your heart is great. Yet, you must recognize that you are fallen beings who cannot even embrace your own body within your own heart. The heart seeks to embrace heaven and earth and even God to bring them to rest. Yet, despite this, you are struggling without conquering your own body centered around that heart. And yet you say, "What does it matter?" But that is not a simple problem.
