If true artists or true religious people were to sing, what kind of song would they sing? They would sing a song that can embrace humanity within the heart that hosts God and includes heaven and earth. You must become such a person. If there were such a person, would heaven punish them? No, it would not. How many such people are there? There are none.

When the absolute being asks, "For whom and for what have you lived?" can you respond with, "I have lived like this and that"? That would be the highest purpose I have sought. Yet, no one has ever received praise for that throughout history.

No matter how capable a person may be, they are swayed by the trends of the times, and no matter how devoted a family may be, if the trends sweep through, they will be shattered. Even the beloved family that cannot be separated from me will break when confronted with the flames of revolution. The society I desired will also break apart. The nation I devoted my whole heart and loyalty to will also break apart. How can this be?

Even in a life lived for others, we cannot find joy because we are fallen beings. What you prioritize is not the purpose itself but merely a process toward the purpose. If you consider that to be everything and continue on, you will find yourself blocked. You will end up surrendering before the great trend.

However, the heavenly principle is alive. It is alive day and night. It exists beyond my consciousness. For this reason, the heart that desires to follow this living heavenly principle, that spirit will seek to guide me. Yet, how much have you betrayed this living heavenly principle? You must recognize that you are betrayers. Regardless of what you claim, you must clearly understand that you are in a position of betrayal.

To become a successful person in the journey of life
When we look at the individual, there is a body, a mind, and a heart. The body represents the earth, the mind represents heaven, but what does the heart represent? It represents the heavenly principle. Therefore, this heart governs the ideology. It also governs God. No matter how much of a creator or absolute being He is, when you call out, "Father!" He responds, "Yes." We must live in a way that exchanges, harmonizes, and enjoys with Him to achieve the ultimate purpose of our lives.

Those who boast about what they have lived for may seem admirable in their time, but from a historical or cosmic perspective, that is not the case. They fit a certain period. That is why the nation itself must clarify what it has lived for until now. Historical figures have clarified families in new fields, clarified societies in new fields, and clarified eras in new fields.

In clarifying, you must focus your heart. Whatever business you engage in, whatever studies you pursue, or whatever work you do, if you do not work from a place where your heart is infinitely soaring, you will fail. If you work from that place where your heart naturally inclines, your body will naturally incline before that heart, and your emotions will naturally incline there, and you will undoubtedly succeed. Many prophets and sages have come and gone throughout history, but no one has completely succeeded in the journey of life. Everyone has failed midway.

Then, where can the relative that can incline the body, mind, and heart be found? Where is the family? Where is society? Where is the nation? Where are such worlds, heaven and earth, and God? The reason for the cries of reappearance and manifestation in religion lies here.

My own life is serious. Once it passes, it cannot be reborn, rectified, or supplemented. The past journey of life cannot be supplemented. For what have you lived? Living for oneself is not living for a purpose. I am merely a body living within that realm.

The human figure that God seeks to establish

However, humans have become beings who have lost both purpose and motivation within their living realm. Such humans, no matter how capable or well-off they may be, will be swept away. Such beings can sweep away individuals, tribes, nations, and even the world. Since humans who have lost motivation and purpose can be swept away, it does not violate the heavenly law.

If we trace the history of the Israelite people, had they held onto the motivation and purpose blessed by God, other nations would not have been able to invade them. However, since they lost the standard of blessing, what kind of chosen people are they? Thus, it became a condition for other nations to swallow them up.

If this is true for human beings, how much more so for God, who moves humanity? If there is heaven and Satan, what is humanity's perspective of purpose concerning God?
In a foundation where one lacks clarity and a firm relationship with God, when Satan attacks, one can only lose God. You must understand that we are humans struggling in such a fate.

Therefore, philosophy and religion must detect the fundamental relationships regarding such matters. They must also discern the purpose. The philosophies and religions up to now have proclaimed and advocated alongside trends, only to perish alongside them. Those that asserted their claims with the times and trends have all failed.

Thus, in this present age, two trends remain, and they are tilting to one side. It has been said that the time of that end is near. The time of purpose is undoubtedly approaching. However, there is no content that can clarify what that purpose is. The suffering incurred from wandering and struggling without motive or purpose is immeasurable. In the past, it was limited to familial, social, and national damage, but now we are facing global harm. That global harm returns to each of you. You have lived believing you were right, claiming to stand for something with your own standards, but the global phenomenon is aimed at you.

In the past, there was no relationship between me and the United States, the United Kingdom, or various Western nations, but today their emotional states reach our surroundings. Their grievances are our grievances, and their difficulties are our difficulties. We must recognize that all phenomena in this world are turning around our individual selves.

So, how should young men and women live in such an environment? They must hold onto both motive and purpose in one hand. This is the mission of what is called a global religion that must be resolved.

The will of God must be taken as the first purpose.

You, our Korean people, are pitiful. We are a pitiful nation that cannot believe here or there.

When I see a young person strutting down the street, I want to grab them and say this: "Hey, for whom are you moving? Ah, I lived for this reason. What can you say? There is nothing. The past is like that, the present is like that, and the future will be the same. It would have been better not to have come to this earth at all. The younger you are, the more you must realize that we are like this.

What you are looking at now is not the first purpose but the second purpose. There is a first purpose that God desires and that history desires. The life of Jesus with a clear purpose

Jesus was a person with a clear understanding of cause, motive, and purpose. He did not know anything else. Jesus held onto God, held onto heaven, and held onto earth as he moved forward. He lost everything that humans possess. He was deprived of everything that humans have. However, he possessed the world of causes and motives that humans do not know, and he possessed the world of purpose. He was unjustly killed by those who moved with authority in that era, but his worldview will remain with human history. His ideology has been leading human history up to today.

Look. Jesus grew up with severe wounds in the household of Joseph, but that was a process. Where was the family for Jesus? He knew that family was not the ultimate destination. He also knew that society was not the ultimate destination. That was Jesus.

So when Jesus came out toward the Jewish community, he faced those who said, "Don't go, you!" and he said, "No, even if you oppose me, I must go." Furthermore, even when the people of Israel mobilized and labeled him a national traitor, telling him not to go, he said, "No, I must go." What did Jesus live for? Even if they told him not to go with his life on the line, he said, "I will go for the lives that are on this earth." What was the purpose behind his death? 

He had to establish motives and purposes, so Jesus bravely transcended all the process-oriented world.

In that sense, Jesus is the Savior. He was with the ideology of heaven in any environment on earth, and even when he ate, he did so with the ideology. While eating, he had a fervent heart asking, "When will the day come when the world of happiness that can make the Father rejoice be realized?" Jesus lived like that. Even in the face of resentment and injustice, he said, "Father! How much have you labored to bestow the historical ideology upon humanity? I am grateful that you have placed us in a position to share in your sorrow."

That was Jesus.

Even today, God is looking for such a person. How long do you think heaven has been waiting for a person who possesses motive and purpose, rather than humans struggling without them? Because of the responsibility to teach motive and purpose to those who do not know such things, heaven cannot abandon humanity and continues to hold onto them. How great must heaven's anguish be? Why can heaven not freely deal with humanity, which is becoming a victim of Satan in the environment of death? If there is anyone who understands heaven's painful heart, that person has fought a fierce battle in their heart and has also fought the greatest external battle in history, and you must understand this.

Jesus fell like a weak person, but his world of heart was closer to God's heart than anyone else since the beginning of history, and because he fought fiercely against the world that opposed him, namely Satan, he was able to rise again on that condition. That is the resurrection.

Jesus said, "Live for that kingdom and its righteousness." But the issue is not Jesus himself; the issue is the motive and purpose. We must clearly understand this. Jesus also sacrificed his life for that motive and purpose. Therefore, even though Jesus left, his ideology and purpose remain.

Since humanity is born with life before the heavenly principles, they must surely live for something. Even if they suffer and fall, those who live to elevate that kingdom and its righteousness will never perish.

The gospel among gospels

What are you living for in whatever environment you find yourself? Are you thinking for yourself? The era of living for oneself has passed. What sovereignty are you boasting about? That sovereignty will also be overwhelmed by global trends. When the subject of purpose, which is heaven, appears, that global trend will also pass away. This is a historical destiny. Because the path of fallen humans has been such, heaven has proclaimed it before humanity.

"Live for heaven." This is the gospel among gospels, the most precious news among news. Heaven knows that everything will pass, but the subject that governs the heavens will remain. Heaven knows that existence itself is eternal and unchanging and will always exist, so it has proclaimed that we should believe in and serve that subject. You must understand that those struggling on the altar and knocking on the door of religion are people who cannot find comfort in the world of conscience.

The heart that believes in heaven and the heart that serves heaven cannot be conquered by any revolutionary ideology.

Many Christians have been slaughtered throughout history, yet Christianity remains. Why? Because nothing can conquer God. The external world can be dominated, but the world of the heart cannot be dominated, and even more so, the world of the heart that transcends the heart cannot be dominated. The world of the heart and the world of the heart's feelings exist beyond the environment. That is why Christianity, which emerged with such an ideology, has indeed become a global religion.

Therefore, we who have a purpose are more revolutionary than any great person or any individual in the historical course. The world of the heart and the world of the heart's feelings cannot be dominated by sin. Only the highest master, God, can govern it. This is something I know and you know. Members of the Unification Church, I am serious. Even if I am trampled upon in the historical course, if there is even one person who can protect the world of heart and feelings from being violated by anyone, I will hold onto that one person. There, a new history awaits.

When Jesus distributed bread to thousands of people, they welcomed him with joy. However, when Jesus prayed in the Garden of Gethsemane or carried the cross, even the three disciples went to their own places. It is sorrowful that Jesus and the disciples parted ways like that. They were disciples who could not bravely transcend the miserable position alongside Jesus and were dominated by Satan.

The goal of the returning Savior and the responsibility of the saints

Everyone! We have stepped out with a new ideology. We stand in the ranks marching toward a new destination with new motives and new goals. As you walk that path, there will be historical conflicts, and you may get entangled in the circumstances of the times. In the process of going through such a painful path, you must not become someone who deviates or is violated in the world of feelings. If that happens, surely the day of victory will come, and the day of liberation will come. That day of liberation, which we long for in our hearts and feelings, is the day that humanity collectively hopes for. The day when a garden of happiness can be enjoyed by the body, the heart, and the feelings is the day we hope for.

On that day, we will not be the subjects who enjoy it. We must invite the Absolute Being as the subject and rejoice, so that His joy becomes my joy, my joy becomes His joy, and it can become the joy of heaven and earth. If there is someone who looks forward to such a day, nothing can dominate them.

Jesus did not betray even when loving parents betrayed him, even when the entire nation that had been waiting for him with a heart like flesh and blood opposed him, even when the Jewish community that prayed for him all night opposed him, and even when the disciples who feared they would starve betrayed him. Why did he not betray them? Because Jesus, who faced heaven, could not betray the world of feelings even if difficult circumstances swept away everything and he lost the world. The path Jesus took to become one who occupied the world of feelings was the path of the cross. Although he could not be a prince serving heaven in body, he fulfilled his responsibility as a prince serving heaven in the world of feelings.

What is Jesus' sorrow? It is that he could not have a living environment to serve heaven. To resolve this sorrow, the one who is to come is the returning Lord. Although he rejoiced in his heart and feelings and was grateful to heaven, he had no substantial family, no substantial church, no substantial nation, and no substantial world centered around him, which is why he must return. If seeking such things is the goal of the Savior, how should the saints of the end times, who are to welcome the returning Savior, act? With heart and feelings...
Although Jeong found such an ideology, he could not live that way in body, so the people of the end times must live in such an environment with their bodies as well. Thus, throughout the course of history, religious freedom and freedom of speech have been granted.

Heaven holds a historical sorrow that cannot freely express all emotional truths or move as it wishes. Therefore, Heaven has pushed humans, who have created sin, to fight among themselves. The one who will come at the end times with a new ideology and measures to resolve this fight is the returning Lord.

Therefore, you who are in the end times must understand that Heaven has mobilized, the earth has mobilized, and countless prophets and sages have mobilized to find one person with whom you can enjoy the heart of the Father, who is the Father of the heart, the Father of the mind, and the Father of the body. You must recognize that God has sacrificed until today to find such a person.

You who know that today is the end times, where is your heart resting, where is your emotion resting, and where is your body struggling? How was the past, how is today, and how will the future be?

This is the way it is. Unless you have a clear explanation that can be recognized before Heaven and earth, you cannot escape judgment. Since the fall, history has become a painful history of continuous sorrow. In this historical process, what was the ultimate purpose of the ancestors who longed for the world of motivation and purpose, who called out to Heaven while collapsing, who called out to Heaven while being oppressed, and who testified to Heaven while dying? It was to establish the world of motivation and purpose. Many ancestors who died longing for the day of the restoration of the original state have blood flowing in their bodies from the historical prophets and sages who fought for Heaven. You must know that this blood is stained in your hearts and emotions, and you must repay it. Furthermore, you must become a person who can repay even to God.

Let us live solely for God. If one has become such a person, that person cannot exchange themselves for anything. That is why Jesus, after fasting for 40 days, rejected Satan when he offered bread and the world. He refused because he had stepped out saying he did not want anything that anyone might give him, and thus he rejected everything Satan offered on earth. Indeed, he cannot be seen as unqualified for the Messiah. Jesus, who rejected everything the world could offer, who said that this world exists solely for God, and who was filled with the spirit of manhood and the burning passion of hope, could not be denied by Heaven.

You who claim to be members of the Unification Church, if you have made a resolution to fight magnificently for Heaven with courageous spirit, you must not exchange that for anything. Even if someone offers you something that humans like, you must say no; even if they offer you any sovereignty, you must say no; even if they threaten to kill you, you must say no. You must only act according to God's will.

If the end does not come from one, it must go to ten, and if it does not end at ten, it must go to a thousand to break through Satan's stronghold. However, humans do not know this. Thank you for having come to the Unification Church. However, you must abandon your own demands and desires from the day you entered. You must start this work after burying all your desires and demands. This is also true from a providential perspective. Jesus did so, and many prophets, even while shedding blood on the spears of their enemies, gritted their teeth and cried out to Heaven, and you must be able to hear their voices.

Father! Please fulfill your wishes. The determination of those who had such thoughts must pierce your hearts.

God hoped that Adam and Eve would fulfill the blessing to govern all things so that all creation could bow before the heart of love, but they could not even enter that position and destroyed all things. What else could that God be but a God of failure?

God comes to find humanity. He has come and failed, come again and not met, and come again but lost the timing. You know this sad fact. He came to find individuals but lost them and has worked through families as hope.

Since history flows according to principles, how much effort has God made to lose individuals and work through families? He wanted to establish families and bless them, but when that broke, He abandoned families and worked through nations. But when that nation also fell, He established a state. When the state falls, He must establish the world, but until now, there has not been a single time or anything that God could claim as His own.

God sent Jesus before the Israelite nation to establish the world, but by killing Jesus, that nation fell and the world fell into chaos. Therefore, the one who comes to reconnect heaven and earth is the Lord of the Second Advent. Although humanity has fallen, because they received the blessing to govern all things, externally, the entire world has been moving under human governance. However, humans are not made only of body; they also have heart and spirit, so there must be a protagonist who can govern this heart and spirit. He is the protagonist of the ideology we can serve.

No matter how well things are externally, without ideology, they will perish. The external must be connected to ideology. The heart must be connected as a standard that can govern the world. If there is a God who is trying to solve the world's problems, would He not carry out such a plan? He does not do things haphazardly or whimsically. Even if you analyze a single particle, it is not in disorder. Where is there anything that lacks tradition or deviates from cause, content, and purpose?

Our posture to welcome the Lord who will come globally

<Words> The title I wish to speak about today is "The Place Where the Father Wants to Be." I will speak on the title, "The Place Where the Father Wants to Be."

What God longs for and yearns for
We know that there is a place in our hearts that we long for and hope for. The human heart earnestly yearns and hopes for that one place. And we hope that that place will never disappear. Even fallen humanity feels this way, so surely, the God who created the world and humanity and has established His will must have something He longs for and hopes for. It is because of that longing that we can see that God has been governing history for Himself and for humanity.

After creating humanity, if God had a longing in His heart, whom would He long for and hope for? It is not for Himself, nor for any object on this earth, but solely for humanity that He has come forth with longing and hope. We must feel once again at this time that humanity is the one He longs for and hopes for. What is the reason that God has suffered and been in pain because of humanity, and has been betrayed by humanity, yet continues to hold onto humanity? It is because humanity is the one to be longed for and hoped for. We must also feel that God has faced sorrowful turning points and has woven the history of struggle throughout the historical journey.

So why does God long for us and have hope for us, and why must He fight for us? It is because of the fall. It is because of the fall. If humanity had not fallen, God could have lived with the humanity He longs for. In other words, He could have fulfilled His hope for humanity and lived together with them.

However, because humanity fell, God has been fighting with longing and hope for humanity until now. Because humanity is the object of His longing and hope, He has fought through individuals, families, nations, and the world until now.

We must understand that God longs for individuals, families, nations, and ultimately the entire world. We must recognize that God has worked hard to take responsibility for the sorrows of our ancestors whenever they faced sorrow, and to give them new hope instead of sorrow. If there is such a friend on this earth, there can be no friend more precious than that, and if there is such a parent or sibling, there can be no one more deserving of honor.

So, at some point in our life journey, have we ever felt that Heaven longs for us, that Heaven longs for our families, our society, our nation, our people, and this land we live on? How many people have recognized the God who has fought with sorrow and longing? How many families have there been? How many nations and peoples have there been? We can conclude that there have been none.

Humanity has not fulfilled God's longing
God's longing for humanity existed even before the fall. God created Adam and Eve and longed for them to become beings of hope, but they fell. The longing that God had before the fall, the hope He had before the fall, was betrayed by the ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve, and thus God's heart was filled with deep sorrow. We know well that whenever God came to find humanity with that longing and hope, our ancestors did not welcome Him but betrayed Him.

God, suppressing His feelings of sorrow and anger towards the family of Adam, established Cain and Abel to regain His longing, but they only caused God more sorrow. After that, after passing 1600 years, He established Noah, but the outcome was the same. After another 400 years, He established Abraham, and again it was the same. God wanted to meet one person who could share His heart, but Abraham also could not fully welcome God's longing. Thus, even after establishing the family of Jacob over three generations, He could not fully realize His will with that family.

Even after establishing the nation of Israel, we must understand that God had to follow them without being able to openly express or teach His feelings of longing, nor could He govern them.

We must recognize that whenever the nation He longed for fell into misery, God felt the same proportionate suffering and sorrow as His longing. We must consider God's heart when the nation of Israel, following Moses, could not understand His feelings of longing and had to be struck down in the wilderness.

From individuals to families, God's longing to find and establish a nation has grown closer as the time approaches, yet the family era of Jacob did not achieve this. The national era of Moses should have brought them closer to Heaven than the family era, yet it did not; rather, the family era was closer to Heaven, and the individual era was closer to Heaven than the family era. As we approach the end times, humanity scattered across the world should be getting closer to God's longing, yet it is going in the opposite direction. When we think about this, we must understand that Heaven's sorrow is influenced by us and by the environment in which we live.

If we trace history, we find that at any time and in any era, there has not been a person who lived holding onto the words and did not long for a person of goodness who represented Heaven's heart.

Through the long historical journey, God has fought to instill the heart of longing in our hearts, in history, and in the world. Therefore, we must recognize that even in the things we encounter, God's longing is present. We must understand that even in our family members, there is the historical longing of God. God's longing is also present in the nation and the world in which we live.

Thus, when we lift our eyes to behold all creation made by God, we must feel that all creation is the object of Heaven's earnest longing. If all things are so, how much more so is humanity, the crown of creation? Even in our wickedness, when we realize that Heaven has longed for us based on a certain standard, we should truly be grateful before Heaven.

Where God wants to be
So, where does God want to be? Where does Heaven want to be? He wants to be where those He longs for live. Heaven has been governing for six thousand years centered on this earth. It is only natural that the Creator God wants to live on this earth where humanity resides, rather than in the heavenly throne. However, the earth where God wants to live has not been an environment where He can truly reside until now. There are no families, nations, or worlds where God can dwell. When we ask ourselves if we are in a position where God can be present, even as individuals, we must admit that we are not.

What is the purpose for which Heaven has been fighting until now? We know that it is to gather those whom He longs for and to reach a day when He can hold their hands and love them. So where will God be? Jesus did not say that God is in Heaven when He came to this earth. He said that God is within you, and when He introduced the Kingdom of Heaven, He said it is in your heart, in your heart. The problem starts from here.

Where is God's sorrow? Of course, it exists in the world, in nations, in peoples, and in families. However, we must recognize that God's sorrow is present within us. Then where should Heaven's joy be? It should be within us. As long as I do not become a standard, I cannot be someone whom God can long for. God says, "You cannot live without Me." Unless I become such a person, God's new history cannot begin. God longs for such people.

What is God's purpose of creation? It is to establish families centered around a protagonist, and to establish societies, nations, and the world to create a heavenly kingdom on earth. However, there is not a single standard in this world that God can long for. We must clearly understand this.

God's hope for humanity before the fall was for individuals, families, nations, and the world to be able to live through the heart of longing. However, due to the fall of humanity, such a world could not come to be. Therefore, we must understand that God has been holding onto humanity with a heart of longing, struggling through the painful and sorrowful path of the cross to restore this world to the world before the fall.

Do you know that God longs for you, that He wants to hold onto you and live with you beyond the peak of longing? You must not forget this. It is not enough to say, "I know Heaven. I know Jesus. I know the Holy Spirit." Rather, Heaven, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit say, "I know you. You must be able to exist." Is there such a person on this earth? There is not. The purpose of God's providence over six thousand years has been to raise such people, to establish families where such people live, to build churches where such people gather, and to establish nations governed by such people. God desires that such people be the center of the world, singing praises before Heaven. The realization of such a world is God's purpose of creation. However, we must recognize that we have not yet found such nations, such peoples, such families, or such individuals.

The purpose of sending the Messiah
We must understand that God's providential history is to find the longed-for people, the longed-for nation, the longed-for family, and then to find a protagonist who can take responsibility for moving Heaven and earth. The one who comes as that protagonist is the Lord of the Second Advent.

What kind of being will that protagonist be? He is the one who comes to resolve God's longing, and He is a being whom God would not exchange for the entire earth and Heaven. He is the one and only being for God.

If there is a place where we, as humans, wish to go, it will be the place where such a being resides. That place is where there is someone who can love me. It is the place where someone who can overcome all trials, even death, and love me resides. So who is there? There are parents. There is someone who takes responsibility for me, who longs for me, and who strives to find me without caring about death.
missed. Therefore, it is natural for a person to long for the place where their parents are.

Ultimately, the place that humans long for is centered around parents, with spouses, children, and siblings, that is, the place where family is.

Why do we miss our hometown? Because it is a foundation where we can express our feelings and find rest at any time. This is not only true for children. Longing transcends regions and distances, so parents long for their children just as much as children long for their parents. The same goes for couples and siblings. Where does our heart long to be? It longs to be in a place where we can sing about our longing for our father, a place where we can earnestly think of each other, a place where our beloved family is.

When he came to this earth, he said, "I am the only begotten Son of God." Until that time, many saints and sages had come and gone, and countless people had lived, but there had been no son of love who appeared with the heart of God's longing. He was the only begotten Son, who had the pride of being able to receive God's love and be the object of God's longing.

The purpose for which God sent Jesus was to establish a heavenly family that God longs for on this earth. Therefore, without centering on Jesus, one cannot become a member of the heavenly family. This is a principle. The heavenly family is to be formed centered on Jesus alone. What is the purpose of our faith in Jesus? It is not merely to be saved and go to heaven. We must become God's family, which is greater than salvation. What was the purpose of Jesus proclaiming the gospel on this earth? It was to choose and establish the bride of heaven as the Son of God and to form a heavenly family. When a family is formed, it aims to create a nation centered on that family, and a world centered on that nation.

What kind of being was Jesus? He was the only begotten Son of God, whom God had longed for over 4,000 years. How joyful must God's heart have been to see the reality he had longed for? On the day he was born in a stable, the heavenly hosts welcomed him with songs of praise. The wise men from the East worshiped him and brought him gifts, and the shepherds also worshiped him. Why? Because although the place where Jesus lay was a manger, he was at last the son whom God could love after 4,000 years, and that is why they treated him so reverently.

The situation and determination of Jesus in his childhood
God was pleased to see how they treated the baby Jesus, but he was not pleased when he looked at the family of Joseph as Jesus grew. The family of Mary and Joseph should have treated Jesus with the same sincerity as the wise men who worshiped him and brought gifts, but they did not.

As God looked forward to the day when his hopes would be fulfilled, he loved and longed for Jesus even more as he grew. However, while both heaven and people on earth welcomed him at his birth, he did not grow up in such a welcoming environment. After longing for 4,000 years, God had to allow his son to be laid in a difficult and lonely place, and we must understand God's heart in this.

As you know, Jesus was conceived by the Holy Spirit. Therefore, to Joseph, he was a stepson. Even Joseph's brothers mocked Jesus. Neither Joseph nor Mary understood Jesus's purpose. When Jesus was conceived, they accepted the angel's command, saying, "I am the Lord's servant. May your word to me be fulfilled." However, there was a difference in how they treated him when he was born, held him in their arms, and nursed him as he grew. Although it is not recorded in the Bible, Jesus must have experienced immeasurable sorrow. As the Son of God who came to earth, Jesus felt the responsibility to fulfill what God longed for and felt a deep sense of shame before the heavenly Father, having left himself in such a miserable state.

The fact that the Israelite people, whom God had chosen and led for 4,000 years, did not recognize Jesus became God's sorrow. The Israelite people, who longed for God and the Lord, became a people who could not recognize the Jesus they should have longed for, which was the greatest source of infinite sorrow for heaven. When the Jewish people, who claimed to believe in God, opposed the Jesus whom God longed for, God's injustice was immeasurable. Wouldn't it be so?

Jesus grew up surrounded by worries and difficulties. Why? Because his emotional experiences and worldview were different from others. His steps and perspective on the world were different. Living in the household of Joseph, he could not find joy or laughter on any given day. Why? Because he knew what the world, parents, and family should be like. He realized that the household of Joseph was not an ideal family.

Jesus, who knew that what God longed for was a heavenly family, came with the mission and responsibility to establish such a family. He had a steadfast determination to fulfill that mission, even if it meant dying. Therefore, even if his parents betrayed him, even if his nation betrayed him, even if the established Judaism betrayed him, he could not change. Before the God who longed for him, he had to carry the heart of longing, so even when the environment changed and the path ahead was blocked, Jesus walked that path, risking death.

We must understand the heart of Jesus at the moment he was crucified, believing in the blood of the cross. After living for over 30 years, even at the end of his life, which he did not want, his desire to see his Father took precedence. His longing for that Father, his love for him, allowed him to overcome the hill of death.

When we think of the heart of God, who established Jesus as his Son and longed for him, we realize that the purpose for which God set Jesus was to find a heavenly family and to establish a heavenly nation and heavenly world. Therefore, even while carrying the cross, he could say, "Father, do not abandon them." Although the Jews who opposed him personally were enemies, he understood that what heaven desired was this world and humanity, and that this earth was the place that should long for and again long for heaven. After his death, he knew that this world would again be what heaven longed for, and Jesus could pray, "Heavenly Father, forgive their sins."

The family that God longs for
The purpose of God sending Jesus to the earth was to live centered on Jesus. However, on earth, they rejected Jesus and pushed him to death, and Jesus could not fulfill God's desire. Therefore, he had to leave behind the promise that he would come again. Christianity has been coming forth believing in that covenant until today.

Who will the Lord bring when he comes again? He will not come alone. He said he would come in the glory of the Father, so he cannot come alone. He cannot come only as the Son. We must understand that the Lord is one who must bring the Father with him.

Jesus said, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride," so we must form a bride and bridegroom with our heavenly parents. However, today, Christians think that Jesus's love is the end. But the purpose of believing in Jesus and receiving him as the bridegroom is to acknowledge God as our Father. The Father, who created heaven and earth, said that he would create a house where he could dwell. We must become a house where God can dwell.

The place where God wants to be and where Jesus wants to be is not the heavenly throne. Jesus also said he prays. The place of prayer is not a place of rest or a place of the gospel. The reason for prayer is that there are still conditions that need to be resolved. And God must be in a position to receive such prayers. Why? Because the heart of God's longing has not yet been resolved. Jesus, whom he sent to resolve that longing, could not fulfill his mission and could not establish the reality that God longs for on this earth. Therefore, until that is resolved, heaven must receive prayers, and Jesus has the responsibility to pray. Thus, 2,000 years have passed.

Everyone, think calmly. The place where God wants to be, the place where Jesus wants to be, the place where the Holy Spirit wants to be, and even the place where the faithful on this earth want to be—have you prepared such a place? For 6,000 years, God has longed for and hoped for that one place and has fought to achieve it.

To become a person who moves the world, one must long for a global ideology more than anyone else. To be a true protagonist who governs a nation, one must have a heart that longs and loves more than any other people or nation. The same is true in families. For those who long for family, everything about that family comes along with it.

Why do fallen humans cling to God? Because God has a connection that longs for humans. God longs for humans. So where does this longing come from? It arises from humanity's fall. To resolve this longing, a standard that can settle the content of longing must be established on this earth. Therefore, the one who comes to establish this standard is the returning Lord. The time when the returning Lord comes is the time of the return. God, who has longed for his sons and daughters for 6,000 years, must establish a standard on this earth where he can say, "You have formed my family. Now I can live with you forever." Have you ever been to such a place? Since you have not, you must diligently prepare to create that world.

The place that God longs for is not a family in a fallen world, but a family with cosmic ideals and values. A cosmic family is a family where cosmic true parents live. It is a family where cosmic bride and groom live, a family where cosmic sons and daughters live. It is a family where cosmic siblings live.

Our hearts are searching for a place where we can live with God and the Lord. I am the same, and so is Jesus, and so is God. God, who has struggled throughout history to hold onto humanity, is in the same fate as us. Therefore, the purpose is the same.

Jesus spoke the gospel to pave the way for life centered on such a cosmic worldview. What was the purpose of Jesus coming and the purpose of the gospel? It was to establish a heavenly family on this earth where heavenly family members can live joyfully with the Trinity. Therefore, Jesus is the Savior of all people, the Savior. What kind of Savior? The Savior who has a heart that longs to love and care for others.

What kind of family did Jesus want to establish?
Parents who gave birth to me may know how to love only me, but they do not know how to love those next to them. Couples may love each other, but they do not think of revealing that glory before all people and giving that glory back to God. They only love their own children. That is not the original purpose of God's creation.

You must love your parents with the perspective of loving our parents on behalf of all humanity. Only then can God love your parents. Couples must love each other while loving all men and women in heaven and on earth centered on God. When loving children, one must expand the connection of one generation to love universally, not just in a flat manner but in a three-dimensional way.

That is why Jesus said, "Love me more than anyone else." However, humans who live in families have forgotten this perspective of love, but Jesus has loved humanity with such a cosmic heart, which is why he is the Savior. When he set out to find the family that God longed for, when his mother and brothers came to him, he said, "My mother and my brothers are those who do the will of my Father." He even addressed his mother, saying, "Woman, why do you involve me?" It was a position he could rightly take.

Humans who could not establish the family that God desires, who could not fulfill the will of heaven, can they truly enjoy themselves? That is why those who follow the way advocate for a life of celibacy. How can one enjoy themselves when they have not found the family that God longs for? That is why the path with a high standard advocates for a life of celibacy. Why? Because they cannot stand before the heavenly principle. Just the sins of my own existence before heaven cannot be forgiven, so how can I establish the form of family that heaven desires? Heaven cannot forgive that. The order is reversed.

The one who came to bear the mission of establishing the family that heaven truly longs for is Jesus, and after he completely fulfilled that mission and established a family, we must become his sons and daughters.

What kind of family did Jesus want to establish? It is not the kind of family you live in. Absolutely not. Upon examination, it is not so. When you go before heaven, everything divides into the east, west, north, and south. When you die, can you say, "This person is my wife, Father, I brought her with me"? Can you say, "I have children, please send them with me to heaven"? No, you cannot. You can confidently say, "Father, I have the confidence to love those with whom I have a blood relationship on behalf of heaven." However, heaven has never met such sons and daughters, whether male or female. That is God's sorrow.

Jesus came to resolve this issue. He was the one searching for the heavenly family. In this regard, Jesus said, "Foxes have dens and birds have nests, but the Son of Man has no place to lay his head" (Matthew 8:20). No matter how comfortable and nice a place you put him, it is worlds apart from the place that heaven longs for. Even if he sleeps on the street, if heaven is with him there, that place becomes a resting place for Jesus.

The Israelite people, who had been prepared for 4,000 years, saw Jesus come to the earth, and God...
When you establish a family that can work together, if you unite around that family, you would undoubtedly have become a priestly nation. As heavenly kin, as a heavenly family, you would have been able to govern this world. However, when Jesus died, the heavenly kinship was severed. What Jesus left behind in the end was the noun "bride and groom." The bride and groom, true couple. At the same time as being a true couple, Jesus was to restore the original standard that God granted to the first Adam and Eve after 4,000 years, as the true parents. However, because Jesus could not fulfill that purpose due to his death, humanity has been struggling until today.

**The Culmination of Heavenly Principles**
Humanity teaches to love parents, to love spouses, and to love children. Have you ever thought about why you should love your parents? Why should spouses love each other, and why should children be loved? Humans have lost the protagonist who takes responsibility for their love. God has spoken of infinite love. In the end, what remains is love. That love is God's love. You must know the purpose of your longing. There must be a purpose for your love. Who do you love for? It is for God. You must love for God. Those who love for themselves, just try dying and see where you go.

When you give birth to children and nurse them, you may find them adorable, but who do you find adorable for? It is because you should find them adorable on behalf of heaven and earth. You should find them adorable for this nation and this world, for God. The fate of heavenly principles, according to God's love, is moving to embrace the universe beyond the world. However, if you love the sons and daughters born through that connection for your own sake, it cannot be accepted. Mothers who nurse and embrace their children must embrace them with the deep heart of loving God's sons and daughters on behalf of heaven and earth.

The sons and daughters who can live in the Eden that God desires must be beings with universality. Since you are told to govern all things, you must be a being qualified to be a ruler.

Until now, humans have set the purpose of raising their children to ensure their family does well. It has been reversed. Today is the age of reversal. After heaven is good, after the world is good, after the nation is good, and after society is good, then I can be good. This is the original principle, but it has been reversed. It is a claim that it should be good for me first, then for my family, and then for my society. It is being done in reverse.

Heaven looks at this land from that perspective, so it is bringing those humans to end the age of reversal. The path of restoration is the path of striking. Strike your own body. Christianity is on such a path of virtue, so it cannot avoid persecution personally, at home, nationally, and globally. Thus, today, Christianity has become a truly global religion.

Humans teach to establish human principles centered around their families, to be filial to their parents, to care for their spouses, and to love their children. However, heavenly principles encompass a broader scope. Human principles teach centered around oneself, but heavenly principles teach centered around heaven. Love should be given as God loves.

I (heaven) am the protagonist of longing, and this land I long for, this world, must be loved with a heart that can embrace all of this. That is heavenly principle. The culmination of heavenly principles is there. The culmination of human principles is an individual family, but the culmination of heavenly principles is the cosmic family that will appear at the end. Such a family must be established without fail. In such a family, the elevated person is not an individual person. It is a person whom heaven can elevate. Only when that day comes will the grievances of heaven and earth be resolved.

We know the historical tragedies up to now. The family you cherish and live in is the foundation that has given rise to historical tragedies. A family can also be a foundation that can ruin history, while at the same time, it can be a foundation that can fulfill a purpose by reflecting on history. You must understand that the rise and fall of history are influenced by the static foundation of your family.

From here, families have split into two paths: good families standing before human principles and those that are not. The path (do) emerges from this middle ground. That path has not yet fully taken root on this land. It is like living in a side room of someone else's house. Therefore, God cannot freely govern. That is why Jesus came to this land and lived for over 30 years but left as if he were living in a side room. We must understand this historical grievance and resolve it, and we must forgive the sins of the Jewish people who killed Jesus.

**Our Responsibility to Establish a Heavenly Family**
What is the foundation of the affection that heavenly principles want to embrace? It is a heavenly family. The foundation of justice that human principles want to embrace is a human family. Human principles must be moved by heavenly principles; that is why Jesus disregarded the family. However, this does not mean you should disregard your family. That is the principle.

When you raise children in your family, do not think that those children will love you centered around your family. If you are a member of the Unification Church, even when nursing a baby, you should know that the baby should think of heaven and earth. If you trace the connection of those sons and daughters, it connects to God's heart, which planned to create the first Adam and Eve before the fall. Therefore, the sons and daughters you give birth to are beings that will replace historical re-creation. However, you are simply calling them your son and daughter.

Do you know why you value your sons and daughters? It is because you pour all your energy into them and want to love them even while crossing the path of death. It is because they are such great beings. They are beings that have appeared on behalf of heaven and earth. When you look at it this way, where is the place that heaven longs to live? Heaven has longed for a family where it can live with such sons and daughters. You must understand that Jesus has continued to fight against Satan for 2,000 years to establish such a family.

As those who long for such a nation, such protagonists of hope, and such places of hope, what should we do? The era centered around nations has passed, and the era aiming for one world is approaching before our eyes. At this time, where is the foundation where God can embrace and enjoy? There must be a person on this earth who can say, "You are my beloved son or daughter. I will live with you." If that does not happen, there is no heaven or anything else. That is the purpose, so such sons and daughters must emerge.

You must become such sons and daughters, but if you are still caught up in "my son, my daughter, my mother, my father," it is not possible. It is impossible. If you cannot transcend the standard of blood relations of "my father, my mother, my son, my daughter," you will have no connection to the heavenly family that God hopes for and wants to establish. Do you think you can go to heaven after living in such a family environment? Absolutely not. Should everyone be sent to heaven? Even if we are being insulted and persecuted now, even if we collapse while fighting, there is one thing we must embrace, and that is the loyalty we should have as sons and daughters whom God wants to be with and longs for.

Therefore, we members of the Unification Church must know how to elevate our children even when raising them. It is not acceptable to think, "What does it matter if this child is mine or not?" It cannot be that way. If you have hope, that hope is inherited through them. It is connected through children, spouses, parents, or any path. If the hope that remains in humanity is the hope that heaven will establish, it can only be connected through the path of heavenly principles.

You do not want to discuss or work with those whose hearts are not the same, right? If there is an eternal ideological principle, an eternal ideal thought, it is the world that God governs. Do you think you can enter that world just by believing in Jesus? Absolutely not.

To all of you gathered here, if there is a grievance, you must be loyal before heaven. What is the existence of the husband or wife you have lived with until now? They are offerings that represent heaven and earth. They are representative beings to connect heaven and earth vertically, and horizontally, they represent women and men throughout history. Have you felt this? It is an altar where heaven and earth connect and all humanity can harmonize. At some point, the teacher said to love women. The love of this family is a standard that must be upheld eternally throughout the whole. However, there are no sons and daughters born from this standard on this earth. Is there anyone who has been recognized by God as, "Ah, you are my true son, my daughter"? There is none. Because there is none, we must start searching from the beginning. If there are parents, those parents are the representatives of many parents on this earth. Those parents must not only love their own children. They must become people who can love and embrace the children of others in the world with a heart that transcends their own family. The same goes for children loving their parents.

**The Path That Fallen Humanity Must Go Through**
What is the path of virtue? What kind of person will be qualified to be established before God and live in a heavenly family? It is a cosmic person. Leaving other matters aside, it is a person who can serve parents with heart. Have you ever served the true parents who represent heaven and earth? Our parents are the true parents recognized by heaven, earth, and the cosmos. They are true parents whom God, angels, and all of creation on this earth can affirm. Now is the time to welcome the one who has appeared as the true parent.

Who was that person? It was Jesus. He is also the Lord who is to come.

So, who is Jesus? Because Adam and Eve fell in the Garden of Eden, they could not become true parents and became false parents, giving birth to false descendants. He came as the true parent to restore this. Adam and Eve could not become true parents, and since they could not become true couples, they could not become true children. That is why if you completely believe in Jesus and become one with him, you can achieve the restoration of true children, true couples, and true parents. That is why it is said to love Jesus the most. You must understand this.

What is the path that fallen humanity must go through now? They must break through this sorrowful history, shouting hallelujah and amen, and must go through the place of serving the heavenly parents as victorious heroes. After that, they must go through the place where they sing the standard of the cosmic bride and groom, and then they must go through the place of loving cosmic children. This is the three major paths that fallen humanity must go through. National borders are not the issue. East and West are not the issue. If you have heart, everyone will bow their heads before such parents, bless such couples, and bow their heads and care for such children. That time must come. Where is such a place? It is the place where the Lord who is to come will be. The place that such a multitude will go is the heavenly throne in the future. Do you know what the 144,000 multitude is? It is that kind of multitude.

From this perspective, examine the Christian believers. You must know how to love the parents of others more than your own. You must know how to love the children of others more than your own. Why? Because God does so. Is God someone who only loves himself?

If you are a family member who longs for heaven and gathers for heaven, you must have the feeling that you cannot fall apart. You must feel his sorrow as your sorrow and his difficulties as your difficulties. Such emotions must well up in fallen humanity living on this earth. Unless the emotions that can transcend one's own nation, transcend the state, and transcend everything well up in the people of this earth, the garden of peace will not be realized. Furthermore, if such a garden of peace is not realized, even if God exists, that God is a failed being. Moreover, we can conclude that God does not exist.

Even humans on this earth are searching for what they long for, so how much more so is the loving God? What is the reason for the heavenly sorrow that has endured infinite suffering until now without letting go of humanity? It is to live together. What is the purpose of wanting to live together? It is to love. That is why when you enter the place of grace, you will serve your children like parents. When you enter the spiritual realm, you are not bound by anything. Today, humans know God as a stern God, a majestic God, but that is far from the truth. When you face your children, your desire to love them wells up, right? Do you know whose heart that is? It is the heart that God has given. That is how God is.

Although 6,000 years of history have passed since humanity fell, God has not found even one person with whom He can live and whom He can love. God has not yet met such a person. You have loved your children, right? You have lived centered around your family, right? However, that family is a fallen family. No matter how good or whatever it is, it is a family that cannot be blessed before the judgment seat. Therefore, we must create a family that can be blessed. Since I have not become such a person, I must become such a person, and I must create such a family, such a society, and such a world. This is what all Christians around the world must do. However, they are not doing such things and are only seeking their own denomination and church. Do you think that will work?

**The Standard of Loving God with All Your Heart, Soul, and Mind**
A person who can represent God's heart, who can embrace any nation and regard brothers who are not brothers and parents who are not parents as more precious than anything else on this earth, will have no connection to heaven. The Bible says, "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your mind. This is the first and great commandment." (Matthew 22:37) Then, what is the standard of loving God with all your heart, soul, and mind? Does heaven desire the leftover love that humans express? Does heaven want to enter such a place? Absolutely not. What is the extent of giving your all? You must embrace 2.7 billion people and share everything you have with them and still feel insufficient.

You cannot say, "I have done this much, so I have done enough." It is impossible with your body, so you must be able to represent the whole with your heart. The heart can represent heaven and earth and the whole. Isn’t that so? Therefore, if you offer the highest heart, the Father will recognize that you have done enough. Then, what should the standard of that heart be? It should be above the standard of loving your own sons and daughters, above the standard of loving your spouse, above the standard of being filial to your parents, and above the standard of any emotional heart that flows to any being on this earth.
You cannot stand before heaven with your own standards. You must exceed those standards. If humanity had stood before heaven with such standards, God's kingdom would have already been established. Because you cannot love the people of this earth with a heart that is below that standard, Jesus said to love me more than anyone else. You must have a heart that exceeds the love for anyone on this earth. You must be willing to forsake your children for the sake of the way, to give up everything for the way, and ultimately to even give up your own life, and still feel grateful. You must be able to do this. You need to have a heart that exceeds that standard.

In this sense, Jesus spoke those words. Think about it. Who wants to be insulted? Who wants to be persecuted and driven away? However, the world he felt was more important than his nation, and it was a world he had to go to even while being persecuted, which is why Jesus walked that path. Jesus, who carried such a heart, had no friends. If he had any, it was only God. Many saints have come and gone, but only Jesus reached that realm. He appeared as the leader who, for the first time in history, established a connection with the world of heart, which is why Jesus is the Messiah even when viewed from the perspective of heart.

So how will you treat God? God has given His all—His heart, His will, and His character. He has done it all. Look. In front of the multitude of sins deserving of death a million times over, heaven sent many prophets. Yet humanity killed them all. What do you think heaven's heart felt when they died? Heaven felt millions of times more pain than those who died and wept together with the countless saints in heaven. We must recognize that this tragic history has sullied the historical path. We must also understand that every time a good group fell, God had to cross the hill of tears.

The reason why Christians have come to this point today is not because there are people praying on this earth. Absolutely not. Do you think the reason this nation has reached this state is because the people living in this era are doing well? No. It is because there are people who have become fertilizer before heaven without our knowledge that we have even this much left today.

When thinking about this, you must understand the heart that gives its all. God has done all that He can for humanity. He has done it all. Look at how much He has grieved. How much did He grieve while raising Moses and guiding him? How much effort did He put into leading the unworthy nation of Israel? Yet they betrayed Him without even a greeting. They betrayed Him without seeing. We must recognize that our ancestors betrayed Him without any consultation. How sad must heaven be, being in a position where it cannot consult with humanity or receive reports from humanity? Yet, heaven cannot let go of humanity. Why? Because it is in the position of a parent and has the responsibility of having created humanity.

Can you pay the price before the effort God has put in with all His heart, will, and character? No, you cannot. Even if you were to offer your body as a sacrifice and burn it, you could not pay that price. Throughout the providential course until today, many ancestors have become sacrifices, but it is clear that it is not easy to achieve what has not been accomplished.

That is why we must urgently feel that some being who embodies heaven's heart must inevitably appear before humanity. That time has come.

So what should we do? God has come before humanity with all His heart, sincerity, and will, but what should we, who have done nothing, do? All we need is a heart that breaks when we think of our Father and tears that cloud our vision.

If it is the Father's command, we must become those who can say, "I can do anything." Only then can we lift our faces and look upon God, who longs to find us.

In this world, many people lose their minds when their sons and daughters are dying. Heaven has gone through such processes. Therefore, even if heaven loses everything it has in longing, if there is someone who can go toward heaven in longing, that person will not perish. They will absolutely not perish.

God's desire is to find the true family of Eden. However, even if we long for it now, it is a time when we cannot meet. Why? Because the day of judgment will come before the day of promise. That is why God is holding onto humanity and guiding them while looking forward to that day. Heaven has been guiding for six thousand long years, yet it has never seen humanity living in longing.

I am a child of the Father, and I thank Him for blessing us. I say, "Thank you for always being with us," but that is an utterly unjust statement. God has never seen His longing children gathered together and living. That is why, even with the twists and turns in His heart, He has sought His children, looking forward to that one moment when all of heaven and earth can rejoice together centered on those children. This is the history of God's six-thousand-year providence.

Pray. The more you pray, the more tears will cloud your vision. The closer you get to the Father, the more sorrow and weeping will arise. You should be able to dance just by thinking of the Father, but you are not yet able to do so. That is why you are still caught in the historical conditions that God must long for and the conditions of the era. Therefore, you must recognize that the time has come to settle the conditions of longing between heaven and yourself, lacking the conditions of hope. After that, what should you do? You must long for the day when you can be registered as a family member of heaven. In longing, it cannot be just one person longing; all of humanity must long for it. All of humanity must long for it.

You who have gathered here, since you are precious, others are also precious. You have met each other through some connection. That connection is not centered on yourself. We, who have met through some connection, must not remain here today. We must expand this connection and connect it to the world, fulfilling what God longs for, and connecting it to the standard where God can live with this world. That responsibility lies with us. For that reason, you must not live for yourselves. Now is the time to live for the world and for God. It is not the time to live for yourselves.

What God desires is the true family of Eden that has been lost. You must understand that the true parents who can be established in that family, the true couples who can stand before the true parents, and the true children who can love in that true couple are the heavenly family that God wishes to have. When such a family appears, then Jesus will also be able to enjoy it like a brother. Such a family must appear.

That is why we are going toward such a place. Therefore, each of you must reflect on whether you have given your all for your nation, the world, and the heart of heaven. Have you given your all? This is the biggest question. Heaven has done so. Those who love heaven more than their children, more than themselves, will go to heaven. Do you know what that was meant to show? Father, have mercy on us. Let it be so. We know that the place where the heart connects is a place that the Father cannot place Himself, so may our circumstances and the Father’s circumstances intertwine. We earnestly hope and desire this.

The Father is the historical Father, and at the same time, He is my actual Father, the Father who is with me in my life, and the Father who is inseparable from my ideals and my life. At this time, may our hearts and bodies be transformed so that we can approach such a Father, and may He appear as such a Father. We earnestly hope and desire this time to be one where we can deepen the connection to share the word in order to strengthen the bond of heart with the Father.

To do this, may we be allowed to give up everything we have held onto until now. Whether it be wealth, position, honor, or anything to boast about, none of these can be offered as victorious conditions before heaven, so let us reject them and prepare a true heart of beauty and a true heart of goodness to serve the Father in this one hour.

May we once again feel the nature and heart of the Father through true beauty and love, bowing our heads before that heart and glorifying the Father centered around that heart, and may this time be one where we can receive new words. 

Have mercy on this sleeping nation. There are loving sons and daughters who are enduring and fighting even in lonely and weary places, so may You be with them. Moreover, we know that there are many sons and daughters who are building hidden altars, worrying without knowing the time, and appealing before heaven, so may You mobilize such sons and daughters to quickly welcome the day of victory, the day of glory, the day when we can judge Satan.

Father, please be with us at this time, and may You be with the words we wish to convey. We have heard many words through people. We have heard many words connected to people, but we do not desire such words; Father, please appear Yourself.

Life is from the Father, true words of truth are from the Father, and the gifts of glory are also from the Father. Therefore, do not accept anything that is not centered on the Father, and adjust our bodies, hearts, and the entire atmosphere with the gifts that come from the Father, so that it may not become a time for Satan to take advantage. We earnestly hope and desire this.

May the heart of the one who conveys and the heart of the one who receives become one in the same heart. If there are those who cannot respond to that heart, grant them a heart to repent of their own sins. At this time, may everything be under the Father’s guidance, and may we be recognized as victorious and glorious sons and daughters who can be embraced by the Father. We earnestly request that the remaining time also be under the Father’s guidance, and we pray in the name of the Lord. Amen.

<Word> The title I wish to speak to you today is "Who understood the heart of heaven?" 

Looking at the heart of God toward fallen humanity

Before creating all things, God already had a heart that desired to create. That heart was the ideal of creation, and to realize it, God set a plan for creation and began to create all things.

God’s desire was for a world of creation ideals where His heart could resonate, a person of creation ideals, and all things of creation ideals. However, the fact that such an ideal world, ideal person, and ideal things do not exist is God’s sorrow.

Why has this happened? As you know, it is because of the fall. The beings that were meant to move eternally centered on God’s heart and along with the ideal of creation have been unable to find the origin of goodness and have moved separately from heaven and humanity, heaven and creation until today. Originally, all things and humans have a connection that has passed through God’s hands and are inseparable from the object of God’s heart, but today, God’s hand cannot remain on our bodies or on all things, and God’s heart cannot remain on all things or on our individual selves. We must understand that this lamentable situation has arisen as a result of the fall.

From the day God looked upon fallen humanity, He could not help but see the fallen world, and from the day He faced fallen humanity, the ideal world He had longed for had to hide deep within His heart. Although there was an ideal, He could not realize it, and whenever He faced all things, His desire to fulfill that ideal moved, but heaven could not express that desire. We must understand that God, who created all things, could not love the children He should love. Therefore, heaven, which looks upon this earth, is not a heaven of joy. It is a heaven that must feel the sorrow of sorrows, a heaven that must feel the pain of pains.

God, who originally created humanity to have the justification of being His direct children, could not abandon that connection and began the history of restoration, that is, the history of salvation and re-creation. In the historical process of seeking the lost, God has gone through much sorrow, and you must understand that there has not been a single person who could sympathize with that sorrowful heart of God. In the midst of this, heaven has come out following fallen humanity with a sorrowful heart. Heaven could not stand in front but followed behind. Just like a parent of a death row inmate follows their child to the execution ground, God has followed humanity, which is being dragged by the hand of death, like a universal death row inmate.

We must understand that whenever God places humanity, which should be governed and loved freely, in a position to be trampled upon and torn apart by Satan, He feels infinite pain. When placing an individual in such a position, He must feel the personal pain of the cross, and when placing a family, nation, or even a country in such a position, heaven must feel the corresponding pain of the cross. We must keep this in mind.

God's heart and hope for humanity

So why has God found Himself in such a situation? It is because humanity has fallen. Who is God? He is the true ancestor of humanity. He is a Father who is inseparable from us and is connected to our entire essence. Humanity does not know that this Father is in such a situation. Heaven is hoping and longing for the day when humanity will destroy this position and be able to call Him Father again. Those who have come out to pave the way of the truth in order to know heaven and follow the direction in which heaven moves are also longing for that day.

Thus, that day is the day the Father has been longing for, and it is also the day the sons and daughters are longing for. That day is when the lost son breaks the chains of death and returns in a liberated form to call upon the Father. It is the day when, as true sons and daughters who were created in the original garden, they can call upon the Father they have longed for with their original heart. You must clearly understand that this day is the day humanity longs for and the day God longs for.

With this heart, heaven has faced the historical process. Even when dealing with the most sinful of sinners, that heart has not disappeared, and even when facing dying sons and daughters, that heart has not disappeared. Moreover, even in the places where countless seekers have lamented and sought the direction of goodness, God has not left. From one sinner to a life that cries out for goodness and righteousness, regardless of the environment or era, heaven has faced humanity with the same heart.

That good God, who loves us so much, even though humanity is trapped in sin, still feels, "My son, my daughter."
has been lamenting until now. The reason for Heaven's lamentation lies in the fact that humans, who should share the origin of heart and live alongside Heaven, governing all things together, have failed to do so. This world is one that is formed by evil, intertwined with the circumstances of evil and the heart of evil, not one that is formed by good, intertwined with the circumstances of good and the heart of good.

For this reason, anyone with a clear conscience who aims for good will feel a sense of dislike for this world. This is because this world is in contradiction to their original heart. Given that the world is like this, Heaven is working behind the scenes through historical processes to establish a path and draw humanity along. Among these, Christianity is a representative example.

Everything that humanity feels, sees, and senses is not from God. We must thoroughly recognize this. It is not because of God that we do things. What I like comes from whom? It comes from Satan. How many people know this?

What kind of people should humanity become? They must realize that everything they immediately like and enjoy is not based on the good God, our Father, but is instead achieved on the stage of Satan, and they must break away from that joyful scene and move forward. To a new place. A world that moves in connection with God, not this world that moves in connection with Satan. That is the world that humanity desires.

You have lived freely until now. Until now, you have pointed out what is good and what is bad, but you must clearly understand that everything you consider good has not originated from Heaven. Instead, it can be a material that could make God sad. Before becoming someone who opposes and strikes out against this, you cannot return to the original world.
