It may be yours, but it has become the enemy's. Originally, it was yours, but it has been taken away by the enemy. A group that is filled with the feeling of lamentation and cries out must emerge on this Earth. 

Until such a group emerges, there will be no way to resolve the historical resentment, and before the resentment of history is resolved, there can be no connection with God's heart of love, which can fulfill hope, love, and ideals. That is why it is said that the world will face a great judgment. After the anger is resolved, the world of the heart that was hoped for will be established. That is the kingdom of heaven on Earth.

Look at Noah, who was central to God's providence. It was not only Cain who betrayed God. Heaven did not mind establishing Noah 1,600 years after Cain and working hard. Noah, who came before Heaven, also did not mind working in accordance with Heaven's will. However, while God knew Noah, Noah did not know God's true heart. Just as God knew Abel and Cain, but Abel and Cain did not know God's heart, Noah also did not know God's heart. Furthermore, the people of that time did not understand Noah's heart, which was for God.

You must understand this. God knew Noah well. Knowing him well, God hoped that when Noah would fulfill God's resentment on behalf of God's heart, He would treat Noah as a son of joy. If there is a blessing, where could there be a greater blessing? If there is glory, where could there be greater glory? God looked at Noah with such a heart, but Noah did not know that heart of God.

In the providential history of restoration, God has repeatedly experienced such things. You must understand how pitiful Noah was, who followed without knowing. You must also understand how pitiful God was, who held onto Noah even when Noah did not know. Noah was struggling to live for God's will without knowing. Heaven hoped that Noah would understand His heart, but Noah did not know that situation. Noah's heart was anxious for not knowing, and God's heart was even more anxious. Not only did Noah not know God, but Noah's family, who moved with him, also did not know Noah. We must clearly understand how great God's suffering was in holding onto these ignorant children.

After Noah worked hard for 120 years, God executed the flood judgment, and what remained afterward was Noah's eight family members. What did Heaven hope for from there? It was to enjoy having God as their Father as a family of Heaven, untainted by corruption, but Noah himself did not clearly understand that. He did not realize that he was called to restore the qualifications of the original Adam and to indemnify the resentment bound to the Adamic family. It is bearable when others do not recognize you, but it is heartbreaking when family members, who should rejoice and grieve together, do not recognize you. This was Heaven's sorrow.

Because of this, Heaven's history was prolonged. It was not prolonged because the people of the world did not recognize it. It was prolonged because the group that should have recognized it did not. Ham did this before Noah, the people did this before Moses, and the apostles did this before Jesus. History has come down like this. The group that was called to be nurtured and fed, hoping for recognition, did not recognize it, and because of this, Heaven's will was broken and torn down.

God's providence and lessons through Abraham's family
When God called Abraham and told him to leave Ur of the Chaldeans, Abraham responded to Heaven's call and left. He abandoned his hometown. Why? Because that was not the world where Abraham could live. This world is one that should be resented, one that should be cursed. No matter how much loving parents and relatives live there, that land is not a place for Heaven's people, so God drove Abraham into the lonely wilderness.

"Leave Ur of the Chaldeans," He said.

Abraham set off unconditionally, not knowing the content of the sinful world he was leaving behind. When he offered sacrifices to God, he did so without knowing the meaning of the offerings. When he was told to sacrifice Isaac, he obeyed unconditionally without understanding the command's significance. We must understand that this is the history of our ancestors who came out in accordance with Heaven's will from a position of ignorance. Those who took responsibility did so without knowing, but they honored and valued Heaven. Few families understood this.

From Abraham to Isaac and then to Jacob, what was Jacob's purpose when he returned with his twelve sons from Laban's house? It was to establish the foundation of a heavenly family in that generation. Jacob, who longed for Heaven's blessing, even deceived his brother, but his sons did not recognize such a father. They were jealous of Jacob's beloved Joseph and Benjamin. This became the origin and condition that motivated the division of the twelve tribes of Israel into ten tribes and two tribes.

In this way, those who took responsibility in the historical process recognized the preciousness of Heaven's will and moved accordingly, but because the family that should have recognized that responsible person did not, they ruined Heaven's history.

Who is the enemy? It is not outside the door. Jesus said, "Your household members are your enemies." This means that those who cannot believe, those who betray, and those who act in positions unrelated to Heaven are the enemies.

God led forth ancestors like Noah, Abraham, and Jacob, who followed without knowing. Heaven hoped that those who did not know would recognize the earnest circumstances. Why did He set up such ancestors as leaders? You have learned the principles well. However, our ancestors did not know this. Even though they followed without knowing, when they betrayed before Heaven's will, they were struck down. There was no way to forgive them.

The providence centered around Moses and the Israelite nation
The same was true in the time of Moses, after the time of Jacob. Moses did not even know God's heart, which was to establish him as the future leader of Israel. He did not understand why he was sent to grow up in the luxurious environment of the enemy's palace.

However, Moses, who did not lose his national spirit, built up the conviction that the more luxurious the glory placed before him, the more it was not the world he was meant to live in. Abraham stood before Heaven with such conviction, and so did Noah and Jacob. Moses was in that position as well. No matter how luxurious the palace of Pharaoh was, he firmly believed it was the palace of the enemy. Moses, who lived in Pharaoh's palace for forty years, never had a happy day. When he saw his people in despair, he wanted to save his people, even if it meant dying or being torn apart, and he was filled with the heart to die for his people, which led him to jump into action for the Israelite nation.

Who understood Moses' integrity? At that time, who among the Israelite nation knew that Moses had a heart that loved the Israelite nation? If at that time the Israelite nation had united with Moses, who had such a determination to defend Heaven and save the chosen people, Heaven's history would not have been prolonged.

However, when Moses appeared before the Israelite nation and spoke of a new conviction and a new purpose, the Israelite nation was one that constantly betrayed him. When he saw these people fighting among themselves, Moses' sense of justice burned. They should have united to fight against the enemy, yet they did not know this and fought among themselves, which made him feel sorrowful. In a moment of burning national sentiment, when he saw an Egyptian fighting with an Israelite, Moses struck down the Egyptian on the spot. If the entire Israelite nation had united with Moses at that time, God's providence would have begun then. There would have been no forty-year extension. Moses, who had to lead the nation, had to walk the path of extension in the wilderness of Midian for forty years due to the betrayal of his people. Moses, who suffered various hardships in Pharaoh's palace while leading the Israelite nation into the wilderness, and the Israelite nation that followed him were all pitiful people.

The central content of God's providence and the gospel centered on Jesus

The ancestors of faith who came and went over 4,000 years believed in God without knowing, and followed with hope for heaven without knowing, but Jesus came to lead them, even while being pushed aside, to convey heaven's heart before the pitiful chosen people of Israel. How frustrated and sorrowful must heaven have been during these 4,000 years while guiding those who did not know? Heaven prepared for thousands of years for the Messiah to come before the ignorant nation of Israel, indicating that they would understand heaven's heart on the day he arrives, and thus the nation was hoping for the Messiah without knowing. Yet, such a nation denied the Messiah. If the people of Israel had not hoped for the Messiah, they would not have faced judgment.

The sons and daughters God seeks

God is searching. He is crying out, having established the laws of heaven. He is looking for those who can be called my sons from birth. He is looking for sons who can be called my sons while living. When that emerges, you will abandon your brothers and go there, abandon your parents and go there, abandon your nation and go there, abandon the world and go there. That is not a logical personality, not a personality that is conceived and imagined. It is a natural, automatic personality that can communicate with heavenly principles. When a heartistic personality that can automatically govern all human feelings moves with heavenly feelings, the world will unite quietly without any effort. Heaven is longing for such a day.

To stimulate such a thing, what must be done? The sons and daughters whom God embraced and loved before the fall must emerge on this earth. They must destroy Satan and appear in a garden of happiness where there is no slander from Satan or invasion of evil, where there is no fear or anxiety, a garden of eternal peace and eternal freedom, where no one can say anything about how and where to embrace and love. Only then will the world unite in an instant. Every time I think of such things, I cannot help but say, "Father, how much have You longed for this?"

Our responsibility to welcome a new day
This longing heart is the heart that the Father has longed for since before the creation of the world. Is that not so? It is the heart that longed before Adam and Eve were born, the heart that existed before all things were created. He created heaven and earth to fill that heart. However, God is infinitely pitiful. He is in the position of having to embrace the children of sin, having to call them beloved sons, and He is the God who comes to this earth where sinful sons and daughters live, being torn, wounded, and oppressed. You must think about this.

God's heart is being torn. God is weeping. There are wounds in God's heart that are torn apart. Every time a nation falls and a new nation is formed, you must understand that the twists and turns of God's heart are permeated in every page of history.

Because God has come out with such a heart in the history of the fall, you must be emotionally united with God, who has such a traditional heart. To do so, you must know the God who has been infinitely sad, the God who has been infinitely tormented. You must know the God who has been infinitely indignant and wronged. Then, for whom is God doing this? For humanity, for us, for this world. Therefore, we who live on this earth must relieve God's sorrow. We must carry on the history of sorrow that does not end until God's sorrow and pain end.

If you understand that, you must become sons and daughters who can say, "Father, please let me bear Your sorrow." You must be able to do this. If He does not want to give it, you must take it away and bear it. You must become sons and daughters who bear God's sorrow, even if you have to take it away. You must be able to say that the Father's pain is my pain, and the Father's indignation is my indignation. However, how many such sons and daughters are there? Those who believe in Jesus and say they will go to heaven? Those who believe in Jesus and say they will be comfortable? Such people are traitors to heaven. You must do everything to go to heaven. You must do everything to be blessed. Do you want to go to heaven and be blessed without doing what you must do? Such people are robbers. You must understand this.

Now you must become the prince who inherits God's sorrow. Jesus was such a prince. He became the Savior because He was the prince who alone inherited death. Although He fell into death, He rose again with the authority of resurrection, becoming a prince who can dominate the authority of death. Jesus shed many hidden tears. Friends, this is recorded only a few times in the Bible. You must understand that my tears, blood, and emotions are all imbued with Jesus's feelings. Only those who have wept with Jesus, who have suffered with Jesus, who have melted their hearts with Jesus, can be accepted. You have come to the Unification Church, but you cannot have the habitual faith of the past. The faith of the Unification Church is fundamentally different from such faith.

Who is the one that Satan fears the most?
Who is the one that Satan fears the most? It is the one who, combining spirit and flesh, says they will bear the cross that God has given. Those who wish to receive God's love are regarded as foolish by Satan.

The one who says, "God, I will bear Your cross," is the one whom Satan fears the most. When you say, "God, I am being wronged," Satan will flee.

For this reason, there will surely be tribulations for the saints of the end times. All the traces of anguish, betrayal, rejection, oppression, death, and the bloody history that God has endured will sweep over you. However, who can dominate the heart that says, "Not my will, but Your will be done, Father"? Who can sever the emotional bond between the Father and me? Is it the authority of Satan? Not at all. The authority of death cannot do that either. What can dominate this heart? Only those who have the standard to endure any difficulties in the journey of seeking this can surpass the final judgment seat. Only such beings can welcome the new day that God is searching for and that humanity is searching for.

Love and absolute goodness are eternal. The beginning and the end are the same. However, those who receive grace from the Father, rejoice, dance, and make vows, and then change at some moment are on Satan's side. We must ask, who can occupy this heart that is emotionally united with the Father? Let the authority of death from the world of Satan come, let the twists and turns of blood from the world of Satan come, let everything from the world of Satan come, let the fears of the end times and the seven-year tribulation all come at once. I will not be conquered. Such things cannot conquer me. You must have the standard to call upon the Father emotionally.

Then, Father, who has fought for this purpose in the world of death, have You met such sons and daughters on any given day to be comforted? O God, who has not been comforted! Today, I will comfort You. You must be able to do this. Such a person can become a son or daughter of God in the new era, a rightful heir to inherit the world.
will take place, and it will take place within myself. Allow us to understand that such events are happening and that the time of the great war after creation is the time of judgment.

Today, believers on this land know that on the day of judgment, fire will come down from heaven to consume this earth, but we know that it is not so. Allow us to understand that the distinction between death and life is made based on the currents of this world, and that the true state of the church, family, ideologies, and the tangled realities of this world will be judged there. Allow us to understand that only those who can cast away the authority of death and possess the authority of life can look forward to a new day, a new era, a new world, and a new heaven.

As I mentioned today, we have been called for a new day. Everything I live for today must pass away. Parents will pass away. Spouses will pass away. All the honor and power I possess, everything precious to me, will also pass away. What must remain? Even if we are tormented again and again before the authority of death, let us understand that what remains is the heart connected between the Father and the Son.

We have come to know that where this remains, all of humanity can live. Even if I fall, let us understand that it remains. Father, please allow the roots of life to be deeply planted in this universe where death is deeply rooted, so that it may become a foundation from which life can infinitely spring forth.

Father, we have been called for this purpose. We are persecuted for this. On the emotional journey of following in the footsteps of the Father, which brother would not be precious? While there may be distances near and far, the heart that desires to face the Father is an ideological impulse that moves with history, with the times, and with the future. If we cannot cry out from the standard of a global heart today, allow us to cry out from the standard of a national heart, and if we cannot cry out from the national standard, allow us to cry out from the standards of this society, this nation, and our families. If we cannot cry out from the familial standard, allow us to cry out from my own standard. We earnestly hope and desire to be able to be established as members of the heavenly family in this way.

Jesus was a pitiful figure. He came to this earth as the prince of the battle against Satan and as the prince of judgment. Father, we have come to know what you desire after you have conducted the final judgment and established the names of the bride and groom, so please grant us the ideology that allows us to stand as sons and daughters who could embrace and love in the original Eden without fall.

Just knowing this fact, Father, we are grateful. In the midst of what others do not know, we can long for such a heart, we can shed tears that others do not shed, and we can think of matters that others do not think about, so even if we have not reached that place, how can we not be grateful?

If our hearts are yours and our bodies are yours, please allow the country we live in to be yours, and allow this world to be yours. This world is a part of the creation you made, so we earnestly hope and desire for it to be yours.

Today, may their bodies and hearts be energized to long for a new day emotionally, and may the suffering of the world of Satan appear. "What do you have to boast about, authority of death? What do you have to boast about?" May we be able to separate from them and unite with the Father, singing songs of joy, and please grant us an hour before them to ensure that we can meet that day.

Thus, as not just adopted sons but as true sons, may we be embraced in the eternal love of the Father, receiving heaven and earth as our inheritance, and may we become beings who can return it to God with joy. We earnestly hope and desire this, and we pray all these things in your name. Amen.

14)
Heaven belongs to those who serve with heart
Matthew 22:34-40
<Prayer> Father, at this time we stand before your presence. We have revealed ourselves before your glorious presence, so please expose our shortcomings and make this time one where we are captured in your light, and grant us the glorious grace to call you Father. Among the many forms of fathers that humans may call, we wish to call you, Father! with a heart and spirit that resonate deeply. We hope to be those who know the heart of the Father before calling any name. Please allow us to become such people.

Since heaven and earth and humanity came into being, we have come to understand that there has been no true sons and daughters that God wishes to love on behalf of heaven, earth, and humanity. Adam and Eve, who were the true people and true parents of humanity, were the protagonists who could enjoy and harmonize with all creation. How much have you longed for an hour when such sons and daughters could stroke your hands and touch your face?

Father, you have created our hands to be exceedingly holy, and our bodies to be exceedingly good, but from the day the unfortunate nature of the fall captured us, our hands have been wounded by Satan. Our bodies have become full of scars. Because of the shortcomings of our historical ancestors, we bear scars all over our bodies, so Father, even if we cannot show you our unfaithful selves before you, please allow us to be those who can empathize with your painful heart that longs for us and can weep bitterly before you. May we become those who long for the original hands that were not wounded, who long for the original bodies that were not wounded, who long for the original hearts that were not stained by sin, and who long for the original hearts that were not connected with Satan.

There is no true person as you created, Father, on this earth. How much do you grieve? Please allow us to realize at this time that we must not become children who do not know where to turn before the Father who grieves at the sight of us with wounds. We, who have gathered here, have come to see the original person who resonates with heart, and we have come longing for your heart that blooms within us, so please allow this time to be one where we can find that purpose, beloved Father, we earnestly hope and desire this.

Father, we are grateful. How much have you labored to raise your children, to care for them, and to pave the lonely path? Father, knowing your circumstances today, we cannot help but weep.

Father, please allow us to repent for our past unfaithfulness, and let us lament our many shortcomings that prevent us from standing before you, so that in this hour we can embrace you with a new heart, and may we be sons and daughters who can mourn in our hearts for not being able to stand as one aspect of the desire you long for.

At this time, countless people are praising your holy name, and your sons and daughters are shedding tears in lonely places, thinking of lonely brothers and worrying about them, so please embrace them with the same love and bless them.

Now, what shall I speak? I have already spoken a lot. You know these things very well. However, let us not just be those who know, but let us be those who can go beyond knowing and become one with the heart.

Please allow the heart of the one who delivers the message and the heart of the one who receives it to become completely one. We know that Satan operates in places of separation, so let us lay down all our claims and all the knowledge we have held before you, and return to the original heart, harmonizing with the movements of heaven, moving according to your commands, and let this hour be one where we can be reshaped based on the original body.

We earnestly hope and desire that you hold all things in your hands and do not let Satan find a foothold. We ask that the Holy Trinity establish a foundation of glory as a shield of victory, and we pray this in your name. Amen.
<Words> Today, I will speak on the topic, "Heaven belongs to those who serve with heart."

Heaven and Fallen Humanity
You may know that one cannot enter heaven without going through the heart. Heaven is the original nation that can govern the whole, the nation of original nature. That nation cannot be possessed with any circumstances. It is a nation that can only be possessed by having a deeply ingrained connection of heart. Therefore, Christianity is ultimately not a church that deals with circumstances, but a church that deals with heart. There is a purpose of heaven that governs the earth to lay the foundation for singing the heart beyond the connection of circumstances.

What is the fall? It is not being unable to discuss God's circumstances, but rather being unable to discuss the heart. God, who comes to find fallen humanity, has the heart to deal with lost sons and daughters, but because there is no one to share that heart with, He works to find and establish those people. This is the work of salvation, and you must clearly understand that the one who is sent to find and establish those people is the Savior.

Before we hope for heaven, we must look at God's heart, and before looking at God's heart, we must think about how we should live our own lives. You must first have a heart that serves. It is human nature to bow our heads and long for that which is high and precious. Even though we humans have fallen, we still want to serve the high and precious heart of heaven; this is the original heart of the humans we were created to be. Therefore, you must clearly understand that those who have not experienced a life of serving through heart have no connection with heaven.

However, to serve, one must be prepared to serve. After going through the process of preparation, a life of serving is necessary. Only after going through the process of preparation to serve and the life of serving can one go to heaven. Heaven is where those who have served with heart go. The world that praises and elevates the preparation for serving and the life of serving is heaven. You must clearly understand this. We are destined to go through the process toward this world of purpose.

Since the day we received the bloodline of the fall until today, has there been a day when all humanity has served heaven with their hearts? There has not been. Our ancestors, Adam and Eve, who were not fallen, grew through the ideal of creation, but they never had the time to serve God while establishing a connection of heart.

What is God's lament? It is that humanity, who should serve God centered on heart, has fallen to a place where they cannot serve, and that God, who should receive service centered on heart, cannot receive it. It is not that there are no believers; it is not that there are no people who know God. The lament of heaven and earth is that there is no one who can serve God and deal with God through heart, and you must clearly understand this.

Fallen humanity is seeking to move forward. What are they seeking? They are seeking heaven. However, is there anyone who feels the profound joy that this is the heaven where I can live forever, the land where my heart can dwell forever, and the stage of my life? Not a single person exists.

The Hope of God and Humanity Seen Through the Feast of the Lamb
Even the Savior Jesus, whom we believe in, came to this earth and could not serve God in an environment where he could connect through heart. All creation was created so that the sons and daughters of God could feel the joy of heart and enter into harmony with the Lord. However, due to the fall of humanity, they could not establish that connection in such a place. We must understand that the Messiah, who came to create an environment where heart could be connected on this earth, also left without having experienced a life of serving heaven.

Jesus said that he is the bridegroom and we are the bride. Furthermore, God is the Father and we are the children. What is the foundation of the connection of heart? It is the connection of parent and child, and the connection of husband and wife. Based on this, the connection of siblings and compatriots is established. This is how it unfolds.

Then, what kind of existence should the world of humanity establish before God, who created heaven and earth? What kind of person should God establish on this earth as He carries out the providence of restoration? We must establish a foundation of heart that can connect horizontally with the world and vertically with God, a foundation that can connect horizontally with reality and vertically with the past and future, and within that, we must establish true sons and daughters, true bride and groom. Therefore, we must understand that heaven desires to have one son and daughter, one family, who serve God in a place where hearts are connected.

Jesus prophesied that the end day would be both a joyful day and a sorrowful day. For those whose hearts are connected, it is a day to receive gifts of joy, while for those whose hearts are not connected, it is a day to receive gifts of sorrow.

Jesus said he would come as the bridegroom. The Feast of the Lamb refers to the meeting of the bride and groom. God's providence began for that one day. The believers who follow the purpose of providence are also fighting for that one day. What is the sole purpose of living a life of faith according to the purpose and will of providence? It is to meet that moment when the connection between heaven and humanity and between humanity and all creation, which was severed, is re-established centered on the sons and daughters who can deal with God's heart.

We are looking forward to serving. Whom do we wish to serve? We wish to serve the coming Lord, and furthermore, we wish to serve the Father whom the Lord serves. This is the hope of humanity. Salvation must also pass through this standard.

Preparation to Serve the Bridegroom and the Offering
Thus, the history until now has been a history of preparation for that one day when we will serve the Lord. Longing for the coming Lord is also preparation to understand the content that can be served, and we must understand that it is preparation for that day when we can understand the heavenly will that longs for us and live with Him.

Christianity has been preparing for 2,000 years. It has been preparing to live a life of serving as a bride. So, what kind of preparation should we make? It is not the preparation of words, nor the preparation of faith, nor the preparation of life. It is the preparation that can connect through heart.

Longing for the bridegroom who has been coming for 2,000 years, you must understand the heart of the bridegroom.
It must be. Have you ever felt the longing of heaven to welcome me as a bride, and the immense effort and yearning of heaven to establish me as a bride? Even if I may seem to be a shabby and insignificant being on the outside, heaven yearns and longs for me. It is not a pretense, but truly, with a genuine heart, heaven comes forth to long for us in a way that is not formal or superficial. Therefore, we must understand that the providential history of heaven up to today is connected with the heart of longing.

Before we prepare to welcome the bridegroom, we must recognize that heaven has prepared countless times for us. Before we prepare, heaven has first prepared for us. Those of you who wish to welcome the bridegroom must reflect on whether you are preparing with a heart that longs deeply. The Lord we long for, the Lord who is so deeply missed, how should our attitude be as we prepare for that one day to welcome Him? You must think about what the attitude of today's Christian believers should be.

The more earnest your desire to meet the Lord, the more the heart of longing towards heaven should come upon you. Rather than looking forward to welcoming the Lord who is coming, you should become someone who can look back and weep for the Lord who is preparing us and coming forth. For 6,000 years, heaven has struggled and toiled to find and establish me, fighting against Satan for 6,000 years, enduring the accusations of the wicked Satan for 6,000 years, and for 6,000 years, there has not been a single day in which heaven has not experienced sorrow. While carrying such a sorrowful heart, heaven seeks and longs for us, who are nothing, to be established as warriors of heart.

What offerings have you prepared to stand before such a heaven? What offerings have the Christian believers, who have remained after 6,000 years of providence, prepared? What have you equipped yourselves with? Heaven is yearning. It does not desire any valuable gold, silver, or jewels in this world, but rather seeks those who possess a heart, a heart that encompasses everything and loves while living alongside heaven.

If you have become someone who prepares with such a heart, what should your eyes, ears, mouth, and body be like? You must see through the heart, hear through the heart, speak through the heart, and act through the heart. You must live with a connection through the heart. You should have eyes that can see the Lord and serve Him, ears that can enjoy with the Lord, and you should long for that moment when you can speak and act through the heart. For 6,000 years, heaven has come forth seeking such individuals.

Do your eyes, ears, mouth, and body have a connection with heaven through the heart? These eyes should see all things through the connection of the heart, these ears should hear the cries of the heart, this mouth should speak words that can connect through the heart, and this body should live a life that can connect through the heart. Yet, we are still in the preparatory stage before moving to the position of serving. Therefore, we cannot help but think about how much of a heart preparation we have made.

Heaven desires to have everything be intertwined through a single touch that can connect through the heart. Heaven wishes for all sons and daughters to be embraced through children who can connect through the heart. Heaven hopes for God's sovereignty to be fulfilled through brides who can connect through the heart. Heaven anticipates that this world will be governed by sons and daughters who can connect through the heart. Have you thought about this? The more you think about it, the more immense it becomes.

When you consider that God's wish is not only for my own self but is connected to the world and the universe, I cannot deny that I belong to the Lord and to the Father. Therefore, my heart is the Father's, my feelings are the Father's, and my entire consciousness, intuition, and senses must also belong to the Father. The understanding that everything I feel and perceive is the Father's, which can connect through the heart, must be established. Unless this happens, you must clearly understand that you cannot possess the heaven that moves through the heart.

When you think about this, dear ones, we must long for it. We must seek it out. We must know this fact and strive with all our might to fulfill heaven's wish. No matter how terrifying the path of death may be, we must become individuals who can overcome it with a strong heart that can laugh and move forward.

Where did the strength that allowed Jesus to overcome the brink of death come from? What was the center of that strength? You must understand that it was solely from the heart. Jesus, who inherited the history of heart prepared over 4,000 years, lived for over 30 years, crying out from the depths of His heart, "Oh, let the history of 4,000 years go by, and let the day of hope to serve God come!" He also sought and searched. He searched for the bride who had prepared with all her heart for 4,000 years.

What was the sorrow of heaven that established and prepared the chosen people of Israel? It was not that there were no sects, nor was it that there were no Pharisees or Sadducees. (Recording paused) Where did the bride prepared for the pitiful Jesus go after 4,000 years? She was not there. This is where the historical sorrow of humanity originates. There was no bride who could connect through the heart with Jesus. Even when He sweated, there was no handkerchief made to wipe His sweat, so He wiped it with a makeshift cloth. The clothes He wore were made by those in the world of Satan who did not even know who Jesus was, and the food He ate was prepared by unclean women of the Satanic world. There was no place for Him to dwell. It is a lamentable matter. It is a painful fact.

What was the reason for establishing and preparing the chosen people of Israel? It was to prepare for the coming of the Messiah, the bridegroom. Therefore, not a single handkerchief, not a spoonful of rice, not a single garment, not a cup of water could appear before Jesus without connecting through the heart. Yet, Jesus died on this earth without having even one hour in such a position. If it is sorrowful, where can there be a greater sorrow, and if it is painful, where can there be a greater pain?

Where did the standard of God's 4,000-year history go astray? You must understand that it went astray from the absence of a true bride who could connect through the heart with Jesus.

At one time, I prayed like this. I wanted to walk the path that no one in the world of Satan had walked, carrying the Lord when He came to this earth. I prayed like that. Who on this earth has made clothes from seeds sown and harvested with a heart, not made by the hands of those in the world of Satan? No one has done it. Can one be blessed like that?

If Jesus is the Lord who was prepared for 4,000 years, then the temple in the land of Judea should have been a temple that could connect through the heart. That temple belongs to Jesus, that nation belongs to Jesus, and those people belong to Jesus. Every priest and scribe of the church belongs to Jesus. Yet, they became enemies of Jesus. You must understand this lamentable fact. You must clearly know that there were such twists and turns in the path of Jesus you are serving today.

Who knew the heart of Jesus, who prayed while holding on to the connections of heaven, longing for the counterpart of the heart, and dying without fulfilling His purpose? No one knew. Even though He resurrected after crossing the peak of death, carrying the twists and turns of His heart, there was no one who understood those twists and turns. Without anyone understanding, how could they be resolved? They could not be resolved because humanity could not recognize the twists and turns related to humanity. Because He resurrected with such a heart, when Mary Magdalene appeared before the resurrected Jesus and called out, "Lord!" He said, "Do not touch me," and stopped her.

Since Jesus left, even until today, who knows His circumstances after 2,000 years? Who knows the heart He had on the Mount of Transfiguration? Dear ones, how will you discern between the true shepherd and the false shepherd? Those who can pierce through the heart of heaven and the heart of heavenly principles are not true shepherds.

Christianity is divided and fighting. Christianity is becoming increasingly faint. Why is this happening? It is because the heart has become faint. It is not because people are lacking or insignificant. It is because, regardless of whether one is talented or not, educated or uneducated, they have not equipped themselves with the heart that must be prepared.

The Lord walked the path of the heart, and you must understand that when He comes again, He will walk the path of the heart.

So, what path must the countless people who have been living a life of faith for 6,000 years to prepare to welcome the coming Lord pave? No matter how much wealth one accumulates, heaven cannot possess it. No matter how splendid a culture one establishes, heaven cannot take it as it is. Even if humans possess some financial power, heaven cannot take it.

What does heaven wish to possess first? Heaven does not want to possess any material goods. What heaven desires is the heart. The heart is the leading authority, the standard of judgment, and the source of life. Isn't that so? What is heaven searching for? Is it searching for money? Is it searching for people? Absolutely not. Heaven has been struggling for 6,000 years to find those who possess a prepared heart, those who are preparing to serve through the heart.

What is a bride? A bride is someone who can appear as a complete object equipped with everything the bridegroom thinks of. That bride must have both a body and a heart as a reality, and an environment corresponding to that must be prepared. Therefore, a bride cannot say that even what belongs to her is truly hers. Even if it is hers, she cannot dispose of it as she pleases. The current ideology of Christianity is speaking of the thoughts of the bride and bridegroom. Like a virgin preparing to serve the bridegroom, when she pours out all her sincerity and her passion boils over with blood, she can finally become his bride. Furthermore, the path of the bride is to seek a place where she can be embraced as the first and the last.

Before that heart, everything of the bride is governed. Therefore, when she steps forward with that heart, even her possessions are not truly hers. To step forward to that place, she must prepare as much as she respects and values it. It requires complete preparation to serve Him, even for a moment or an hour.

Today, the time has come for Christians around the world to awaken. As brides in the process of preparing to serve through the heart, what did the Jews prepare? If there had been those among the Israelites during Jesus' time who understood this heart and prepared, they would not have laid Jesus in a manger. It is a bitter and lamentable fact. What does it mean for the Savior to live as a carpenter for over 30 years? Where did the Eastern wise men, who testified that He was the Son of Heaven, go? Where did the family of John the Baptist go? Where did Anna go? Where did Mary and Joseph go, that the Son of Heaven became the king of beggars? For that one person, for that one person's resting place, for that one person's peace, even if it meant shedding blood, they were chosen and sent forth, yet no one fulfilled that heavenly wish. They left after making their own claims. This was not what God wished for.

If the Eastern wise men had welcomed Jesus, they would have become His disciples. 

"I will take responsibility for your precious body and everything in your life. I will take responsibility for all the sorrows of the earth. If you worry about not having money, I will take responsibility for that. If you worry about not having clothes to wear, I will take responsibility for that. I will take responsibility for everything necessary for your life." Was there anyone like that? No, there was not. Joseph and Mary doubted Jesus, and even His brothers mocked Him. They said to Him, "Why are you here? Go up to Jerusalem," and even His brothers laughed at Him. (John 7:3-5) What does this mean?

Everyone gathered here, we must be able to weep as we think of the time of Jesus. No, we must weep as we think of God, who labored with blood, sweat, and tears before sending Jesus to this earth. Furthermore, we must weep as we consider God, who endured the pain while looking at the fallen Adam and Eve, and who felt sorrow for the fallen Adam and Eve.

From the time God labored to create this world until the fall of Adam and Eve, through the 4,000 years of sorrowful peaks, through the 30 years of sorrowful peaks of Jesus, and through the 2,000 years of sorrowful peaks that the Holy Spirit had to go through, we must weep, saying, "Please forgive the unfaithfulness of our ancestors, forgive the shortcomings of our ancestors, and forgive the sins of our ancestors." While our ancestors treated the one who came in such a way, I will never treat Him like that. I hope to see a figure, a group on this earth who, regardless of any loss or damage to their own selves, struggles without eating or wearing anything. If there is such a person, God will hold them and weep. Jesus will hold them and weep. The Holy Spirit will hold them and weep. Of course, the Triune God and all the prophets and saints of history will hold them and weep. But is there anyone on this earth who can bear witness with tears? Is there anyone who can embody the heart of heaven that God can bear witness to with tears? Is there anyone who can be recognized by God, Jesus, or the Holy Spirit as someone who has prepared their heart? If there is no one, then we must perish. We must perish. We must inevitably perish.

What governs history is not any culture. It is not any ideology. Unless there is a standard of heart that can move along with heaven, which moves ideologies, history cannot find its direction. Humanity has not understood this.

In the end, what will remain before humanity is not any civilization, nor any formal religious organization, nor any subjective person asserting their own ideology. Only that which can connect through the heart, which cannot be explained in words, will remain.
The heart is something that cannot be changed even if you give the entire universe. Before theory, a protagonist with the ability to feel such emotions must emerge on this earth for it to be restored. The one who comes as such a missioner is the Lord of the Second Advent.

What will remain before humanity in the end?
Everyone, we must think once more. At some point, have you ever made even a handkerchief with a tearful heart? Ladies here, have you tried? Holding the needle, wouldn't it be nice if this needle passed through the hands of a saint who truly conveys the heart? It is frustrating. Oh Father, if I had the skill to make a needle, I would like to create a needle with sincere effort to make a handkerchief, but since I cannot do that, I will use the needle that has been made to create a handkerchief with all my heart. Please accept it. And as I thread the needle and stitch each piece of cloth, may the historical grievances of women be resolved through the movements of this needle, and may the longing of the bridegroom, Jesus, be reconciled. Have you ever prayed like that? 

For the husband who cannot live even a hundred years in this world, you would have done everything possible. You would have tried all sorts of things, saying you love him and so on. It is not a laughing matter. So, what kind of person should the one preparing as a bride be? Even if the environment he is in is limited and his body is but a single entity, he must understand that the environment he stays in is connected to the world and the heavens, and that the place he stands is a position representing God and Jesus. 

When the Lord comes with such a heart, if I say, "I have nothing to offer. I have no material possessions. I have prepared nothing. This unworthy body, with this one piece of handkerchief filled with heart, I want to present it before the Lord," then you must understand that Heaven is more pleased with that than with all the good things of heaven and earth. Heaven is looking for such a person.

What kind of bride should there be? Not a bride who hopes for the luxurious glory of the Lord, nor a bride who wishes to go to heaven because of the Lord, but a bride who says, "I will be the stepping stone from hell, so please live on this earth with the heart of heaven." Such a bride is needed. 

In this light, all Christians around the world must go to hell. What heaven? They must go to hell.

Heaven is for those who serve with the heart.
You all, we must offer gifts. Even before the miserable Jesus who was born in a stable, the three wise men from the East presented gold, frankincense, and myrrh as gifts. What gifts do you have prepared to present before the coming bridegroom? 

Father! I have nothing. My heart is eager to give, my desire to offer is earnest, but I have nothing. So, before I eat a spoonful of rice, please eat it first. Even if it is a shabby piece of clothing, please wear it before I do. Even if it is a hut, please dwell there before I do. 

Heaven only needs that kind of heart. The material viewed with such a heart can replace the value of thousands of gold. The world longed for with that heart can replace the original world, and when you long for it with that heart, the Lord will appear in that place. 

Among you, is there anyone who has believed in Jesus for decades and claims that even if everyone else goes to hell, they will surely go to heaven and receive salvation? If there is, then before that, they must first mourn. They must mourn for not knowing the heart of the Lord. Even if the Lord comes to this earth, they must mourn for not having the environment in which the Lord can dwell. They must mourn for not having a single material to offer before the Lord. Everything visible is a symbol of sorrow, and there is nothing that does not bring sorrow, yet we are not in such a position. 

However, if the heart that worries about God goes ahead, the Lord will look upon it, and even if you lose the world and lose the earth, you must clearly understand that you cannot lose yourself. Such a person, even if heaven turns upside down, the Lord will say, "You cannot be left in the world of Satan." The reason the Lord's Second Advent has been delayed for two thousand years is that there has been no such person in the course of history.

Everyone! We must cry with our hearts. We must weep with our hearts. Looking back brings tears, looking forward brings tears, looking to the left and right brings tears, looking up and down brings tears. Thinking of God who worked for our sinful selves, we must forget whether we are inside or outside our bodies to the extent that we forget our existence, forget to eat, forget to wear, forget our faith and situation, and have a time of prostration before Heaven, crying out in anguish. This must be the first step into the path of the bride. You must understand that those who cannot be touched by the shock of faith in such a heart have no relation to the coming Lord.

The attitude of life for those who become brides before the Lord.
We must walk the path where we can look back and shed tears. Jesus, the Savior of this earth and the Prince of Heaven, the King of Kings, came to this earth and walked such a path. Where has the foundation of the bride prepared for four thousand years gone? We must understand the grievance of Heaven, which lamented to see Jesus, who should sing songs of happiness with the bride and harmonize the universe, suffering on the painful cross. He could not eat or wear while walking that path, and as a stepchild, he did not receive respect even from his form, and he was pointed at by neighbors and relatives. Because he shared the same emotions and longed for a good living environment, his sorrow was greater than anyone else's, and he felt more pain than anyone else. You must understand that when Jesus was driven away from the church and persecuted by the priests, tears blurred his vision as he walked along the foot of the Mount of Olives.

You must know that Jesus was so humble. Compared to the humble life of Jesus who walked for thirty years, your environment is too wonderful. You have so much. If you feel wronged, you can express that grievance, and if you are happy, you can express that joy. However, Jesus, who did not know pretense and external appearances, could not express his grievances even when he had something to be indignant about, and he never showed his unfair circumstances. That was the sorrow of sorrows. Have you ever shown a joyful expression at any time? You must understand that you have not.

Now, even when you eat, you must eat in place of the bridegroom. Just as a parent sends a beloved child to another place and before eating a spoonful of rice, they first think of their child, you must also place a spoonful of rice down and say, "Lord, have you ever sat at such a table?" You should be able to say that. When you wear a shabby piece of clothing, you should be able to say, "Lord, have you ever worn such clothes?" And when you have a joyful occasion, you should be able to say, "Lord, have you ever experienced such a situation?"

The bride you wish to serve has not experienced such an environment, so those who wish to become brides must be prepared to have a deep emotional connection with the Lord's life. That is the issue. Such a person does not need any leader. They do not need any shepherd. The Bible is not a problem. The Bible is a letter. You must clearly understand that it is a letter left to cultivate a person of emotional character.

We must have the heart that can shed tears when seeing a single object in a place where our hearts are inclined, and before holding that object, we must say, "Lord!" Before eating, we must say, "Lord!" Before wearing clothes, we must say, "Lord!" Before lying down, we must say, "Lord!" If there is such a bride, the bridegroom will seek that bride.

What is heaven like? It is a place where those who boast of what they have prepared and those who have lived a life of service can go. Then, what kind of person goes to that heaven? Is it a place for those who believe in the Lord and go forward seeking blessings? No. Heaven is a place for those who prepare emotionally to serve. Even if they die during the preparation period, those who can leave behind a life of service and go joyfully are the ones who go there. That is where resurrection exists.

After preparing to serve, you must live a life of service. The purpose of preparation is to serve. How will you live a life of service? You must examine your environment. The details of life are not apparent. How to live is now a significant issue we must consider in our lives of service.

When facing the Lord, we must prepare to treat Him in such a way. We must live a life of preparation to serve. Serving does not mean going to the heavens to serve; it means becoming one who serves on this earth. Have you ever served the Lord? What is the Lord's face like? What is the Lord's body like? What is the Lord's nose like? What are the Lord's smiling eyes like? What is the Lord's voice like? What is the Lord's mouth like when He speaks? What are the Lord's hands and all His attitudes like?

The world of the heart
Where the heart leads, there is a law of harmony that can draw people in. The heart of a parent longing for a child transcends distance and space to recognize the situation of the child. This is a natural phenomenon, but it occurs supernaturally. When the heart is deeply felt, it happens that way. Such a heart encompasses the universe. With such a heart, even Jesus can be drawn closer. When you are deeply moved by such a heart, the Lord, who seems unrelated, appears in a relational form, and the Lord, who seems to have no connection, comes to have a connection. You must understand this. Only then will you know what the Lord will do when you meet Him. Therefore, you must understand that the life of service must be prepared and equipped in this way.

In the scriptures, which are written as letters for the bridegroom to find the bride, there are many codes. Why were they spoken in code? Because He is the God of the heart. Not everyone can decipher the Bible. They cannot. Only the bride and bridegroom can decipher it. Only those who have prepared to serve through the heart can decipher it; those who have not cannot. What is the identity of the codes here? It is the secret that opens the door for the bridegroom to come, and what is that secret? It is the heart. The heart of a parent is the same when nursing a baby or when that child grows old and has white hair. There is no difference in that heart.

Therefore, we must dig into all the sources of the heart hidden in the scriptures. We must understand this. Knowing this does not require a PhD. No matter how much they interpret, academic theories will pass by. The heart cannot be governed by logic. It cannot be experienced through theory. It cannot be directed by a system. Why? Because the heart flows with the natural order.

The Bible can be understood and felt without learning, and before interpreting the flow and feeling of the heart, it cannot be known. The modern theological trends that scholars advocate will pass by. However, the world of the heart does not pass. This is what is called the Alpha and Omega, the beginning and the end.

There are no conditions for the heart to pass. Where the heart is, the Lord cannot pass. God cannot pass. The Holy Spirit cannot pass. Even the historical philosophers cannot pass. Therefore, the more a nation has such emotional connections, the less likely it is to perish. It does not perish. The closer the national spirit permeates the line of heart for the country, the less likely that nation is to perish. When it becomes divided and dispersed, the natural order passes, and it perishes.

The motive of single-mindedness is the heart. Single-mindedness is the result. Single-mindedness, before establishing a noun, is the heart; if one possesses this heart, they may be on earth, but they are in heaven. Even if they are in an unfortunate situation, they are in a happy place, and you must clearly understand this.

If we are in the process of acquiring such a heart, what must we do? When you appear before Abraham, you must be qualified to say, "Abraham, you did this and that." You can even give direct commands to Abraham in that land. You can command Moses. You can command the twelve apostles. If it resonates in the world of the heart, you can push Abraham from four thousand years ago into that world and command him. The same goes for Moses and the apostles.

No matter how great the apostle is, they are messengers. You cannot call an apostle a bride. Who is higher, the apostle or the bride? The bride is higher. The apostle must bow their head before the bride.

Heaven is a place for those who live a life of service with the heart.
The historical Apostle Paul! Of course, he is great. However, today, there must be a person of emotional character who can even say "Oh!" to the Apostle Paul. A person who can command those who have come and gone on this earth, who can govern those who have emotional connections on this earth, and who can establish emotional connections in the future would undoubtedly be qualified to be a bride. We must meet such Christians, such sons and daughters of God on this earth.

If we can feel Abraham's heart when speaking of it, and if we can know Moses' heart when speaking of it, and if we can know Jesus' heart when speaking of it, and if we can reflect and feel the heart of God in a historical context, unless such a figure appears on this earth, the Lord's Second Advent is impossible. It is impossible.

What is the purpose of the Lord coming to this earth? It is to establish heaven on earth. What is heaven like? It is a place where those who have passed the preparation for service and those who have passed the life of service go. The world where the preparation for service and the life of service can be eternally boasted of in the universe is heaven.

Do you know what you do in heaven? Do you think it is just a place to play? Absolutely not. To play, there must be conditions of preparation and living that allow for playing. 

Yet, what do people do? They pray for blessings without doing anything. The main reason why spiritual people struggle is right there. No matter how much grace they say they have received, it is hard to last beyond seven years. Asking for blessings unconditionally is not true faith.

What must you do to reach such a place? Today, the 2.7 billion people on this earth are descendants of Adam who have come down for six thousand years. Therefore, you must have a standard of heart that can hold onto and weep for these 2.7 billion people. Otherwise, you will never establish a connection with that world. 

You must have a heart that cannot bear to see a poor beggar and feels pain, that cannot bear to see someone without clothes and thinks of how well you are dressed, and that cannot bear to see someone without food and thinks of how you are eating. You must have such a heart.

We must become the protagonists of the heart.
The current heart of humanity is a reflection of six thousand years of history. Therefore, the times...
Only those who have gone through the process of living with deep indignation and have cried out from their hearts can find the motivation to face historical sentiments. 

Although it is not detailed in the Bible, Jesus shed many tears upon seeing the nation of Israel. He had compassion for the suffering people of Israel. Based on that compassion, Jesus extended his mercy to all the nations of the world. Heaven raises such individuals to work in history.

Moses, too, had a stronger heart of compassion for the Israelites suffering under the power of Satan than for his enemies, which led him to side with the Israelites and strike down the Egyptians. He did not strike out of hatred but rather out of a love for Israel. Because Moses acted from a love for Israel rather than hatred for Egypt, he was not caught in wrongdoing. If one acts out of a love for heaven, then heaven cannot deem that action a sin. Even if someone were killed, if the sentiment was prioritized, it would not fall under the laws of heaven. Satan cannot accuse such a person.

During the 40 years of wandering in the wilderness on the way from Egypt to the land of Canaan, when the remnant of the Israelites entered Canaan, God commanded them to destroy all seven nations of Canaan. He commanded them to wipe them out. This is the kind of God He is. If the Israelites had gone forth with a deep love for the promised land of Canaan and a sincere desire to have God with them, they would not have faced destruction. Those who have the qualifications to judge are such individuals. God longs for such people.

We know that the end days are coming. We are saying that this is the end time. Then, what kind of people can remain in these end days, the ones who can judge? Naturally, they are the protagonists of sentiment.

How much indignation and injustice must God have felt towards Satan, the enemy of heaven, who has tormented our ancestors for 6,000 years? Centered on that overwhelming sentiment, He cannot forgive. When He strikes out in anger, Satan would say, "That is right." Those who cannot possess such a sentiment cannot stand before the law of justice.

There is one thing we must hold onto even in times of oppression. Even if we are persecuted at home, oppressed by our brothers, or chased out by our nation, we must not forget one thing: sentiment. The sentiment that history has overlooked, that the times have overlooked, that the earth has overlooked is the sentiment of heaven. When that sentiment is established, heaven and earth will be separated. The day we hold onto that sentiment and rejoice will be the day when sorrow and suffering in the world will come to an end. On the day we can say, "Father! My son!" and hold onto that sentiment, on the day we can say, "Bridegroom! Bride!" the gates of heaven will open in the world. From there, we must clearly understand that the world of eternal life and happiness will be built.

Heaven is a place where those who serve through sentiment can enter, and it is a place where those who can overcome Satan through a life centered on sentiment can enter.
