<Word> The title I wish to speak about today is "What is My Name?" and "What is Our Name?" When speaking individually, it becomes "What is my name?" and when speaking collectively, it becomes "What is our name?"

Today, I will speak on this title.

The name of humanity and all things through creation and fall. 

There are many people living on this earth, and it is filled with many beings. However, there is no person or being that does not have a name. Each of you has a name. It is not just us; everything has a name.

God created the progenitors of humanity and named them Adam and Eve. After blessing Adam and Eve as the protagonists of all things, God commanded Adam to name all of creation. As recorded in Genesis 2, it says that whatever Adam called each living creature, that was its name.

So, what kind of name is the one Adam gives? It is an eternal name, a name that cannot exist in two forms. It is a name that cannot change, no matter how history or times change. Those who must remain with such names are all of creation, yet today, the names of all things that exist on this earth are diverse. Moreover, every person living on this earth has a name that has gone through various connections.

From the day God created all things and established Adam and Eve, the ancestors of humanity, and blessed them to govern all things, God hoped that the name given by Adam to all creation would remain forever. God also hoped that our ancestor Adam and Eve, whom He personally named, would become the true ancestors of humanity, whom He could neither forget nor ignore. However, we humans, who could not stand in such a position, have forgotten heaven, and creation has forgotten its name and its position, struggling through the course of history.

Why has this happened? It is because of the fall. You, who have gathered here today, also have names, but you must understand that those names were given after the fall and are sad names. Therefore, all the names of creation that exist on this earth are not the names that Adam personally called before the fall, but rather names that have been defiled due to the fall. We must mourn this fact infinitely. 

In Revelation 14, it says that the Lamb stood on Mount Zion, and with Him were 144,000, having His name and the name of His Father written on their foreheads. We must understand that fallen humanity and all things under the power of the fall are eagerly longing to return to their original positions and receive new names given by God.

The names you have must be discarded. The name that God can eternally remember and boast of in the world of goodness must be given by the Lord and by the Father. Fallen humans cannot stand in the glory of heaven as realities without going through this process. When we look at the course of history, we can see that there are nations that can possess the names of the good world and nations that can possess the names of the evil world, emerging in these two branches. 

When we speak of names, this is not about the individual or the reality. When we speak of God, we may refer to Him as the Absolute Being or the ultimate cause, or we may say He is the one with the highest intellect.

Today, those who strive to live according to the commands of their conscience or those who walk the path of the Way, all the hopes and ideals they pursue centered on goodness are things that humans must possess and seek to achieve. However, we cannot deny that these remain in the realm of objective nouns or figurative nouns. Jesus referred to Himself as the way, the truth, and the life. This means that Jesus is indeed the truth, the life, and the way, does it not? Such things are Jesus.
is the name and equal.
The name of Jesus and I
What do the words of the 66 books of the Bible say that heaven desires from us? It is to create a true person, to find a true person. We must understand that these are the words that have been granted to us. 
Then, what is the purpose of following the words and keeping them? It is to become the way, the truth, and the life, just like Jesus. What will be accomplished by fulfilling what Jesus has said? It is to become the bride of Jesus. This is the ultimate goal of a believer. That is why it is said that in the end, we will reign together with Christ. It is a relative relationship. Therefore, when you pray, you pray in the name of Jesus.
We must first seek His name before the reality of Jesus. We must receive the seal that is in the name of Jesus before meeting Him. This is an inevitable destiny that we must recognize in the course of restoration.
On the other hand, in this world, there are names that come from Satan. The devil is called Satan, and Satan is called evil. Evil has various attributes such as envy and jealousy. We must recognize that these attributes of evil are synonymous with Satan.
Thus, every being stands at a crossroads of whether to have a name that can exist with God or a name that can exist with Satan.
Although we have fallen, we are walking the path of restoration, receiving the benefits of heaven's providence. What are we restoring? We are restoring the lost original Adam and the lost original Eve. Then, what is the long history of 6,000 years? It is the history of finding again the true ancestors of humanity, Adam and Eve, who were lost due to God's creation. Establishing Adam and Eve, who can be the true ancestors of humanity, is the feast of the Lamb, and the time when this will be realized is the era of the Second Coming. The 6,000 years of history is the history of restoring the fallen Adam and Eve.
Not the dead Adam, not the fallen Adam, not the Adam who was invaded by Satan, but the Adam and Eve who were loved before God 6,000 years ago, and the Adam and Eve who must survive without dying, must be the position of today's believers. Therefore, when you hold onto one, you are connected to God's 6,000 years of history. In this sense, your one life is greater than the universe. Now, the man whom God is trying to hold onto and bring out is a being that has survived continuously from the day of creation until today, without being cut off at any point in the historical course of the fall, representing Adam.
History is not a dead history. History circulates and revolves. There are only differences in the size of the form. Personally, we go through such forms, and then, on a larger scale, we go through such forms in families, and then expand to national and global levels. However, the shape remains the same. Therefore, we must clear the world of death and cross over to the new world of grace, and we must find the authority of resurrection by crossing over the peak of judgment. In what position should we be? We must stand in the position of Adam and Eve who did not fall.
Our existence has become an object of heaven's sorrow as we have come through the long history of 6,000 years, and we have been dragged out in front of heaven's providence, unable to be pulled out until now. Even if you look at one, you have a bloodline connected to the prophets throughout history, starting from Adam, Noah, Abraham, and so on. Furthermore, there is a connection to God's heart, who is trying to bring out such a nation. We must not forget this.
Therefore, what should you do now? You must trace history and clear all the things that have been tangled in the historical course. To go to a place where you can receive the new grace of resurrection, you must be in a position to align with God's heart, which gives the new ideology and new authority.
To align with God's heart, what must we do? God created Adam and Eve and looked at them with a hopeful and joyful heart, but from the day of the fall, He looked at them with despair, sighs, and a sorrowful heart. So, what must we do? With my heart, I must long for the good Adam and Eve that God looked upon, and with my body, I must feel God's sorrow and long for God, who was struggling in despair.
The name to be left and the name to be removed
If you have a certain name, you must recognize that you are in the position of replacing the old Adam, and furthermore, you are in the position of replacing the old Cain and Abel. We are beings that replace Adam, and at the same time, we are beings that replace Cain and Abel. But what kind of being was Adam? He was the ancestor of disbelief who did not trust heaven. Therefore, you carry Adam's name, and at the same time, the name of disbelief is attached to it. The fallen us do not have a name aligned with heaven but rather a name that Satan can invade.
Because we were born from the ancestor of disbelief, we carry the name of disbelief along with Adam's name. Therefore, the critical point of restoration lies with Adam. Thus, you must judge the name of disbelief and leave the name of Adam that God hoped for. There are elements of disbelief that remain within you.
We still do not know the entirety of the grace that God wanted to bestow upon us centered around the ideology of the creation of heaven and earth. We do not know the eternal world that remains unknown. As humans who could not believe the words that God manifested as reality, we cannot believe the words and facts that are spoken in the invisible world. Therefore, you must leave the name of Adam that can please God and remove the name of disbelief that has been tangled due to the fall.
In the family of Adam and Eve, who fell due to disbelief, God established Cain and Abel to carry out the providence of restoration. You must feel that all the disgraceful acts that appeared in the historical course were your own disgraceful acts. The name of disbelief that our ancestors left behind is also yours, and the name of the murderer when Cain killed Abel is also your name. To stand before heaven, we must take responsibility for the historical sins and clear them, or we cannot comfort the historical God and cannot please God, who desires repentance with a historical heart. Therefore, you must establish only the original name of Adam that God has drawn upon the name you currently possess, and remove all other filthy names.
You have the name of disbelief attached to you. Just as Cain has the name of a murderer when he killed Abel, you too have the name of a descendant of a murderer attached to you. When one goes to prison, their name is attached along with the name of a murderer or a robber. Similarly, you have the name of the crime of murder that Cain committed against Abel attached to you. The act of murder is not only Cain's from the past but also inheriting to today’s me. The act of disbelief is not only Adam's from the past but also today’s me. We must recognize this.
After Adam, there was Noah 1,600 years later. Noah devoted himself for 120 years to establish the integrity of faith. Even those who could not truly cooperate with Noah's work were able to enter the blessings of Noah's faith for free. However, Ham became a shameful figure before heaven. Everything that heaven does not rejoice in the biblical history or the providence of salvation after the fall remains ours, becomes yours. After 1,600 years of labor to establish Noah and judging the world with water, Noah's eight family members who remained were truly the family of God's hope. However, among them, Ham became a shameful lineage before heaven by being ashamed of seeing Noah naked. Because of this, you too have a shameful name that cannot lift your face before heaven.
It did not stop there. After 400 years from Noah, during the time of Abraham, when offering the three sacrifices, the cattle and sheep were divided, but the dove was not divided. Dividing is to sanctify. The dove, which should be sanctified and divided, was not divided, so Abraham's sacrifice returned in error. Because of this inability to divide and sanctify, the noun of impurity is attached to you.
Furthermore, looking at Moses, he struck the rock twice in anger. Of course, it was said that the nation made a mistake, but since he is your ancestor, it is the same as what you did. Moses's anger betrayed God's will and fulfilled Satan's will. Therefore, the sin that arose from Moses striking the rock twice in anger remains in your name. Not only that, but the Israelites who followed Moses also betrayed him. They not only disbelieved but also betrayed him. They betrayed and cursed heaven. Whose names are attached to this disbelief, betrayal, and curse? They are attached to us, the descendants.
In Romans chapter 1, there are twenty-one kinds of sins listed. You must understand that all these nouns of sin are not the world's nouns but are the names that are burdened upon you. Look from verse 29. All unrighteousness, wickedness, greed, malice, envy, murder, strife, deceit, malignity, whisperings, fornication, things that are hateful to God, despiteful, proud, boasters, inventors of evil things, disobedient to parents, without understanding, covenantbreakers, without natural affection, implacable, unmerciful, and so on. All these nouns that are placed before heaven have been created by our ancestors and have continued until now. In the end, what must we do with all these nouns? We must take responsibility and clear all these nouns. You must recognize that this mission is upon you.
What does faith require?
Therefore, those who believe in Jesus consider themselves sinners. I am a sinner. Father, please forgive this sinner. What sin? The sin of Adam, the sin of Cain, the sin of Ham, the mistakes of Abraham, the mistakes of Moses, the mistakes of the Israelite nation, the sin of killing Jesus on the cross, and the sins of countless nations that have betrayed Jesus since then are all the nouns of sin that are burdened upon you. Many believers throughout history have confessed themselves as sinners, but no one has confessed as a sinner while placing history before them.
You have a mission to establish a center of victory at the end and to carry out the judgment. If you want to walk this path, you must be able to judge all the names of sins that have occurred in the historical course. You must judge the Satan that has prompted sins and attached the names of sins to our bloodline or our lives. Therefore, as the end approaches, we must establish ourselves as cosmic sinners and become those who can subdue this. Only such people can cross over the peak of judgment.
When we look at the state of sin in this era, that sin does not belong to those people but to you. Even the family murder case in Myeongdong is not just the sin of that person. You must recognize that you have also committed such murders. They have appeared, and you have not appeared.
So, what does faith demand? It demands repentance, repentance. What kind of repentance? Historical repentance and era repentance. Heaven desires historical repentance and era repentance. Knowing this, all past sins are my sins, and all sins that remain in this era are my sins, so Father, please forgive me. Only those who pray like this can stand before heaven.
Have you ever thought at any time that you are a murderer or a robber? Have you ever felt that you are a robber or a thief? Have you ever felt that you are wearing the name tag of all the ugly sins that cannot be accepted before heaven? Have you ever hated this self and sacrificed everything to subdue the elements of sin within you, forgetting everything and seeking forgiveness before heaven? If you have not done so, you cannot stand before heaven.
Jesus carried all the sins of 4,000 years of history in His body and walked the path of the cross with all the sins of the era. Today, 2,000 years after Jesus came and went, we at the end must bear all the sins of 6,000 years of history in this one body and make atonement before heaven. Thus, we must receive the grace of atonement and the grace of liberation. You must understand that as long as you cannot establish a standard that can please heaven and earth, you cannot cross over the peak of judgment.
We are sinners among sinners, and we are sinners who have killed our parents. We did not kill parents who gave birth to us in the world of Satan but killed Jesus, whom we must honor as our eternal parents. Who is Jesus? He is the figure of the second Adam, the one who came to restore the true parents because Adam lost the true parents due to the fall. We killed the one who came as the true parent to embrace humanity.
It was not only the ancient Israelite nation that killed Him. It was not only Judas Iscariot who sold Him. You are also related to this. It was not only Pilate or the priests who conspired to kill Him. It was not only the Roman soldiers who pierced Him with a spear. It was not only the Roman soldiers who placed the crown of thorns on Him. It is you. It is you.
Humanity has lived with the history of 6,000 years of sin. We are still living while committing such sins. We have the culmination of 6,000 years of sin. Therefore, you must repent. You must repent while placing the entire history of 6,000 years of sin before you. Since we struck the true parent, who is the subject of true goodness, we must indemnify and restore the sins. Shouldn't we? Since we have killed the true parents and committed sins, we must uproot the elements of sin with the words of the true parents. Only by being able to eliminate the sources of all sins from the family of Adam to today’s me can we become the bride of Jesus.
What name do you have? 
Therefore, you must repent. There is a name of falsehood attached to my body, so I must repent to remove this name of falsehood. Or perhaps there is a name of envy attached, and a name of pride attached, and a name of anger...
Since it has been named, we must repent to remove these names. Also, in my heart, there are murderous elements that want to hate and kill others, so I must repent to remove these as well. Paul participated in the killing of Stephen and was sent to Damascus to capture Christians. However, on his way to Damascus, he met Jesus and repented. He realized that the Jesus he had killed was the Messiah. He recognized that Stephen, whom he had supported in killing, was the beloved son of God by Jesus. At that moment, instead of repenting for killing Stephen, he repented for the nation killing Jesus. He repented for the nation's wrongs, worrying about God, who had worked hard for 4,000 years to establish the nation.

After that, he went to Arabia and lived a life of prayer for three years. That period was not one of joy or happiness, but a time of sorrow and tears. During that time, he prayed with a heart that was filled with the desire to bear all the sins of killing Jesus and to have all the sins of killing Jesus forgiven through this one body. It was a time of great repentance before heaven. Because of this period, he was able to step forward with the name of Jesus, regardless of the place of death or any circumstances.

Where did the strength for Saul to appear as Paul come from? It started from feeling like a sinner. When he recalled the entire history of 4,000 years, he felt that he was the representative of sinners. Therefore, he was overwhelmed with emotion at the thought that such a sinner could be held by the hand of heaven's mercy.

When one who feels like a great sinner encounters a great gift, heaven and earth are turned upside down. That is why Paul transformed the history of Israel into a new history of the gospel. Where did that driving force come from? It came from striking down his sinful self and repenting of his sins. Through such a process, having triumphed, Saul received the original name given by God and became Paul.

At the end of days, heaven will ask you what name you have. What is your name? Are you the Adam before the fall? Are you Noah, who was faithful for 120 years for heaven? Are you Abraham, who left Ur of the Chaldeans according to heaven's will? Or are you Moses, who lived with a heart of concern for the chosen people for 80 years?

What name has been given to you? This is the problem. Heaven hopes that you will pass through the name before the elements of evil invade and ultimately carry the name of Jesus. If you do not possess the name of Jesus, who can judge the cross, you cannot become a bride.

Have you ever prayed, "God, please move me to the place where Adam and Eve stayed before the fall"? Do you long for the heart of Adam and Eve before the fall? Do you miss the environment where you could freely approach God and where God could freely approach you? Do you long for the heart of Abel, who offered sacrifices with all his devotion? Or do you miss the heart of Noah? The heart of Abraham? The heart of Moses? Or even more, the heart of Jesus?

In the historical journey, we must have the heart of our ancestors who fought against evil and cared for heaven, and without the tears of repentance to clear away all the defiled names until now, we cannot receive the name of Jesus. If there is still anger in your heart, your name is anger. If there is jealousy in your heart, your name is jealousy. When you appear before God, such names remain. It is not just any name.

Therefore, we must escape from these elements of sin and receive the nine fruits of the Holy Spirit (Galatians 6:22-23), namely love, joy, peace, patience, kindness, goodness, faithfulness, gentleness, and self-control as our names. What are these fruits? They are the names we should have after acquiring the heart of the original Adam and Eve, who were not connected to sin. Your name is not the name that heaven desires. Heaven does not want names like Kim, or any other names. What does heaven desire? Heaven hopes that your name will be love. Heaven hopes that your name will be peace. You must possess the names of the nine fruits of the Holy Spirit. What name can you present?

We must long for this. We must clear away all the names defiled in the world of sin through repentance, faithfulness, and sacrifice, and possess the nine fruits of the Holy Spirit to cross over the hill of the cross and meet the resurrected Jesus. Which name do you have among love, joy, peace, patience, kindness, goodness, faithfulness, gentleness, and self-control? Can you present one of these nouns before heaven and say, "This is my name"? To have such a name and to be recognized as such requires the testimony of three or more people. Along with the name you possess, that person must indeed be a child of heaven, a gentle person, a merciful person, a person who brings peace, and must receive testimony from three or more people. Without the testimony of the saints, you cannot receive the testimony of the Father, the Son, and the Holy Spirit.

That is why, in our journey of faith, heaven sends us out while saying, "I love you and recognize you." We cannot rely solely on heaven's recognition. We must receive recognition from three or more people on earth. From what standpoint must we receive this recognition? We must be qualified to be recognized by three or more people who stand in the position of loving children, who would die together or live together. Only then will heaven grant them a heavenly name along with their name.

So when you reflect on yourself, what name do you have? Do you not have a name of jealousy and envy rather than a name of love? Do you not have a name of dissatisfaction and complaint rather than a name of peace? You must examine what name you have and possess a name that you can present before heaven.

Jesus said, "I am the way, the truth, and the life," so without passing through such a way, we cannot become the protagonists of truth, life, or love. We must either replace the way, truth, or life with the name of the word given by heaven above the name we possess. If we cannot do that, it means we have no relationship with Jesus.

Until now, we have lived a life of repentance. What have we repented of? The wrongs between brothers are very few. More than that, we must repent for being descendants who have come through the blood of historical sin, who are ignorant and tremendous sinners and prisoners. Therefore, we must be embraced by the hand of heaven's mercy.

After repenting, we must receive the sign from heaven that says, "You are my son, you are my daughter." We must receive that sign. Without receiving that sign, your name cannot remain in the eternal heavenly kingdom. Therefore, you must strive to judge everything that is contrary to the heavenly.

There is no separate enemy. You are your own enemy. Everything that hopes for the earth is the enemy. Everything that wants to possess something of the earth, to know something, or to relate to something must be struck down. You must let go of all of this.

You must have a heart that longs for heavenly things rather than worldly things, and live each day with heaven to avoid receiving the name of Satan. Only such a person is one who possesses the name of heaven and can welcome the Lord.

Father, what have I done?
Matthew 25:1-46
<Prayer> Father! We are like the prodigal son who has come back home in shabby clothes and an ugly appearance. 

You have longed for your lost sons and daughters for 6,000 years, and we have been ravaged by Satan for 6,000 years. Please help us understand your painful heart as you struggle to find your sons and daughters.

Regardless of how ugly our appearance is or how we look, you wanted sons and daughters who recognize you as their Father, yet we stand before you, having come through a sorrowful historical journey, unable to recognize you as our Father. What can we say now? On this earth, we desire nothing but to recognize you as our Father.

Father, we have seen the words of the Bible. But who knows the earnest circumstances of Jesus who spoke such words? Who knows the sorrowful heart? Who knows the painful heart? That Jesus was the Savior of all people, the true Father of all people, the representative of the struggle to save all, the one who was mocked by Satan, and the prince of sorrow who carried the cross. We did not know that he was the prince of pain who comforted heaven with tears amidst suffering and persecution.

Your sons and daughters who have gathered here, for what reason, we do not know, but we have met while passing through this village and that village, this valley and that valley, this alley and that alley. Father! Now please hold onto them. Please create a foundation in their hearts where they can speak what they want to say.

Father, we have heard many words in this world. We have learned and know many things. We can speak as well as anyone else. Yet we do not have a heart that earnestly longs for you. Please forgive us. Now, standing in this place, we do not wish to boast of anything, so Father, please allow us to form a bond of connection that we cannot forget or sever. This is both heaven's wish and our wish. If this is fulfilled, we will not need millions of believers.

Let us know that kneeling before you and bowing our heads in tears is the most precious thing. Let us realize that we are those who should comfort you by weeping over the historical process you have gone through.
I wish to serve my Father, and I wish to face my Father. May You entrust us with the path of sorrow and suffering that You left behind, and may You allow us to take on the rough path of Golgotha. I will become the way and the stepping stone so that my Father can walk on a smooth path. 
Please allow us to be children who can say this. I earnestly hope and desire this.
Father! Now that Your sons and daughters have gathered, please do not let this time be in vain. Allow this time to be one where the dead come back to life, where those in despair can have hope, and where those who were bound in the world of death can experience the liberation of freedom. May this time be one where those who have lost the center of their hearts and do not know You can once again establish that center and call You Father. I earnestly hope and desire this, Father.
Now, I wish to convey Your words, so please guide me according to Your will. Allow the heart of the one delivering the message and the heart of those receiving it to become one, and let us have the heart of a little child. We are not our own; we belong to You, and everything that belongs to us is not ours but Yours, so please allow us to return it to You.
As heaven moves, may we move, and when heaven stirs, may we also stir. Please bless us to settle all sorrows and to sing and rejoice in Your glory within the realm of Your life. I earnestly hope and desire that You embrace us with Your grace.
I entrust everything to You, so please take charge. I know that lonely vessels are appealing to You at this time, so please be with them. I pray in the name of the Lord. Amen.
<Words> The title of the message I wish to share with you is "Father, what have I done?" I would like to speak briefly on this title.
Our appearance, wandering in search of a way to live
None of us gathered here can deny that we are imperfect people and that we are bound by the shackles of sin. You are living in such an environment, and you are seeking something within that environment. People are always demanding something. Moreover, as long as we have our senses and limbs, we are constantly moving. We are searching for something and are always doing something. Even at this moment, you are doing something. This is not limited to you as individuals. Broadly speaking, this applies to the world, this land, and the entire universe. If there is a Creator and some deity, surely they are also doing something and are waiting for something.
We cannot deny that individuals, families, societies, nations, the world, and even the universe are all moving under certain connections and motivations. We are those who live in such circumstances. We are those who claim to live our lives meaningfully. We are those who have lived with a desire to boast of ourselves in every direction.
Then, knowing that today exists alongside yesterday and that today coexists with tomorrow, what are we doing now?
When someone asks, "What have you done?" I might respond, "I have done this." Because what you long for is this, I have lived for this in the past, I am living for this in the present, and I wish to live for this in the future. Is there anyone who can confidently and proudly answer like this? There has been no such person in the past, nor is there one in the present.
If there had been such a person, the world would not be like this. Heaven cannot have such an indifferent relationship with us. Even if we are but a small individual, if a victorious figure could appear on this earth who represents the whole and answers on behalf of the universe, we would not be living such sorrowful lives.
Even if we delve deep into our hearts, there are continuous sorrowful twists that we cannot sever. Furthermore, this is true when we look outside. Heaven and earth are in such circumstances. We must understand that it is the sad and painful life of fallen humanity to gather oneself and approach the great universe in such an environment. In such circumstances, where is the one who feels great sorrow and pain and is crying? You must not forget that it is heaven that seeks such a person.
We are moving. We are doing something. This body, which is destined to go and to do, where is it staying? Is it resting in a happy family? Is it placed in some glorious position of the nation? That place is not our settlement. Therefore, our hearts urge us differently. There are shocks that come from every place we stay. In the midst of this, our true selves are wandering in search of a resting place for life, a way to live.
Have you ever criticized yourself from a third-party perspective? Is there nothing like this?" If you have not, you must realize that you are in a pitiful position. You must recognize that you are living a life that does not consider the front, back, left, or right in such circumstances.

Father, what have I done?

Jesus also walked such a path, and there has been no sage among the sages who did not walk such a path. Especially, we who are at the end must resolve the sorrows of history. If there is nothing that connects us to the heavenly heart behind history, we will be in despair.

Therefore, throughout history, those who have aimed for goodness have not been free from rejection by those who should uphold that intention. A person who can receive the comfort of heaven

A history of repeated betrayal
We thought the father we believe in is the glorious father, but he is not. We believed that the Lord we serve would come in glory, but he did not. He is a father who is at the very bottom, shedding tears and suffering even at this moment, following the beloved sons and daughters who are being dragged away by Satan. Is there anyone who has looked back at that father, who follows with a parent's heart, and shed tears? No, there is not. You did not know such a heavenly being, but you must understand that heaven has replaced you millions of times.

Father, what have I done?
What have we done? What have I done? It is a solemn and overwhelming matter. We cannot deny that we are the vanguard of the traitors. We have utterly violated the voice that God cherished and entrusted in Eden. We were the ones who thoughtlessly betrayed the father who wanted to believe, embrace, and love us. It was the father who set the conditions for restoration to find such humans and has been fighting against Satan. But Abel has disappeared, and only Cain remains, so we cannot deny that we are the descendants who have continued the Cain altar. We are participants in the Cain altar. Heaven has established ancestors to resolve this grievance, allowing them to go through a pitiful life. After 1,600 years, God found Noah, who was a pitiful figure. He was Noah, who bore a heavenly mission that went against the times. Noah had no friends. He had no companions. His wife was not someone he could communicate with, nor were his children able to discuss matters with him. In such a position, he held on to the voice of heaven's command and endured, fighting for 120 years. Even if grievances were inflicted, he was Noah who kept his loyalty to the promise. After the 40-day flood judgment, he failed to understand the meaning of fulfilling heaven's wishes and committed acts of disbelief. We are a group that has participated in the Cain altar and the altar of Ham.

Heaven called the father of faith, Abraham, to complete the great work of heaven and commanded him with heartfelt attention, but Abraham made mistakes and could not offer the three sacrifices according to heaven's will. Is there anyone who can say they have surpassed Abraham's position? Who would have thought that the 600,000 people taken out from Pharaoh would betray heaven while energetically heading toward the new land of Canaan? It was Moses, who struck the rock twice out of deep sorrow, holding onto the heart of heaven while grasping the group that betrayed. Who among you can say they have surpassed Moses' position?

Is that all? Countless prophets, including the four major prophets and the twelve minor prophets, upheld heaven's will, supported them, embraced them, and became their fence. However, they became the ancestors who betrayed. Who can guarantee that you, the descendants who received such ancestral blood, are not part of that lineage?

Still, heaven, in order to save this pitiful nation, waited for 4,000 years as if it were a day and sent Jesus as the Messiah to the Israelite nation to sing the victory song after defeating Satan. However, the Israelite nation betrayed him as well.

Believers must believe in the suffering Jesus
We respect the historical Jesus. We believe in Jesus, a historical figure. I do not want that. We must believe in Jesus, who was a commoner in that era. We must believe in the Jesus who was marginalized and pointed at, whom the priests called a servant of Beelzebub. When Jesus entered the city early in the morning, he was hungry. He saw a fig tree by the roadside, went to it, and found nothing but leaves, and said to the tree, "Let no fruit grow on you ever again." (Matt 21:18-19) We must understand the heart of Jesus, who had no choice but to curse.

There are many who believe in the glorious Jesus. However, there is no one who believes in the suffering Jesus, the marginalized Jesus. Jesus, who while being crucified prayed for his enemies, saying, "Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they do," and who cared for the heart and will of the Father, is not believed by anyone.

Everyone! Why have you come here today? This is a place where people gather to become pitiful followers of Jesus. The person speaking here wants to make you friends of the marginalized Jesus. You must understand that this person stands in a pitiful position to teach you to walk that path.

There was a time when I cried out for this nation. There was a time when I blamed heaven. I have cried out that there is no greater sinner than I. Knowing what others do not know and feeling what others do not feel, I had to strike my chest in a place of joy and weep in a place of dancing. I felt that I was a sinner of the times. I felt that I was a traitor of the times. Because heaven needs someone like me, I must consistently walk that path. Such tangled feelings lead and hold me, which is why I am doing this today.

I have sometimes reproached you. I have also held you and wept and advised you. Each time, I did not treat you as individuals.

O Father who dealt with Adam, appear at this time. O Father who dealt with Cain, appear at this time. O Father who dealt with Ham, appear at this time. O Father who dealt with Abraham, O Father who dealt with Moses, O Father who dealt with Jesus, appear at this time. Even if I forget everything in the world, I must not forget this matter.

What have I done? What have I done? Have you ever felt ashamed of yourself? Have you ever realized that you are ashamed to look up at the mountains and trees? Have you ever looked at this nation, struggling in death, and wept, saying that you would become a sacrifice in their place? If you have not done so, heaven's heart will depart from you.

Therefore, we must learn. We must understand. And we must possess. We must make everything our own. Our bodies, minds, and hearts must become heavenly, and at the same time, they must become historical, timely, and future-oriented. To become such, we must be able to say that God is my Father. Have you ever done that? No matter what happens in the world, you must be able to say that God is my Father.

Jesus left behind the desire to call God Father. We must enter a position where we can call the Father beyond that heart. We must look forward with the Father, look back with the Father, and observe our surroundings with the Father. We cannot have a consciousness of self. I have long been captivated as the Father's. I have long been connected to the Father. It is not just ten years, not just a hundred years, not just a thousand years, not just six thousand years. From before the foundation of the world, from the time the great plan of creation, that is, the creation ideology, was established, I have been bound before the Father. Have you ever felt such a thing?

I want to be a friend of the Father and a dutiful child. I want to be a son of God without consulting angels. Adam should not have fallen but should have consulted with the Father. However, because of the fall, sorrow arose, so you must have the heart that says, "I want to grieve with the Father. I want to grieve with the Father who has not grieved for six thousand years." Have you ever had such a heart? Many ancestors have come and gone, but there has been no ancestor who had such a heart.

Therefore, the Bible contains hidden heavenly twists and painful truths. What happened to Adam? What happened to Cain and Abel? What about Noah's family, Abraham's family, and Moses' family? What about the life of Jesus centered around Joseph's family? To understand this, your blood and flesh must become one with the Father's blood and flesh, so that when the Father moves, I move, when the Father is righteous, I am righteous, when the Father rejoices, I rejoice, and when the Father grieves, I can grieve.

Heaven's secrets that must be taught in code
There may be such people among our family. There may be times when unexpected weeping comes out and unexpected tears flow endlessly. Such people have become connected to such a Father. You must look at the Bible with such feelings. When looking at Genesis, you must become Adam and Eve. You must become that Adam and Eve who stood before God and received blessings. Only then will you understand the Bible correctly.

All theories and ideologies will pass away. The world of heart cannot be explained logically. God does not move under logical laws, which is why we call God the Absolute. Each verse of the Bible is intertwined with the heart of the Absolute. He is the Father of hearts who transcends logicality by millions of times. He is someone you can understand without explanation. To enter this realm and establish a relationship with God as Father and feel that heart, you must be able to unravel Genesis chapters 1 and 2. Before that, you will not understand.

God has led history and is waging a fierce battle in unseen places even at this moment, protecting His beloved sons and daughters. Not only that, but He has been working hard to ensure that today’s me becomes tomorrow’s heir without turning away from the direction of blessing while caring for the lineage of goodness. Therefore, He is a historical God, a timely God, and a future-oriented God. Thus, you must enter a position where you can truly call God your Father.

Look. If you stand before heaven without having established anything in your life, and if you are asked, "What have you done?" what will you answer? We are those who cannot give any answer. It was heaven that has held onto us, who are so ignorant, and has come to us with words we did not know until today. Even though heaven should come to us with content that we can understand, it has come with content that we do not know.

That is why the Bible is filled with parables and symbols. Heaven, which must personally free beloved sons and daughters bound by the chains of death, has circumstances that prevent it from freeing them directly, so it has come to teach us the secrets of liberation in code. The Bible does not provide the criteria that distinguish life from death. Since heaven cannot teach it directly, we must understand that it has taught us in code.

Everyone! You think that just having the Bible is enough, right? To some extent, it is. However, heaven is determined to establish the victorious prince before Satan. It desires to create a prince who can subdue Satan through heart and teaching. Because it fell in a position where it could not teach, being caught by Satan, it cannot teach the method of breaking away from that Satan. Therefore, the process of teaching in code is the path of faith.

You did not know. In coming to ignorant humans, God could not come with content that could be understood and instead came with content that could not be known in prophecy. Now you must look at heaven with a correct heart to understand the hidden will behind it. You must understand that the path of faith is to go where heaven says to go, even if you want to go this way.

This world is a battlefield. Normally, you can teach a marathon runner the secrets of running. However, when it comes to the final match, you cannot teach them. Heaven has done the same in seeking the victorious prince. It cannot teach everything. You must understand the heart of heaven that urged you to go while pretending not to know about ignorant humans.

Children must feel the Father's heart
Do you know how many times heaven has come to you while you are sleeping? To establish just one person like me, heaven has tried hundreds or thousands of times, either in pretense or through voice or parables. However, humans did not know. They did not know for six thousand years. Now we must know such a Father. We must understand that heaven has worked so hard to find just me.

You have raised children, right? What do you think the heart of a parent is like when they see their beloved child being brutally violated in the arms of an enemy? It must be heartbreaking. If your heart towards your child is like that, where does that heart come from? Can it come from nowhere? It is the same with God. If fallen parents feel that way, how much more so would God feel?

Therefore, everyone, we must know our Father. What kind of Father is He? We must understand that He is the Father who has walked the most miserable path in the history of the journey. We must recognize that He has endured greater tragedies than any tragedy in the history of the journey.

When looking at a child struggling within the fences of sorrow, pain, despair, and death, it is not heaven saying, "You are doing well." Rather, it is a Father who was in a more sorrowful position to save a child steeped in sorrow, and a Father who was in a more painful position to save a child groaning in pain. You must understand that He is a Father who does not care about death to save a son who is perishing.

So what should we do from now on? When you see a bent old man on the road, you should think, "My Father must have come like that." When you see the hands of a laborer that are swollen, you should think, "My Father, who is seeking his son, must have looked worse than that." When you see a poor beggar, you should think, "This beggar is not just a beggar; he is my Father." You must be able to bow your head. Do you understand? Even in a worthless and pitiful life, you must know that the heart of God dwells there, and you must be able to shed tears and act beyond your circumstances and dignity, recognizing that he is your Father.

Among the scriptures we read today, there is a passage that says, "Lord, when did we see you hungry and feed you, or thirsty and give you drink? When did we see you a stranger and take you in, or naked and clothe you? Or when did we see you sick or in prison and come to you?" And the King will answer and say to them, "Assuredly, I say to you, inasmuch as you did it to one of the least of these my brethren, you did it to me." (Matt 25:37-40) The meaning of this passage is that you must reach the realm I mentioned earlier.

If your heart is in tune with the Father, there are no enemies. There is no distinction between rich and poor. You must become someone who can forget your dignity and pride before the Father who came through a humble path and bow your head and weep. Such people are the ones who can understand God on this earth.
Even if you go to a place, you are a son or daughter of God.  
It turns out that this was the life of Jesus. This is not an abstract statement. It is a factual statement. It is not only the poor people living in this society but also those who are branded as traitors before the nation or ethnicity, locked in cages or disappearing like dew from the gallows, that heaven treats from such a perspective. Furthermore, we must understand that we have an unbreakable heavenly bond, and thus, we must recognize that the suffering we endure is not our own pain. Heaven walks this path. There was a time when I was in prison with a death row inmate. At that time, I held him and cried endlessly. It was because I thought my Father was weeping at this time for such sons and daughters. Those who cannot suppress such feelings and instead explode with them are the sons and daughters walking the path of nature.  
This path is the path of death. To walk this path, one must fight against those who betray heaven, even at the cost of their lives. Even if there are only one or two people in the church who possess such a heart, I would stand with them, and this is the Unification Church. I am also caught up in leading the Unification Church. However, heaven is weeping with them even at this time. Those who betray such people are betraying the Father, and those who betray the Father cannot be forgiven. This is the living Satan. The day they receive heaven's final judgment, the day of their curse, is not far off.  
God's desire for humanity  
We have understood. Therefore, we must seek and hold on. When I lift my eyes to see the mountains, when I see the villages, when I see the cities, we must find the figure of the Father who has walked the historical path. We must welcome the Father who has come through the path of sorrow, the path of Golgotha, regardless of the struggles.  
Even if I die, I am the son of the Father, and no matter what pain I endure, He is my Father. Who can sever this bond that is tied to heaven? We must become a group that walks this path. Heaven is looking for such a group. When this heart explodes in the chests of the young men and women who must carry this thirty million nation, this nation will live. If that happens, no nation will be able to dominate this nation. Neither the policies of the state nor any individual or ideology with ambition can do anything.  
Every time I walk through the back alleys, do you imagine the figure of the Father, who, worried about our future, has lost His own dignity, looking around anxiously? It has been six thousand years since He has come out like this. Even a human life of less than a hundred years is a great suffering, yet the Father has walked the path of suffering for six thousand years.  
When I think of this, what have I done? I must reflect. We must once again make a new resolution. I thought the Father was only my Father, but He is not. He is the Father of all mankind. He is the Father who fought to make even enemies His sons. Such is the Father, such is the Father. To face such a Father and just say, "Father!" is truly shameless. I cannot lift my face. I feel this a lot. You greet me because you see me as a teacher, but I hesitate to accept it. It is because I fear I might violate the truth. Those who violate the truth will receive heavenly punishment. Such people are those who trample on God, who is moving even at this time, and trample on the historical God. They are those who violate the hope of the future. We must have an increasingly humble heart as we go on.  
Everyone, if you have lived, how many years have you lived? If you have believed, how many years have you believed? Heaven has held onto traitors for six thousand years and has tried to believe in those who cannot believe. Heaven has tried to believe in those who cannot believe more than those who can believe. How much have you believed? Just a few years of belief cannot compare to the Father.  
Then how will we make up for this? We must make up for it with our hearts. From the day we came into the world with life until now, if there is anyone we have longed for, it can only be the Father. If there is anyone we love, it can only be the Father. We must be able to say this. If we have the same heart as the Father, then children are not a problem, nor are spouses or parents a problem.  
In the past, I could not stand in the position of a son with such a heart, but now I must have such a heart and come before the Father, who has held onto the historical heart, and say, "Father," and He will respond, "Yes, my son." We must have a relationship that can be held with heartfelt attention. Those of you are the historical sons and daughters of the Father, the sons and daughters of the Father of the times.  
Heaven desires to relate to you. Now that you know the Father's heart and understand the effort He has made for you, if you say, "I will live or die with the Father," then the Father will forget all your wrongs up to now. Even if you have not achieved anything until now, He will embrace you.  
The Father who comes with the most precious offerings  
You, who have no merit like you, should be placed in a position to be cursed like Cain, placed in a position like Ham, placed in a position like the fallen Moses, and placed in a position to be judged like the nation of Israel. However, heaven will call you and place you in a position like the original Adam, who has not fallen, or even a higher position. It means He will place you in a position higher than Cain and Abel, who offered sacrifices, and higher than Noah, who labored for 120 years to fulfill his purpose. It means He will place you in a position higher than Moses, who led six hundred thousand people and established God's will, and higher than the people who joyfully served God in Canaan. It means He will place you in a position higher than the hopes of the apostles after Jesus came and went. Furthermore, the Bible says that we will reign with Christ, and He will grant us the name of that king. We must understand that heaven comes to us with such precious offerings and gifts.  
Then how does He come? He comes to the field of humanity's heart. Heaven has been coming this way since six thousand years ago. He has come from the Adam family, through Noah, and then through Abraham and the nation of Israel. After Jesus came and went, He is crossing nations, mountains, and seas to come to us.  
What offering does He bring? He comes to grant us the glory of being the bride of the Messiah of humanity, the only begotten Son of heaven, the Prince of heaven. He comes to grant us the glorious crown that allows us to be in the same position as Jesus.  
He comes through the whole world. We did not know, but He must have passed through Korea several times. He comes from the individual to the family, society, nation, and world. For six thousand years, He has come according to personal, social, national, and global standards. This is the sad path of God, from which we cannot turn back.  
In such a journey, where is the one who is to receive the blessings of God, who must find and give gifts to His sons and daughters? Is there anyone who can welcome the One who comes with gifts? What is the purpose of your gathering here today? You have gathered hoping for God's gifts. Then what must you do? You must seek this. He has come to Korea, so you must look for Him. You must seek Him in the good and the bad, in the rich and the poor, in the beggars and even among the dead. They say this time is the end. The time has come to welcome the Father who is coming. He does not come in a haphazard way. Jesus said, "Ask, and it will be given to you; seek, and you will find; knock, and it will be opened to you" (Matthew 7:7). Therefore, we must continue to seek even after we think we have found.  
To receive the Father's blessings  
The Lord said that when He comes, the world will be divided into sheep and goats (Matthew 25:21-33). In this way, the world is already divided into two camps. From individuals to families, societies, nations, and the world, it is divided. We cannot deny it, can we? We must seek friends of the heart. We must seek friends of the heart. If there is someone who can make all 2.7 billion people in the world into friends, that person can live with all 2.7 billion. When someone, as a friend, proposes something to all 2.7 billion people, and if they all move, that person can represent all 2.7 billion. Wouldn't that be so? God is looking for such a person. You cannot say, "You fit my heart, but you do not fit my heart, so I do not like you." You cannot do that. If you want to find the Father, you must not do that.  
Everyone! This church is also a microcosm of 2.7 billion humanity. Therefore, the Father that this person is seeking with their heart, I must seek, and the Father that the other person is longing for with their heart, I must seek as well. I must be able to find that person's heart. Do you understand what I mean? Before finding the Father, you must be someone who can find and possess the heart of the other. What ideology will dominate the world in the future? It is the ideology that can capture the hearts of others. The era of such an ideology is the era of the heavenly kingdom on earth. The Lord comes to do such work. The place where I can give all my heart and be grateful is the kingdom.  
The Father's representative  
Since the world has been divided into two parts, like Cain and Abel, one side must be discarded. This phenomenon also occurs in my heart, so I must be in a position that claims that the conscience that aims for good is mine. Even when looking at the family, the one who is more righteous must be my brother; when looking at society or the nation, such a person must be our family, our tribe, our own, our compatriots. If you cannot be someone who can find this beyond national borders, you cannot welcome the Father who comes through the world, nor can you possess the gifts He brings.  
Everyone! What kind of being is God? He is the subject of discussion for all mankind, the protector of all mankind, and the one who holds and protects the secrets of all mankind. Therefore, you must meet the One you want to discuss with in your heart. You must meet the One you truly want to pour out all your painful heart to and discuss with. You must have such a friendship. You must find a friend who can forget their own life’s hardships and protect you, a comrade who can hold all the secrets of your heart. Do you have such a person?  
In the same way, God is looking for such sons and daughters regarding the earth. If you want to welcome the Father who comes, it cannot be one-sided. God has walked for six thousand years to leave such figures in the world. It means that they are needed in the world that heaven aims for. Because He is the Father who comes knocking on the hearts of people, He is working to connect this person's heart and that person's heart. Thus, the One who comes with the ideology that can move this world as one is the Lord of the Second Advent. Now you must seek. You must find the Father who is coming and the Father who is within your heart. Jesus also said that He is in you.  
If you can truly welcome Him with your heart, and if you can establish a father-son relationship with Him, saying that even if I die, I cannot sever this bond, then you can enter the position of receiving many heavenly gifts. Therefore, blessed are the peacemakers, for they shall be called the sons of God. Those who can establish good relationships with everyone and anyone can become sons and daughters of God.  
Where is the decision to go to heaven made? It is not made through my prayers or anything like that. It is decided among yourselves. Heaven is decided among us, and hell is also decided among us. Judgment is not decided elsewhere; it occurs among you.  
So what will you do? You must become the mother of those who weep, the father of those who suffer, and the parent of those who are sad. Since heaven has come out with this heart, if you have any feeling of life or have experienced the heart of the Father, you must become a group that weeps for this nation and a group that sympathizes. You must become someone who can welcome such a person as a friend and comfort them on behalf of the Father. Such a person will be one who receives the historical blessings of the Father, whom heaven can bless, and to whom heaven can grant the blessings it has allowed.  
<Prayer> Please allow us to realize that our merits and demerits are not even a piece of paper in the sight of the Father. Let us understand that even the parents of the world, who have hearts, have more pity for their unworthy children, and how much more so does the heavenly Father, who has a heavenly heart.  
Generally speaking, let us understand that those who sympathize with the poor are close to heaven, and those who pray for the oppressed are close to heaven. We know that a new history is being made through the gathered masses.  
Those who have received the heart's offering and have struggled to multiply it have received many blessings from God. The one who received five talents did so, and the one who received two talents did so, but the one who received one talent could not do so and was cursed, as we have seen through the Bible.  
Father, it is not only I who have gold; it is everywhere. Please allow us to understand that the Father's heart, which is buried in anyone, is a precious thing that cannot be exchanged for thousands and millions of dollars, and let us become the protagonists who occupy the Father's heart.  
Connected to the Father's lifeline,  
We have learned that only by receiving the blessings of heaven can we overcome the power of death and call out "Hosanna" within the glory of victory. Please forgive our shortcomings of the past. Although we were unable to act, if there is someone who can unite with heaven in heart, they can possess the original garden, inherit heavenly authority, and receive heavenly gifts.  
Now, in preparing, I must not stop at my own prayers but must overcome the tangled hearts between brothers and brothers in the environment I am in. Please allow me to establish a bond with heaven's heart that cannot be severed. Now, we have learned that heaven is with those who want to share life and death with heaven.  
If the Father has walked such a historical path and has established a heart connection, we earnestly hope and wish that we can establish a horizontal heart connection and praise the Father.  
May the words spoken today help in the resurrection of their lives, help them discern between good and evil in the world of darkness, and help them develop the courage and character to boldly move toward heaven. We earnestly ask this in the name of the Lord. Amen.
